# VML PHARMACEUTICAL SECTION — FOLIO F87R

## PHARMACEUTICAL PREFACE: Payload Definition
### Sub-Section: Jar/Container Recipe | Page 1 of 57 in Pharmaceutical Section

---

## POSITION

F87r opens the manuscript's largest and final section. Everything prior — 66 herbal folios identifying plants, 7 astrological folios establishing timing, 10 balneological folios purifying raw materials, 2 cosmological folios coordinating the system — feeds into what begins here. This page defines WHAT A PHARMACEUTICAL RECIPE IS before any specific recipe executes.

**Visual:** Small jar/container illustrations with associated text. Labels identify ingredients; paragraph text provides the processing protocol.

**Source summary:** "A compact pharma preface: define the payload, then purify it through clamp-governed cycling until it holds."

---

## PAGE STRUCTURE

15 paragraphs in manuscript reading order:

**Block A (P.1 → P.14):** Lines 1–6, ending with terminal seal `daiin=`
**Block B (P.2 → P.9a):** Lines 7–15, ending with terminal seal `qoty=`

Two sealed blocks = two phases of the pharmaceutical template.

---

## BLOCK A: LINES 1–6 (P.1 through P.14)

---

### LINE 1 — P.1

**EVA:** `poal.shsal.shocphor.ypcho.cpheo.saiin.oteodal.saiin-`

**VML:** poal = PROJECT/FLUID → oal; shsal = VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → salt-structure; shocphor = TRANSITION-HEAT → cphor; ypcho = RECEPTIVE/MOIST → pcho; cpheo = cpheo; saiin = SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle; oteodal = TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → eodal; saiin = SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle

**Process Flow:** PROJECT/FLUID → oal → VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → salt-structure → TRANSITION-HEAT → cphor → RECEPTIVE/MOIST → pcho → [cpheo] → SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle → TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → eodal → SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle

**ATOMIC DECOMPOSITION:**

Now — the VML source glosses `cpheo` as untranslatable. But the Rosetta Stone at §2.3 explicitly defines CPH = C+P+H = **pressure vessel** (sealed aludel, pressure-rated flask — "containing pressurized volatile spirit"). And PCH = P+C+H = **press-channel** (wine/oil press connected to channel). These are SPECIFIC APPARATUS TERMS. Let me re-read every token with this knowledge:

**`poal`** = P(press/seal) + O(heat) + AL(structure/matrix)
- The p- prefix = press, seal, project fluid mechanically
- Root: oal = heat-structure
- READING: Press/project the heated structural material. The mechanical press initiates the pharmaceutical process. This is physically consistent — a screw-press or lever-press forces material into the processing apparatus. The FIRST WORD of the pharmaceutical section is a MECHANICAL ACTION: press.

**`shsal`** = SH(vigorous flow) + SAL(salt/substrate)
- sh- = vigorous steam/distillation force (the Rosetta Stone maps this to Mars ♂, vigor)
- SAL = the salt substrate, crystallization medium, fixative
- READING: Vigorous flow through salt substrate. The pressed material is driven vigorously through a salt bed or salt-based medium. Physically: forcing a liquid extract through a salt filter or salt-impregnated matrix. This IS a real pharmaceutical technique — salt-based filtration purifies extracts.

**`shocphor`** = SHO(vigorous-heat) + CPH(pressure vessel) + OR(outlet/source)
- SHO = S+H+O = vigorous steam + heat = forced heating (Rosetta: "bellows-driven fire application")
- CPH = C+P+H = pressure vessel (sealed aludel)
- OR = O+R = source/outlet (alembic neck, vessel opening)
- READING: Apply vigorous heat to the pressure vessel at its outlet. Physically: heating the sealed aludel with bellows-forced fire, driving material toward the outlet neck. This is DISTILLATION UNDER PRESSURE — a more aggressive form than standard atmospheric distillation.

**`ypcho`** = Y(receptive/moist) + PCH(press-channel) + O(heat)
- Y = the receptive/moist principle (imbibition)
- PCH = P+C+H = press-channel (mechanical press connected to channel)
- O = heat
- READING: The moist medium receives through the heated press-channel. The condensed distillate (moist) collects via a heated press-channel. Physically: the receiver flask is connected by a heated channel to the press, and the distillate drips into it while still warm.

**`cpheo`** = CPH(pressure vessel) + E(essence) + O(heat)
- CPH = pressure vessel
- E = essence (Air, Hot+Moist — the volatile quintessence)
- O = heat (Fire, Hot+Dry)
- READING: The pressure vessel contains heated essence. This is NOT untranslatable — it is a precise description of the state of the apparatus. The sealed aludel holds pressurized, heated volatile essence. Physically: the pressure vessel is charged with hot essential oil/volatile spirit.

**`saiin`** = SAL(salt) + AIIN(double-cycle-complete)
- The universal salt-cycle verification marker
- READING: Salt cycle verified. The material has passed through one complete cycle of salt-based processing.

**`oteodal`** = OT(temporal-drive) + E(essence) + O(heat) + DAL(fix-structure)
- OT = O+T = temporal-drive (the §3.1 selective prefix — time DRIVES fire operations)
- E = essence
- O = heat
- DAL = D+A+L = fix-structure (coagulatio applied to structural matrix)
- READING: Time-driven essence, heated and structurally fixed. This is the TIMED CALCINATION PRODUCT: the temporal schedule controls how long the essence is heated, and the result is fixed into structural matrix. Physically: the essence is heated for a precisely scheduled duration, then coagulated into solid form.

The Rosetta Stone at §4.3 specifically calls out `oteody` (14×) as "the standard pharmaceutical intermediate." `oteodal` is the same operation but with -al (structural matrix) rather than -y (active). The structure is FIXED rather than volatile.

**`saiin`** = Salt cycle verified AGAIN.

**LINE 1 PHYSICAL READING:**

Press material into apparatus → drive it vigorously through salt substrate → apply bellows-forced heat to the pressure vessel at its outlet → moist condensate collects through heated press-channel → pressure vessel holds heated essence → SALT CYCLE VERIFIED → time-controlled heating fixes the essence into structural matrix → SALT CYCLE VERIFIED AGAIN.

This is a COMPLETE PHARMACEUTICAL SETUP in one paragraph: mechanical pressing, salt filtration, pressure distillation, collection, timed calcination, double verification. The opening line of the pharmaceutical section describes the ENTIRE APPARATUS AND ITS BASIC OPERATION in 8 tokens.

The double `saiin` is not redundant. The first salt verification occurs AFTER the pressure vessel is charged (`cpheo`). The second occurs AFTER the timed calcination (`oteodal`). Two different stages, two different checkpoints. The salt principle verifies both the CHARGING of the vessel and the FIXATION of the product.

---

### LINE 2 — P.10

**EVA:** `psheodshy.dal.shee.saldal.shol.aldy-`

**VML:** psheodshy = PROJECT/FLUID → sheodshy; dal = FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix; shee = TRANSITION-ESSENCE → e; saldal = SALT/FLOWING → structure/matrix; shol = TRANSITION-HEAT → l; aldy = structure/matrix → [fixed/stabilized]

**Process Flow:** PROJECT/FLUID → sheodshy → FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix → TRANSITION-ESSENCE → e → SALT/FLOWING → structure/matrix → TRANSITION-HEAT → l → structure/matrix → [fixed/stabilized]

**ATOMIC DECOMPOSITION:**

**`psheodshy`** = P(press) + SHE(steam-essence) + OD(heat-fix) + SH(vigorous-flow) + Y(active)
- This is a MASSIVE compound. Five operational layers stacked:
  1. P = press mechanically
  2. SHE = steam the essence (vaporize)
  3. OD = heat and fix (calcine)
  4. SH = vigorously flow
  5. Y = keep active
- READING: Press-steam-calcine-flow in active state. All five operations happen in sequence within a single token. This is a compressed PIPELINE: the material is pressed, steamed, calcined, flowed, and remains active — all described in one word. This is why VML is a "process language" — each word is a micro-algorithm.

**`dal`** = D(fix) + AL(structure/matrix)
- Simple, direct: fix into structural matrix. Coagulatio into earth-body.
- Physically: the material solidifies into a structured form.

**`shee`** = SHE(steam-essence) + E(bare essence)
- SH = vigorous flow. E+E = the double-e here is NOT double-intensity but rather the compound SHE + bare E.
- Actually, re-reading the Rosetta Stone: SHE = S+H+E = "steam-essence, vaporized essence in motion." Then the suffix is just bare -e.
- READING: The vaporized essence, stripped bare. The transition removes everything that isn't pure essence. What remains after steaming is JUST the essential principle — no substrate, no salt, no structure.

**`saldal`** = SAL(salt/substrate) + DAL(fix-structure)
- This is a ROOT + ROOT compound, not prefix + root.
- SAL = salt principle. DAL = fix-structure principle.
- READING: Salt structurally fixes. The salt and the fixation principle COMBINE to create a doubly-reinforced structural matrix. Physically: the salt provides the crystalline lattice AND the fixation process locks it into place. This is SALT-DRIVEN CRYSTALLIZATION.

**`shol`** = SHO(vigorous-heat) + L(fluid/layer)
- SHO = vigorous heating (bellows-forced)
- L = fluid state
- READING: Vigorous heat produces fluid. The solidified, salt-fixed material is re-liquefied by aggressive heating. The fixed salt-structure MELTS. Physically: the crystalline salt matrix is heated past its melting point or dissolved back into solution by vigorous heat.

**`aldy`** = AL(structure/matrix) + DY(fixed/stabilized)
- READING: The structure is fixed and stable. Terminal state. After the melt-and-recrystallize cycle, the final structure is LOCKED.

**LINE 2 PHYSICAL READING:**

Press-steam-calcine-flow (all in one compound operation) → fix into structural matrix → strip to bare essence by steaming → salt crystallization reinforced by fixation → vigorously heat to re-liquify → structure finally fixed and stable.

This paragraph describes a RECRYSTALLIZATION PROCESS. The material is:
1. Processed through a multi-stage pipeline (`psheodshy`)
2. Fixed into structure (`dal`)
3. Stripped to essence by steam (`shee`)
4. Crystallized by combined salt-fixation (`saldal`)
5. Re-melted by vigorous heat (`shol`)
6. Re-fixed into final stable structure (`aldy`)

Recrystallization — dissolving and re-precipitating a substance to improve purity — is one of the most fundamental pharmaceutical purification techniques, used from the 15th century to today. The text DESCRIBES THIS PROCESS with precision.

---

### LINE 3 — P.11

**EVA:** `ysheees.chetchy.teodar.otsheol.tockhy-`

**VML:** ysheees = MOIST-TRANSITION → triple-intensity; chetchy = VOLATILE-ESSENCE → tchy; teodar = ENERGY/TEMPORAL → eodar; otsheol = TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → infuse-fluid; tockhy = ENERGY/TEMPORAL → ockhy

**Process Flow:** MOIST-TRANSITION → triple-intensity → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → tchy → ENERGY/TEMPORAL → eodar → TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → infuse-fluid → ENERGY/TEMPORAL → ockhy

**ATOMIC DECOMPOSITION:**

**`ysheees`** = Y(moist/receptive) + SHE(steam-essence) + EEE(triple-intensity) + S(salt/flow)
- Y = the receptive/moist principle (imbibition — wetting, adding vehicle)
- SHE = steam-essence (vaporized quintessence in motion)
- EEE = TRIPLE-E = maximum essence intensity (Rosetta Stone: "Peak" energy, ~1.6% of corpus, concentrated in Leo/Scorpio)
- S = salt/flow principle
- READING: Moisten the steamed essence at MAXIMUM INTENSITY with salt/flow. This is the FIRST TRIPLE-E TOKEN in the pharmaceutical section. It appears on LINE 3 of PAGE 1. The Rosetta Stone tells us triple-e clusters in Leo (Sun domicile) and Scorpio (Mars rules) — domains of MAXIMUM FIRE. The pharmaceutical section (FIRE element) immediately reaches maximum intensity.
- PHYSICALLY: The pure vaporized essence is moistened (adding a liquid vehicle — perhaps water, vinegar, or alcohol) at maximum concentration. The salt principle is present to stabilize. This is IMBIBITION AT PEAK STRENGTH — wetting the calcined residue with the most concentrated possible essence to revivify it.

**`chetchy`** = CHE(Mercury/Spirit) + TCH(drive-channel) + Y(active)
- CHE = ☿ Mercurius — the volatile, mutable spirit (essential oils, alcohol, volatile vapors)
- TCH = T+C+H = drive-channel (heated conduit, fire-driven flow path)
- Y = active state
- READING: Mercury/spirit driven through heated channel, active. The volatile spirit — revivified by the triple-e imbibition — is driven through a heated conduit. Physically: the essential oil or volatile spirit passes through a heated tube (a DISTILLATION THROAT or delivery tube). The apparatus is actively channeling the energized spirit.

**`teodar`** = TE(agent/tincture) + O(heat) + DAR(fix-root)
- TE = T+E = the driven essence, active principle, tincture (the therapeutic agent itself)
- O = heat (calcinatio)
- DAR = D+A+R = fix-root (coagulatio applied to the root/foundation)
- READING: The tincture (active therapeutic agent) is heated and fixed at its root. The essential therapeutic principle is being GROUNDED — locked into its deepest foundation. Physically: the active medicinal compound is calcined and anchored so it won't evaporate or degrade. This is FIXATION OF THE ACTIVE PRINCIPLE.

**`otsheol`** = OT(temporal-drive) + SHE(steam-essence) + OL(fluid)
- OT = temporal-drive (the selective prefix — time drives)
- SHE = steam-essence
- OL = fluid medium
- READING: Time-driven steaming into fluid medium. The source translates this uniquely as "infuse-fluid." The temporal schedule controls how long the steamed essence is held in fluid form. INFUSION = controlled-time soaking of the steamed essence in a liquid medium. This is REAL PHARMACEUTICAL INFUSION — steeping medicinal material in a solvent for a precisely timed duration. Tincture-making, tea-brewing, decoction. The most fundamental pharmaceutical operation.

**`tockhy`** = T(drive) + O(heat) + CKH(static valve/clamp) + Y(active)
- T = fire/drive
- O = heat
- CKH = C+K+H = static valve/clamp (lute seal, stopcock, clamped joint)
- Y = active (the valve is OPEN/operating)
- READING: Heat-driven valve is active. The clamp or stopcock on the apparatus is OPEN and actively controlled by heat. Physically: a heat-sensitive valve that opens or regulates based on temperature — or a valve that is manually operated during the heating phase. The fire schedule controls when the valve opens.

**LINE 3 PHYSICAL READING:**

Moisten calcined residue at MAXIMUM CONCENTRATION (triple-e imbibition) → the revivified Mercury/spirit flows through the heated distillation channel → the active therapeutic tincture is calcined and fixed at its root → time-controlled steaming infuses the spirit into fluid medium → heat-driven valve is active.

This is the KEY OPERATION of the preface. After the apparatus was set up (Line 1) and the material was recrystallized for purity (Line 2), Line 3 PERFORMS THE CRITICAL PHARMACEUTICAL STEP: imbibition at maximum strength, distillation of the spirit, fixation of the active principle, and timed infusion. This is WHERE THE MEDICINE IS MADE.

The triple-e token `ysheees` on the opening page tells us: pharmaceutical operations START at maximum sensitivity. There is no warm-up period. The medicine is made at peak concentration from the beginning.

---

### LINE 4 — P.12

**EVA:** `keor.ckheey.shody.qoeeety.schody.daiin-`

**VML:** keor = BODY/CONTAIN → eor; ckheey = VALVE/BIND-VOLATILE → essence-active; shody = TRANSITION-HEAT → dy → [fixed/stabilized]; qoeeety = TRANSMUTE-ENERGY → essence-energy; schody = SALT/FLOWING → chody; daiin = FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle

**Process Flow:** BODY/CONTAIN → eor → VALVE/BIND-VOLATILE → essence-active → TRANSITION-HEAT → dy → [fixed/stabilized] → TRANSMUTE-ENERGY → essence-energy → SALT/FLOWING → chody → FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle

**ATOMIC DECOMPOSITION:**

**`keor`** = KE(essence/quintessence) + OR(outlet/source)
- KE = K+E = contained volatile, Fifth Essence, purified extract
- OR = O+R = at the alembic neck, vessel opening
- READING: The quintessence at the outlet. The purified extract is emerging from the vessel opening. The distillation product is appearing at the alembic beak. Physically: drops of purified tincture are forming at the outlet of the distillation apparatus.

**`ckheey`** = CKH(static valve/clamp) + EE(double-essence) + Y(active)
- CKH = the lute seal, stopcock, clamped joint
- EE = double-intensity essence (elevated)
- Y = active/operating
- READING: The valve clamps double-intensity essence in active operation. The stopcock is regulating the flow of concentrated essence. At double-e (elevated, not maximum), this is precision flow control of a concentrated product.

**`shody`** = SHO(vigorous-heat) + DY(fixed/stabilized)
- SHO = vigorous heating
- DY = D+Y = fixed, stabilized (coagulatum)
- READING: Vigorous heat produces a fixed product. The material is calcined to stability. After controlled collection (keor, ckheey), the vigorous heat phase fixes what was collected.

**`qoeeety`** = QO(circulate/extract) + EEE(triple-intensity) + T(drive) + Y(active)
- QO = Q+O = circulatio/cohobation — the retort cycle (Rosetta: "Refluxing, rotating, recycling")
- EEE = TRIPLE-E = maximum intensity
- T = drive/propel
- Y = active
- READING: Circulate/extract at TRIPLE-E MAXIMUM INTENSITY, driven, active. This is COHOBATION AT PEAK POWER — the redistillation cycle operating at the absolute maximum concentration. Physically: the distillate is returned to the vessel and redistilled, and this cycle is performed at maximum essence concentration. This is the most aggressive extraction possible.

**SECOND TRIPLE-E on the page**, and it's in the first qo- (transmutation/circulation) token. The pharmaceutical section's first transmutation fires at MAXIMUM POWER. There is no gradient, no warmup. The retort cycle launches at triple-e.

**`schody`** = S(flow/dissolve) + CHO(Sulphur/soul) + DY(fixed)
- S = solutio (dissolution)
- CHO = C+H+O = Sulphur principle — the combustible soul, oils, resins, color-bearing compounds
- DY = fixed/stabilized
- READING: Dissolve the Sulphur principle, then fix it. The soul of the material (its characteristic properties — taste, smell, color) is dissolved and re-fixed. Physically: the oily/resinous components are brought into solution and then re-precipitated. This captures the THERAPEUTIC CHARACTER of the medicine.

Note: CHE (Mercury) was the subject of Line 3. CHO (Sulphur) is the subject of Line 4. The TRIA PRIMA is being processed in order: Mercury first, Sulphur second. SAL (Salt) has been the verification agent throughout.

**`daiin`** = D(fix) + AIIN(double-cycle-complete)
- READING: Fixation verified at full double-cycle. The standard quality gate closes.

**LINE 4 PHYSICAL READING:**

Quintessence emerges at the outlet → valve clamps the double-intensity flow → vigorous heat fixes the product → RETORT CYCLE AT MAXIMUM INTENSITY (triple-e cohobation) → the Sulphur/soul principle is dissolved and re-fixed → FIXATION VERIFIED.

Line 4 completes the Tria Prima processing: Line 3 handled Mercury (volatile spirit), Line 4 handles Sulphur (characteristic soul). Salt has been verifying throughout. The three Paracelsian principles — Mercury, Sulphur, Salt — are each addressed in the opening lines of the pharmaceutical section.

The two triple-e tokens (`ysheees` in Line 3, `qoeeety` in Line 4) mark the TWO PEAK OPERATIONS: imbibition (Line 3) and cohobation (Line 4). These are the pharmaceutical section's highest-energy moments, and they appear back-to-back on the opening page.

---

### LINE 5 — P.13

**EVA:** `daiin.shol.cthey.okeol.cheor.okeeo.daiim-`

**VML:** daiin = FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle; shol = TRANSITION-HEAT → l; cthey = CONDUIT/BIND-ENERGY → essence-active; okeol = PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eol; cheor = VOLATILE-ESSENCE → source/rotation; okeeo = PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → essence-energy; daiim = FIX/STABILIZE → aiim

**Process Flow:** FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle → TRANSITION-HEAT → l → CONDUIT/BIND-ENERGY → essence-active → PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eol → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → source/rotation → PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → essence-energy → FIX/STABILIZE → aiim

**ATOMIC DECOMPOSITION:**

**`daiin`** — Opens with verification. Line 4 ended with `daiin`, Line 5 opens with `daiin`. Back-to-back verification across the line break. DOUBLE-GATE: the product must pass fixation twice before continuing.

**`shol`** = SHO(vigorous-heat) + L(fluid)
- Vigorous heat produces fluid. The fixed product is re-liquefied. Same token as Line 2, same function: aggressive heating melts the solid.

**`cthey`** = CTH(conduit/throat) + EY(essence-active)
- CTH = C+T+H = the distillation throat, alembic neck (rostrum)
- EY = E+Y = essence-active (elevated intensity, not just base active)
- READING: The distillation throat carries active essence. The liquefied product enters the alembic neck and flows through as an energized essence. The apparatus is WORKING — spirit is in motion through the conduit.

**`okeol`** = OK(phase-shift) + E(essence) + OL(fluid)
- OK = O+K = phase-shift (the selective prefix for K-roots — Rosetta §3.1: "phase CONTAINS")
- E = essence
- OL = O+L = fluid medium
- READING: Phase-shift the essence into fluid state. A controlled state change: the essence transitions from one phase (vapor? solid?) into fluid. Physically: CONDENSATION — the vapor condenses into liquid at this point in the apparatus.

**`cheor`** = CHE(Mercury/spirit) + OR(outlet/source)
- CHE = ☿ Mercurius — the volatile spirit
- OR = at the vessel outlet
- READING: Mercury/spirit at the outlet. The volatile spirit has arrived at the vessel opening. This is the PRODUCT EMERGING — the distilled spirit appears at the beak of the alembic.

**`okeeo`** = OK(phase-shift) + EE(double-intensity essence) + O(heat)
- OK = phase-shift
- EE = double-intensity (elevated)
- O = heat
- READING: Phase-shift at double-essence intensity with heat. A SECOND PHASE SHIFT within the same paragraph. The first (okeol) shifted to fluid. This second (okeeo) shifts at elevated intensity with heat — a DIFFERENT PHASE TRANSITION. Perhaps: the fluid product undergoes a second heat-driven transformation, concentrating it further.

TWO phase-shifts (ok-) in one paragraph: `okeol` → `cheor` → `okeeo`. The material shifts to fluid, emerges at the outlet, then shifts AGAIN at higher intensity. This is FRACTIONAL DISTILLATION — collecting different fractions at different phase-shift points.

**`daiim`** = D(fix) + AIIM (variant: A+I+I+M instead of A+I+I+N)
- Standard AIIN has N (seal/close) as terminal consonant
- This AIIM has M (unite/marry) as terminal consonant
- READING: Fixation completes with UNION rather than closure. The product isn't just sealed — it's MARRIED. The Coniunctio (chemical wedding) happens at the fixation checkpoint. The two fractions from the double phase-shift are UNITED.

**LINE 5 PHYSICAL READING:**

Verify again → vigorously heat to re-liquify → essence flows through distillation throat → FIRST PHASE SHIFT: essence condenses to fluid → Mercury/spirit emerges at outlet → SECOND PHASE SHIFT: at higher intensity with heat → fixation verified with UNION of fractions.

This is FRACTIONAL DISTILLATION WITH RECOMBINATION. The material is liquefied, distilled, and collected in two fractions at different phase points, then the fractions are MARRIED (`daiim` with M=unite) back together. Physically: separating the distillate into early and late fractions, then recombining them. This produces a more balanced product than either fraction alone — a real technique still used in perfumery and spirits production.

---

### LINE 6 — P.14 [BLOCK A TERMINAL]

**EVA:** `shos.cheol.cheos.ckhey.saiin.qockheol.daiin=`

**VML:** shos = TRANSITION-HEAT → s; cheol = VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid; cheos = VOLATILE-ESSENCE → os; ckhey = VALVE/BIND-VOLATILE → essence-active; saiin = SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle; qockheol = TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → ckheol; daiin = FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle

**Process Flow:** TRANSITION-HEAT → s → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → os → VALVE/BIND-VOLATILE → essence-active → SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle → TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → ckheol → FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle

**ATOMIC DECOMPOSITION:**

**`shos`** = SHO(vigorous-heat) + S(salt/flow)
- Vigorous heating with salt/flow. The heat transitions toward the salt principle.

**`cheol`** = CHE(Mercury/spirit) + OL(fluid)
- Mercury is in fluid state. The volatile spirit is dissolved, liquid, flowing.

**`cheos`** = CHE(Mercury/spirit) + OS(saturated)
- Mercury is heat-SATURATED. The volatile spirit has absorbed maximum heat. Rosetta §4.1: OS = "Saturatio — heat-saturated; Physically: fully absorbed maximum heat; 'The matter drinks no more fire.'"
- The Mercury can't absorb any more heat. It's FULLY CHARGED.

**`ckhey`** = CKH(static valve/clamp) + EY(essence-active)
- The valve clamps essence in active state. Flow control applied.

**`saiin`** = Salt cycle verified.

**`qockheol`** = QO(circulate/extract) + CKH(valve/clamp) + EOL(essence-fluid)
- QO = retort/cohobation cycle
- CKH = through the valve/clamp
- EOL = essence in fluid state
- READING: Circulate/extract THROUGH THE VALVE in fluid form. The cohobation cycle operates through the valve — the retort process is VALVE-CONTROLLED. The valve regulates how much distillate returns for redistillation and how much passes through as product.

**`daiin=`** = Fixation verified. **TERMINAL SEAL (=).** Block A complete.

**LINE 6 PHYSICAL READING:**

Vigorous heat with salt → Mercury becomes fluid → Mercury becomes heat-SATURATED ("drinks no more fire") → valve clamps the active essence → salt verifies → COHOBATION THROUGH THE VALVE → fixation sealed.

The Block A terminal describes the Mercury at its FINAL PREPARED STATE: fully saturated with heat, clamped, salt-verified, and then run through one last controlled cohobation through the valve. After this, the preparation phase is COMPLETE.

The progression `cheol` → `cheos` is subtle and important: Mercury goes from merely fluid (cheol) to heat-SATURATED (cheos). The difference between "dissolved in liquid" and "fully charged with thermal energy." The Mercury is not just in solution — it has absorbed all the heat it can hold. It is at maximum energy before the processing begins.

**BLOCK A SUMMARY:**

Block A (Lines 1–6) defines THE PREPARATION PHASE of the pharmaceutical template:

| Line | Operation | Tria Prima Focus |
|------|-----------|-----------------|
| 1 | Set up apparatus: press, salt-filter, pressure-distill, timed calcination | SAL (salt as framework) |
| 2 | Recrystallize for purity: dissolve-fix-melt-refix | SAL (salt crystallization) |
| 3 | PEAK OPERATION: triple-e imbibition, spirit distillation, fixation of tincture, timed infusion | CHE (Mercury/spirit) |
| 4 | PEAK OPERATION: triple-e cohobation, Sulphur dissolution and re-fixation | CHO (Sulphur/soul) |
| 5 | Fractional distillation with recombination (daiim = union) | CHE + CHO (recombination) |
| 6 | Mercury fully heat-saturated, valve-controlled final cohobation | CHE at saturation |

The Tria Prima is processed in order: SAL provides the framework (Lines 1–2), CHE (Mercury) is processed first (Line 3), CHO (Sulphur) is processed second (Line 4), they are recombined (Line 5), and the Mercury reaches full saturation (Line 6).

# VML PHARMACEUTICAL SECTION — FOLIO F87V

## LOCK AND BOTTLE: Volatile Sealing Protocol
### The Verso Companion to the Pharmaceutical Preface

## POSITION AND RELATIONSHIP TO F87R

F87v is the VERSO of the pharmaceutical preface. Where f87r defined WHAT a recipe is (the template, the infrastructure), f87v defines HOW TO SEAL THE PRODUCT. This is "lock and bottle" — the protocol for capturing volatile spirits and locking them into stable containers.

The recto/verso pair works as a unit:
- **F87r** = "Here is how the processing system works"
- **F87v** = "Here is how you capture and seal what it produces"

The visual shows jar illustrations with SEALED vessels — containers with closures, distinct from f87r's open processing apparatus.

---

## PAGE ARCHITECTURE: THREE PHASES

The page contains 12 paragraphs. Unlike f87r's clean two-phase structure, f87v organizes into THREE phases, separated by TWO terminal seals:

**PHASE 1 — INITIAL CAPTURE (Lines 1–4, P.1 → P.12):**
Project volatile essence, capture, fix, seal into vessel.
Terminal seal: `olcthr=` (P.12) — fluid locked in conduit. UNUSUAL: not a daiin or qo- seal but a PHYSICAL seal — fluid literally locked into apparatus.

**PHASE 2 — PROCESSING (Lines 5–9, P.2 → P.6):**
Salt-conduit circulation, triple extraction, conduit-mediated transmutation.
Terminal seal: `otol=` (P.6) — temporal-heat drives to fluid completion.

**PHASE 3 — This phase is actually Phase 2's continuation. Let me re-examine...**

Actually, looking more carefully at the terminal markers:

**Terminal seal 1:** `olcthr=` at end of P.12 (Line 4)
**Terminal seal 2:** `otol=` at end of P.6 (Line 9)

But wait — there's ALSO `sal=` at end of P2.10 (Line 6), making THREE terminal seals. Let me re-trace the reading order carefully.

**READING ORDER (from EVA transcription):**
P.1 → P.10 → P.11 → P.12 → P.2 → P.3 → P.4 → P.5 → P.6 → P.7 → P.8 → P.9

Now checking terminals:
- P.12 ends with `daraiinm-saiin.olcthr=` — TERMINAL SEAL (=)
- P.6 ends with `otol=` — TERMINAL SEAL (=)
- P2.10 ends with `sal=` — TERMINAL SEAL (=)

Wait — P2.10 is from the f88r transcription, not f87v. Let me re-examine. The f87v transcription shows:

P.1 through P.12 — that's 12 paragraphs total.
P.6 ends with `otol=` (equals sign visible in Line 9 of process flow).

Actually, re-reading the EVA more carefully:
- P.1 ends with `-` (dash, continues)
- P.12 ends with `olcthr=` (TERMINAL SEAL)
- P.6 has `otol=` in its text string
- P1.5 of f88r ends with `sam=` 
- P2.10 of f88r ends with `sal=`

So f87v has TWO terminal seals, creating TWO PHASES:

**PHASE 1 (Lines 1–4, P.1 → P.12):** Capture and seal volatile into vessel.
Terminal: `olcthr=` — fluid locked in conduit.

**PHASE 2 (Lines 5–12, P.2 → P.9):** Process the sealed volatile further.
The Phase 2 terminal is within P.6 at `otol=` midstream, but P.9 ends with `daiin-` (dash, not equals), suggesting the page continues to f88r or that P.9's daiin is the working terminal.

Let me proceed with the paragraph analysis and let the structure reveal itself.

## PHASE 1: CAPTURE THE VOLATILE (Lines 1–4)

**EVA:** `pcheey.daiin.cphodar.shody.dcheody.todor.ochepchody-oldar-`

| `ochepchody-oldar` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → chepchody-oldar | **THE GREAT COMPOUND.** This is a HYPHENATED MEGA-TOKEN — two complex words joined by a hyphen. Breaking down: oche(heat-volatile-essence) + pch(project-volatile) + ody(heat-fix) HYPHEN ol(fluid) + dar(fix-root). The hyphen encodes SEQUENTIAL DEPENDENCY: the first half (heat-volatile-essence projected and heat-fixed) must complete BEFORE the second half (fluid fixed at root). This is a TWO-STAGE OPERATION compressed into one compound. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Project volatile at double-e precision → VERIFY IMMEDIATELY → [cph-process at root] → heat fixes → volatile essence heat-fixed → time controls the fixing during projection → **TWO-STAGE COMPOUND: heat-project-fix THEN fluid-fix-at-root.**

| Contains | No verification markers | Immediate daiin |
| Compound complexity | Simple tokens | Hyphenated mega-compound |
| Material focus | Fluid (general) | Volatile (specific, dangerous) |

F87v is IMMEDIATELY more cautious, more precise, and more complex than f87r. The volatile material demands double-e sensitivity from the first word, immediate verification from the second, and a hyphenated two-stage operation to lock it down. This is dangerous material.

| `cthey` | CONDUIT/BIND-ENERGY → essence-active | Conduit active — the expansion is channeled, not uncontrolled. |
| `cpheckhy` | [untranslatable] | The cph- cluster + ckhy (valve-active). Whatever cph- is, it's operating through the active valve. |
| `cheor` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → source/rotation | Volatile essence returns to source. A RESET — the material goes back to its origin point. |
| `chepcheol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → pcheol | Volatile essence through project-volatile-fluid. A complex volatile-projection compound. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** EXPAND through volatile-essence → conduit channels → [cph-valve process] → volatile returns to source → volatile projects as fluid.

**Critical observation:** After two sealed phases, the system OPENS. The op- prefix (expand/project) reverses the sealing — the product is expanded, released from compression. But it's immediately channeled through conduits and valves. This is CONTROLLED EXPANSION — not bursting open but deliberately released.

The `cheor` (volatile returns to source) echoes f87r's Line 13 (P.8) where `cheory` performed the same function. The return-to-source is a recurring motif: after processing, the volatile essence always cycles back to its origin, still active.

---

### Line 11 / P.8: LAYERED EXTRACTION WITH TRIPLE-E

**EVA:** `kchor.ol.cheeol.qok.odal.lseeey.keodam-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `kchor` | BODY-VOLATILE → source/rotation | Volatile body rotates at source. The container is being turned/rotated. |
| `ol` | FLUID-MEDIUM | The fluid medium. Simple, bare. |
| `cheeol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → eol | Volatile essence at double-e sensitivity as fluid. |
| `qok` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE | **BARE qok-.** Extract-essence, standing alone. Another bare operational prefix — like the bare `qo` in Line 9 and the bare `s` in Lines 5 and 9. Command form: *extract.* |
| `odal` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → fix-structure | Heat activates fixation of structure. |
| `lseeey` | LAYER/STRUCTURE → seeey | **TRIPLE-E IN LAYERED STRUCTURE.** l(layer) + s(salt) + eee(TRIPLE-E) + y(active). Layer-salt-triple-intensity-active. The layered structure is operating at MAXIMUM SENSITIVITY. This is the page's HIGHEST-SENSITIVITY token. |
| `keodam` | BODY/CONTAIN → eodam | Body contains essence-heat-fixation-vessel. The triple-e-sensitive layered product is placed in a containment vessel. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Volatile body rotates → fluid medium → volatile double-e essence → *EXTRACT* → heat fixes structure → **LAYER-SALT AT TRIPLE-E SENSITIVITY** → contain in vessel.

**Critical observation:** `lseeey` is the page's crown jewel. LAYER/STRUCTURE + SALT + TRIPLE-INTENSITY + ACTIVE. The layered structure of the sealed product is being examined at maximum sensitivity — looking for defects, irregularities, or contamination at the finest possible resolution.

This is QUALITY INSPECTION. After two phases of processing and sealing, the finished product's layered structure (the physical layers within the sealed vessel) undergoes triple-e examination. Only THEN is it placed in its final containment vessel (`keodam`).

The progression from `qok` (bare extract-command) through `odal` (heat-fix-structure) to `lseeey` (triple-e layer inspection) to `keodam` (final containment) tells the complete quality-control story: extract sample → fix for inspection → inspect at maximum sensitivity → approve and contain.

---

### Line 12 / P.9: FINAL PARAGRAPH — Salt-Valve-Salt-Fix

**EVA:** `ytchea.qy.chos.ckhor.cheay.scheol.sal.daiin-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `ytchea` | MOIST-ENERGY → chea | Moist energy through volatile-essence-root. |
| `qy` | [untranslatable] | Just two characters. Possibly a bare qo-variant or a scribal abbreviation. The shortest token on the page. |
| `chos` | VOLATILE-HEAT → s | Volatile heat reaches salt state. |
| `ckhor` | VALVE/BIND-VOLATILE → source/rotation | Valve binds volatile at source — the valve is at the ORIGIN point, controlling flow from source. |
| `cheay` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → ay | Volatile essence with root-active endpoint. |
| `scheol` | SALT/FLOWING → cheol | Salt flowing through volatile-essence-fluid. |
| `sal` | SALT/FLOWING → structure/matrix | Salt as structural matrix. PENULTIMATE token. |
| `daiin` | FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle | **FINAL VERIFICATION.** The page's last daiin. Dash (-) terminal: not an equals-sign seal, but a standard paragraph break. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Moist energy acts → [qy] → volatile heat to salt → valve binds at source → volatile essence at root → salt flows through volatile fluid → SALT STRUCTURES → **VERIFY (daiin).**

**Critical observation:** The final paragraph ends with `sal.daiin-` — salt-structure then verification. But with a DASH, not an equals sign. This means the lock-and-bottle protocol doesn't have a third terminal seal — it leaves the door open. After quality inspection (Line 11) and final salt-verification (Line 12), the material transitions to the next page (f88r) without a hard seal.

This makes sense: the lock-and-bottle protocol PRESERVES material that will be further processed. The sealed product isn't the end — it's the INPUT for the next stage. The dash says: "verified, ready to proceed."

---

## PAGE-LEVEL PATTERNS

### Prefix Distribution (All 12 paragraphs)

| Prefix | Function | Count | Notes |
|--------|----------|-------|-------|
| cth- (conduit) | Channel/route energy | 9 | **DOMINANT.** The sealed system IS conduit. |
| che-/cho- (volatile) | Volatile essence/heat | 15 | Carrier tokens — the volatile is everywhere |
| sal/s- (salt) | Salt/flowing/structural | 10 | Infrastructure medium |
| ckh- (valve) | Bind volatile/clamp | 5 | Sealing operations |
| dch- (fix-volatile) | Fix volatile specifically | 4 | The core locking operation |
| qo-/qok- (transmute/extract) | Transform/extract | 7 | Including 2 bare forms (qo, qok) |
| y-/yk- (moist/receptive) | Moisture/receive | 6 | Processing environment |
| k-/ke- (body/contain) | Contain/hold | 5 | Vessel/container language |
| ot-/ote- (temporal) | Time-driven | 4 | Schedule control |
| d-/daiin (fix/verify) | Stabilize/verify | 5 | Verification checkpoints |

**CONDUIT DOMINANCE:** The cth- prefix appears 9 times — the most frequent operational prefix on the page. F87v is about CONDUIT PROCESSING. The volatile material is processed WITHIN sealed conduits, not in open vessels. The pipe is the reactor.

Compare: f87r was SALT-DOMINANT (14 salt tokens). F87v is CONDUIT-DOMINANT (9 conduit tokens). The preface established the salt architecture; the lock-and-bottle page runs material THROUGH that architecture.

### Unique Features Not Found in F87r

| Feature | Token | Significance |
|---------|-------|-------------|
| Bare transmutation prefix | `qo` (P.6) | Imperative: *transmute now* |
| Bare extraction prefix | `qok` (P.8) | Imperative: *extract now* |
| Triple-e in layered structure | `lseeey` (P.8) | Quality inspection at max sensitivity |
| -aiim vessel-completion | `aiim` (P.10) | Morphological distinction: vessel vs. cycle |
| Hyphenated mega-compounds | 3 instances | Two-stage sequential operations |
| Physical terminal seal | `olcthr=` (P.12) | "Fluid in conduit" — physical, not process |
| Bare completion | `ain` (P.11) | Simply "complete" — no qualifications |

### Completion Marker Distribution

| Marker | Count | Paragraphs |
|--------|-------|-----------|
| `daiin` | 3 | P.1, P.9, (also within compounds) |
| `saiin` | 1 | P.12 (within daraiinm-saiin compound) |
| `aiim` | 1 | P.10 (vessel-variant) |
| `ain` | 1 | P.11 (bare completion) |
| `olcthr=` | 1 | Phase 1 terminal (physical seal) |
| `otol=` | 1 | Phase 2 terminal (temporal-fluid seal) |

**6 completion markers in 12 paragraphs** — one per 2 paragraphs. LESS verification-dense than f87r (which had 14 in 15 paragraphs). The lock-and-bottle protocol is less obsessively verified because it's working with ALREADY-VERIFIED material from f87r. The preface did the heavy verification; the sealing protocol trusts it.

### F-Atom Presence

**ZERO F-atom tokens on f87v.** Same as f87r. The first two pages of the pharmaceutical section contain NO growth/vegetative principle. These pages define INFRASTRUCTURE and PROCESS. The biological material hasn't entered yet.

### Hyphenated Compounds (Sequential Operations)

| Compound | Line | Translation | Sequential Logic |
|----------|------|-------------|-----------------|
| `ochepchody-oldar` | P.1 (Line 1) | Heat-volatile-project-fix THEN fluid-fix-root | Process THEN seal |
| `cthos-dcheecthey` | P.3 (Line 6) | Conduit-salt THEN fix-volatile-conduit-essence | Transport THEN fix-in-transit |
| `scheom-dcheos` | P.4 (Line 7) | Salt-vessel THEN fix-volatile-salt | Deliver THEN fix |
| `sheol-techol` | P.6 (Line 9) | Essence-fluid THEN energy-volatile-fluid | Dissolve THEN energize |
| `daraiinm-saiin` | P.12 (Line 4) | Fix-root-vessel THEN salt-verify | Seal THEN verify |

**FIVE hyphenated compounds on f87v.** Compare: f87r had ONE (`ochepchody-oldar` in P.1). The lock-and-bottle protocol is INHERENTLY SEQUENTIAL — each operation must complete before the next begins. The hyphen encodes this dependency linguistically. Sealing is a sequence of dependent steps; you cannot skip ahead.

---

## WHAT F87V TELLS US

The lock-and-bottle protocol says:

**Phase 1 (Lines 1–4):** "Project the volatile essence at double-e precision. Verify IMMEDIATELY. Heat-fix it. Fix the volatile's essence specifically. Apply the cph- process. Dissolve the vessel's salt interface, transmute at root, deliver into vessel. Salt-structure forms. Vessel-completion (not cycle-completion). Then compress to monosyllables: salt, root, structure. Fix-root-vessel, salt-verify. FLUID LOCKED IN CONDUIT. SEALED."

**Phase 2 (Lines 5–9):** "Now circulate within the sealed system. Salt-conduit circuit. The conduit doesn't just transport — it transforms. Double-e sensitivity throughout. *Transmute.* *Extract.* Twice. Temporal heat drives to fluid. SEALED."

**Post-Seal (Lines 10–12):** "Open carefully — controlled expansion through conduits. Rotate the vessel. Extract a sample. Inspect the layered structure at TRIPLE-E SENSITIVITY. Approve and contain. Salt structures one last time. Verify. Ready for next stage."

The page is a SEALING MANUAL. It treats volatile material as DANGEROUS — requiring immediate verification, double-e precision, self-checking valves, and five sequential (hyphenated) dependent operations. The product ends up as fluid medicine in sealed conduit vessels, quality-inspected at triple-e resolution.

---

## F87R + F87V AS A UNIT

The recto-verso pair forms a complete PHARMACEUTICAL PRIMER:

| Aspect | F87r (Preface) | F87v (Lock & Bottle) |
|--------|---------------|---------------------|
| Opens with | Project FLUID | Project VOLATILE (double-e) |
| Dominant prefix | sal- (salt: 14) | cth- (conduit: 9) |
| Terminal seals | daiin= (verify), qoty= (transmute) | olcthr= (physical), otol= (temporal-fluid) |
| Verification density | 14 in 15 paragraphs | 6 in 12 paragraphs |
| Hyphenated compounds | 1 | 5 |
| Triple-e tokens | 2 (ysheees, qoeeety) | 1 (lseeey) |
| Crystallization | YES (chekal, Line 12) | NO |
| Product form | Crystal (active-solid-matrix) | Fluid (in sealed conduit) |
| F-atoms | 0 | 0 |
| Function | Define the template | Define the sealing |

Together they say: "Here is how pharmaceutical processing works (f87r). Here is how you capture and seal what it produces (f87v). Now you're ready for actual recipes."

**NEXT: F88R — Three-Stage SOP: Recipe as Iteration**

---
# VML PHARMACEUTICAL SECTION — FOLIO F88R

## THREE-STAGE SOP: Recipe as Iteration
### The First Actual Recipe — Multi-Chambered Processing

---

## POSITION AND SIGNIFICANCE

F88r is the FIRST ACTUAL RECIPE in the pharmaceutical section. Where f87r defined the template and f87v defined the sealing protocol, f88r runs the template on real material. But it does something unprecedented: it organizes the recipe into THREE EXPLICITLY NUMBERED STAGES, visible in the paragraph numbering itself:

- **Stage 1:** P1.1, P1.2, P1.3, P1.4, P1.5 (5 paragraphs)
- **Stage 2:** P2.6, P2.7, P2.8, P2.9, P2.10 (5 paragraphs)
- **Stage 3:** P3.11, P3.12, P3.13, P3.14, P3.15, P3.16 (6 paragraphs)

This three-stage numbering system appears NOWHERE in the herbal, astrological, balneological, or cosmological sections. It is a pharmaceutical invention: the explicit labeling of processing stages within a single recipe. The visual shows multi-chambered jar illustrations connected by tubes — each chamber is one stage.

The principle it establishes: RECIPE AS ITERATION. The same transformation cycle runs three times, each pass at a finer/stiffer stage. Stage 1 names the parts and runs the program. Stage 2 runs the program under the parts. Stage 3 repeats at maximum refinement. The product of each stage becomes the INPUT for the next.

---

## STAGE 1: NAME THE PARTS (P1.1–P1.5)

### Line 1 / P1.1: OPENING — Fix at Root, Route Through Apparatus

**EVA:** `darsheoy.ctheol.qockhey.dary.sheor.sholfchor.dal.chcthol-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `darsheoy` | FIX/STABILIZE → root/projection | **THE FIRST RECIPE OPENS WITH FIXATION.** Not projection (poal, f87r) or volatile projection (pcheey, f87v), but FIXATION. The recipe assumes the material is already in the system — it's been prepared (f87r) and sealed (f87v). Now it gets FIXED at root/projection. The compound includes she(transition) + o(heat) + y(active): fix through heat-transition, actively. |
| `ctheol` | CONDUIT/BIND-ENERGY → eol | Conduit routes to essence-fluid. The apparatus is engaged. |
| `qockhey` | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → ckhey | Transmute through the valve system. First qo- of the recipe — transmutation via valve, same pattern as f87r P.14. |
| `dary` | FIX/STABILIZE → root/projection → [active/energized] | **SECOND fixation in 4 tokens.** Fix at root, active state. The double-d opening (darsheoy → dary) is emphatic: fix, process, fix AGAIN. |
| `sheor` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → source/rotation | Essence transitions to source rotation. Recalibration — checking against the source. |
| `sholfchor` | TRANSITION-HEAT → lfchor | Complex compound: sho(transition-heat) + l(fluid) + f(formative) + ch(volatile) + or(source/rotation). FIVE MORPHEMES. Heat transitions through fluid-formative-volatile to source. Note the embedded f- — this compound CONTAINS the formative/vegetative principle within a transition operation. The F-atom is embedded, not standalone. |
| `dal` | FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix | Fix into structural matrix. Third fixation marker in the paragraph. |
| `chcthol` | CHANNEL/SPIRIT → cthol | Spirit channel routes through conduit-fluid. The spiritual/channel dimension engages. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** FIX at root through heat-transition → conduit routes to fluid → transmute through valve → FIX at root (active) → return to source → heat transitions through fluid-formative-volatile-source → FIX in structural matrix → spirit channels through conduit.

**Critical observation:** THREE fixation operations in 8 tokens: `darsheoy`, `dary`, `dal`. The first recipe paragraph is FIXATION-SATURATED. Where f87r opened with projection and f87v opened with volatile projection, f88r opens with triple fixation. The material is being LOCKED DOWN before anything else happens.

The embedded F-atom in `sholfchor` is subtle but significant. The formative/vegetative principle (f-) appears INSIDE a transition compound, not as a standalone token. It's not saying "apply the growth principle" — it's saying "transition through the growth state." The material passes through a formative zone during its heat-transition. The growth principle is encountered, not applied.

---

### Line 2 / P1.2: THE SALT CATHEDRAL — Four Salt Tokens in One Paragraph

**EVA:** `sal.sheam.kol.cheyr.shekar.qokor.daiin.sar.saiin.oky.sam-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `sal` | SALT/FLOWING → structure/matrix | Salt structures. Opening salt declaration. |
| `sheam` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → union/vessel | Essence transitions into the union vessel. The material enters the first processing chamber. |
| `kol` | BODY/CONTAIN → fluid | Body contains the fluid. The vessel holds liquid. |
| `cheyr` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → yr → [active/energized] | Volatile essence active and rotating/projecting. The material is energized within the vessel. |
| `shekar` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → essence-root | Essence transitions to its own root. Deep self-referential operation: the essence finds its own foundation. |
| `qokor` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → source/rotation | Extract the essence at its source rotation. Pull the essential principle while the material rotates. |
| `daiin` | FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle | Verification checkpoint. |
| `sar` | SALT/FLOWING → root/projection | Salt at the root. |
| `saiin` | SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle | Salt completes its cycle. |
| `oky` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → y → [active/energized] | Phase-shift to active state. |
| `sam` | SALT/FLOWING → union/vessel | **SALT DELIVERS TO VESSEL.** |

**Paragraph-level reading:** SALT structures → essence enters vessel → body contains fluid → volatile essence activates → essence finds its root → EXTRACT essence at rotation → VERIFY → salt at root → salt cycles → phase-shift activates → SALT TO VESSEL.

**Critical observation:** FOUR SALT TOKENS in one paragraph: `sal`, `sar`, `saiin`, `sam`. Each represents a different salt function:
- `sal` = salt as STRUCTURE (the framework)
- `sar` = salt at ROOT (the foundation)
- `saiin` = salt CYCLING (the process verification)
- `sam` = salt into VESSEL (the delivery)

This paragraph is a SALT CATHEDRAL — salt performing four distinct roles in a single processing step. The material is being structured by salt (sal), rooted by salt (sar), verified by salt (saiin), and delivered by salt (sam). The salt principle IS the first stage.

The `shekar` token (transition-essence → essence-root) is noteworthy: the essence transitions to its OWN root. Not "root" as an external structural feature, but the essence's INHERENT root — its fundamental nature. Stage 1 identifies what the material IS at its deepest level.

---

### Line 3 / P1.3: HEAT BURST — Rapid Fire Activation

**EVA:** `oaiin.or.am.otam.okeom.cheeor.qokeody.dar.or.om.cheody-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `oaiin` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → double-life-cycle | Heat activates through full cycle. |
| `or` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → r | Heat-rotation. Bare, fast. |
| `am` | union/vessel | Into vessel. |
| `otam` | TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → union/vessel | Temporal heat into vessel. |
| `okeom` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eom | Phase-shift into essence-heat-vessel. |
| `cheeor` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → eor | Double-e volatile essence projecting from source. |
| `qokeody` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → eody | Extract essence to heat-fixation state. |
| `dar` | FIX/STABILIZE → root/projection | Fix at root. |
| `or` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → r | Heat again. Bare. |
| `om` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → m | Heat to vessel. |
| `cheody` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-fix → [active/energized] | Volatile essence heat-fixed, active. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Heat cycles → heat rotates → vessel → temporal heat to vessel → phase-shift to vessel → double-e volatile projects → EXTRACT to fixation → fix root → heat → heat-to-vessel → volatile heat-fixed active.

**Critical observation:** This paragraph EXPLODES with short tokens. Average length: 3.7 characters. Compare P1.1's average of ~6.5 characters. The language has shifted from complex compounds to RAPID-FIRE monosyllables and disyllables: `or.am.otam.okeom` — heat, vessel, heat-vessel, shift-vessel. Four operations in four beats.

The o- prefix (heat/activate) appears FIVE TIMES: `oaiin`, `or`, `otam`, `okeom`, `or`, `om`. This is a HEAT PARAGRAPH. After salt-structuring (P1.2), the material is being BLASTED with heat — rapid, repeated, from multiple angles. The material enters vessels, gets heated, phase-shifts, gets extracted, gets fixed, gets heated again. It's a bombardment.

The double `or` (heat-rotate, positions 2 and 9) creates a frame around the central processing block. Heat bookends the extraction and fixation.

---

### Line 4 / P1.4: THE TRIPLE-E EMERGES — doleeey

**EVA:** `qokeol.cheol.saiin.cheos.cheol.doleeey.or.cheom.cheomam-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `qokeol` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → eol | Extract essence to fluid. |
| `cheol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid | Volatile essence as fluid. |
| `saiin` | SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle | Salt verification. |
| `cheos` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → os | Volatile essence in heat-salt blend. |
| `cheol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid | **REPEATED.** Same token again — volatile essence as fluid. The material keeps returning to fluid state. |
| `doleeey` | FIX-FLUID → triple-intensity → [active/energized] | **TRIPLE-E.** do(fix) + l(fluid) + eee(TRIPLE-INTENSITY) + y(active). Fix the fluid at MAXIMUM SENSITIVITY in active state. This is Stage 1's critical operation — the fluid is fixed at triple-e resolution. |
| `or` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → r | Heat activates. |
| `cheom` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → vessel | Volatile essence into vessel. |
| `cheomam` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → vessel → [union/vessel] | **DOUBLE VESSEL.** che(volatile-essence) + om(vessel) + am(union-vessel). The volatile goes into a vessel WITHIN a vessel. Nested containment. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Extract to fluid → volatile-fluid → salt verifies → volatile-blend → volatile-fluid AGAIN → **FIX FLUID AT TRIPLE-E** → heat → vessel → **VESSEL WITHIN VESSEL.**

**Critical observation — doleeey:** This is the first triple-e token in an ACTUAL RECIPE (f87r's triple-e tokens were in the preface/template). `doleeey` = FIX-FLUID at triple-intensity. The fluid fixation demands maximum sensitivity. This tells us: the transition from fluid to fixed state is the recipe's MOST SENSITIVE OPERATION. Get this wrong and everything fails. The triple-e ensures the fixation happens with absolute precision.

**Critical observation — cheomam (nested vessel):** The compound `cheomam` = volatile-essence → vessel → union-vessel. The -om (vessel) gets a SECOND vessel suffix (-am). This is nesting: the product goes into a vessel, and that vessel goes into a UNION vessel. In practical pharmaceutical terms: an inner container sealed inside an outer container. Double-walled containment. The triple-e-fixed product is SO precious or SO dangerous that it requires nested protection.

The doubled `cheol` (volatile-essence → fluid) at positions 2 and 5 frames the `saiin.cheos` pair. Extract to fluid → fluid → verify → blend → fluid again → THEN triple-e fix. The material must be confirmed as fluid TWICE before the critical fixation happens. No shortcuts.

---

### Line 5 / P1.5: STAGE 1 TERMINAL — Salt into Vessel, SEALED

**EVA:** `yokeody.cheom.qoor.chees.yteor.shy.sam=`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `yokeody` | RECEPTIVE/MOIST → phase | Moist-receptive principle undergoes phase change. The material, now triple-e-fixed and nested-contained, undergoes a FINAL phase shift. |
| `cheom` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → vessel | Volatile essence in vessel. |
| `qoor` | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → source/rotation | Transmute at source rotation. A calibration transmutation — checking against the source state. |
| `chees` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → es | Volatile essence-salt. Stripped form. |
| `yteor` | MOIST-ENERGY → eor | Moist energy projecting from source. |
| `shy` | VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → y → [active/energized] | Vigorous flow, active. A final stirring. |
| `sam=` | SALT/FLOWING → union/vessel **[TERMINAL SEAL]** | **STAGE 1 CLOSES.** Salt flows into the union vessel, and the equals sign SEALS. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Moist phase-change → volatile in vessel → transmute at source → volatile salt-essence → moist energy projects → vigorous stirring → **SALT TO VESSEL. SEALED.**

**Critical observation:** Stage 1's terminal is `sam=` — SALT delivers to VESSEL, sealed. Compare:
- f87r Phase 1 terminal: `daiin=` (fixation-verification)
- f87r Phase 2 terminal: `qoty=` (transmutation-active)
- f87v Phase 1 terminal: `olcthr=` (fluid-in-conduit)
- f87v Phase 2 terminal: `otol=` (temporal-fluid)
- f88r Stage 1 terminal: `sam=` (salt-into-vessel)

Each page has a DIFFERENT terminal type. The pharmaceutical section doesn't repeat terminal formulas — each phase ends with whatever ACTUALLY HAPPENS at that point. Stage 1 ends with salt delivery to the vessel because that's what Stage 1 DOES: it structures material with salt and puts it in a vessel.

---

## STAGE 1 SUMMARY

Stage 1 (5 paragraphs, 47 tokens) = **NAME THE PARTS:**
- P1.1: Triple fixation — lock the material down
- P1.2: Salt cathedral — structure, root, verify, deliver via salt
- P1.3: Heat burst — rapid-fire activation and phase-shifting
- P1.4: Triple-e fluid fixation, nested vessel containment
- P1.5: Final phase-shift, salt delivers to vessel, SEALED

**Dominant operations:** d- (fix, 7 instances), sal/s- (salt, 8 instances), o- (heat, 7 instances)
**Key discovery:** `doleeey` (triple-e fluid fixation), `cheomam` (nested vessel)
**Product:** Triple-e-fixed fluid in nested double-vessel, salt-sealed

---

## STAGE 2: RUN THE PROGRAM UNDER THE PARTS (P2.6–P2.10)

### Line 6 / P2.10: STAGE 2 HEADER — Return and Phase-Shift

**EVA:** `ychey.okaiin.chol.cheor.ol.chor.chol.sal=`

**Reading order note:** The manuscript reading order places P2.10 BEFORE P2.6, despite the numbering. The physical page layout determines reading order, not the paragraph numbers. P2.10 functions as the HEADER paragraph for Stage 2.

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `ychey` | MOIST-VOLATILE → essence-active | Moist volatile receives active essence. Stage 2 opens with RECEPTION — receiving the Stage 1 product. |
| `okaiin` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → double-life-cycle | Phase-shift with full cycle verification. The received material undergoes phase transformation and is verified. |
| `chol` | VOLATILE-HEAT → l | Volatile heat to fluid. |
| `cheor` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → source/rotation | **RETURN TO SOURCE.** The material goes back to its origin before Stage 2 processing. Same reset pattern as f87r Line 13 and f87v Line 10. |
| `ol` | FLUID-MEDIUM | Bare fluid. |
| `chor` | VOLATILE-HEAT → r | Volatile heat rotates. |
| `chol` | VOLATILE-HEAT → l | Volatile heat to fluid. REPEATED from position 3. |
| `sal=` | SALT/FLOWING → structure/matrix **[TERMINAL SEAL]** | **UNEXPECTED MID-STAGE SEAL.** Salt structures, and the equals sign closes. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Receive Stage 1 product → phase-shift with verification → volatile heat to fluid → RETURN TO SOURCE → fluid → volatile heat rotates → volatile heat to fluid → **SALT STRUCTURES. SEALED.**

**Critical observation — THE SHORTEST SEALED PARAGRAPH:** P2.10 is only 8 tokens long and SEALS with `sal=`. This is a MICRO-SEAL — a brief, sealed paragraph that functions as a gate between stages. It receives the Stage 1 product, resets it to source, and seals. It's a STAGE HANDOFF: "Stage 1 product received, reset to source, salt-sealed. Stage 2 may now proceed."

The `cheor` (return to source) is the key operation. Between stages, the material ALWAYS returns to its fundamental state. It doesn't carry forward any Stage 1 processing artifacts — it goes back to source and starts fresh. This is the iteration principle: each stage begins from the same starting point, not from the previous stage's endpoint.

The doubled `chol` (positions 3 and 7) frames `cheor.ol.chor` — return to source is bookended by volatile-heat-fluid transitions. The material liquefies, returns to source, and liquefies again. The source-return happens in the FLUID state.

---

### Line 7 / P2.6: CONTAIN AND PROJECT — The cph- Mystery Returns

**EVA:** `koacphy.cphol.orchor.pcheoly.otchol.oldy.salsaly-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `koacphy` | BODY/CONTAIN → oacphy | Body contains whatever cph- represents. The k- (body) prefix wraps around the mysterious cph- cluster. The cph- element is being HELD IN A CONTAINER. |
| `cphol` | [untranslatable] | Standalone cph- with fluid suffix. The cph- element in fluid form. |
| `orchor` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → rchor | Heat activates rotation-volatile-heat-rotation. Circular heating — the volatile heat turns on itself. |
| `pcheoly` | PROJECT-VOLATILE → eoly | Project the volatile as essence-fluid-active. The volatile substance is projected outward in liquid form. |
| `otchol` | TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → volatile-fluid | Temporal heat drives toward volatile fluid. Time-controlled heating produces liquid volatile. |
| `oldy` | FLUID-MEDIUM → dy → [fixed/stabilized] | Fluid fixed and stabilized. The liquid locks into place. |
| `salsaly` | SALT/FLOWING → structure/matrix | **DOUBLED SALT.** sal + sal + y = salt-salt-active. Salt structures TWICE. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Contain the cph- element → cph- as fluid → circular heating → project volatile as liquid → temporal heat produces volatile fluid → fluid FIXES → **SALT-SALT STRUCTURES.**

**Critical observation — salsaly:** The doubled salt `salsaly` is unique. We've seen `saldal` (salt + fix) on f87r, and `sam` (salt + vessel), but never `salsal` — salt doubling on ITSELF. This is DOUBLE SALT STRUCTURING — the salt framework is reinforced by a second layer of salt. In physical chemistry terms: a supersaturated salt matrix. The salt architecture isn't just present — it's DOUBLED.

The cph- cluster appears TWICE here (`koacphy`, `cphol`). Stage 2 is working WITH the cph- element that Stage 1 merely passed through. Whatever cph- represents — and it remains untranslated — Stage 2 actively processes it: containing it (koacphy), dissolving it as fluid (cphol), and then projecting it outward (pcheoly). This is the first time cph- is the SUBJECT of processing rather than a background element.

---

### Line 8 / P2.7: CRYSTALLIZATION AND DOUBLED TRANSMUTATION — The Heart of Stage 2

**EVA:** `dchey.chokal.daiin.qoekol.qoekol.qockhol.okol.cheol-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `dchey` | FIX-VOLATILE → essence-active | Fix the volatile's active essence. Opening fixation — the volatile is locked down. |
| `chokal` | VOLATILE-HEAT → active-solid-matrix | **CRYSTALLIZATION.** cho(volatile-heat) + kal(active-solid-matrix). The volatile-heat product crystallizes. Compare `chekal` on f87r (volatile-ESSENCE crystallizes) — here it's volatile-HEAT that crystallizes. Different input pathway, same endpoint: the active-solid-matrix. |
| `daiin` | FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle | Verify the crystallization. |
| `qoekol` | TRANSMUTE-ENERGY → essence-fluid | Transmute the crystal's energy to essence-fluid. The crystal is being RE-DISSOLVED — transmuted from solid back to liquid. |
| `qoekol` | TRANSMUTE-ENERGY → essence-fluid | **EXACT REPETITION.** The same token appears TWICE consecutively. Doubled transmutation: dissolve, dissolve again. Not a new operation — the SAME operation repeated for emphasis or thoroughness. |
| `qockhol` | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → ckhol | Transmute through valve to volatile-fluid. Third qo- in a row. The dissolved crystal passes through the valve system. |
| `okol` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → fluid | Phase-shift to fluid state. |
| `cheol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid | Volatile essence as fluid. Final state: liquid. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Fix volatile essence → **CRYSTALLIZE** → verify → DISSOLVE crystal to fluid → DISSOLVE AGAIN → transmute through valve → phase-shift to fluid → volatile-fluid endpoint.

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — THE CRYSTALLIZE-THEN-DISSOLVE CYCLE:**

This paragraph reveals the core pharmaceutical logic: CRYSTALLIZE, then DISSOLVE the crystal. The material doesn't stay as a crystal — it crystallizes (chokal), gets verified (daiin), and then is DISSOLVED back to fluid through TRIPLE transmutation (qoekol.qoekol.qockhol).

Why crystallize only to dissolve? Because crystallization is PURIFICATION. When a substance crystallizes, impurities are excluded from the crystal lattice. The crystal is PURER than the liquid it formed from. By dissolving the pure crystal back into fluid, you get a PURIFIED SOLUTION. This is recrystallization — one of the most fundamental techniques in pharmaceutical chemistry.

The doubled `qoekol` (identical transmutation repeated) means: dissolve it completely. Don't stop at partial dissolution. The repetition ensures thoroughness. In practical terms: make sure every crystal grain has returned to solution.

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — chokal vs chekal:**

| Token | Folio | Input | Output |
|-------|-------|-------|--------|
| `chekal` | f87r, f89v1, f84v, f86v6 | Volatile-ESSENCE → active-solid-matrix | Essence crystallizes |
| `chokal` | f88r P2.7 | Volatile-HEAT → active-solid-matrix | Heat crystallizes |

BOTH produce the same crystal (active-solid-matrix), but from different inputs. `chekal` crystallizes from essence (the purified extract). `chokal` crystallizes from heat (the energized state). Two pathways to the same product. This is consistent with real chemistry: crystals can form from solution (essence pathway) or from melt (heat pathway). The manuscript encodes BOTH crystallization mechanisms.

---

### Line 9 / P2.8: POST-DISSOLUTION — Extract and Salt-Seal

**EVA:** `dsheol.qokeey.schy.saiin.chor.oteor.aiin.chosals-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `dsheol` | FIX-TRANSITION → eol | Fix the transition product as fluid. The dissolved crystal (from P2.7) is fixed in its fluid state. |
| `qokeey` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → essence-active | Extract active essence at double-e sensitivity. High-precision extraction from the purified solution. |
| `schy` | SALT/FLOWING → volatile-active | Salt flowing with active volatile. Salt medium carrying the extract. |
| `saiin` | SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle | Salt verification. |
| `chor` | VOLATILE-HEAT → r | Volatile heat rotates. |
| `oteor` | TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → eor | Temporal heat drives essence to rotation/projection. Time-controlled heating. |
| `aiin` | double-life-cycle | **BARE COMPLETION.** Just the cycle marker, no prefix. Like the bare `ain` on f87v — stripped, emphatic. |
| `chosals` | VOLATILE-HEAT → salt-structure | Volatile heat PRODUCES salt structure. The heat generates the salt framework. This is the INVERSE of `sal` (salt-as-structure): here, heat creates salt from the material itself. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Fix dissolved crystal as fluid → extract at double-e → salt carries extract → salt verifies → volatile heat rotates → temporal heat drives → CYCLE COMPLETE → volatile heat produces salt structure.

**Critical observation — chosals:** The compound `chosals` = volatile-heat → salt-structure. The volatile heat (cho) generates a salt structure (sals). This is ENDOGENOUS SALT FORMATION — the material's own heat produces the salt that structures the next phase. Compare the `salsaly` from P2.6 (exogenous double-salt applied from outside). Stage 2 introduces BOTH external salt structuring (P2.6) and internal salt generation (P2.8). The salt comes from both outside and inside.

The double-e extraction `qokeey` operating on the recrystallized solution confirms: recrystallization produces a PURER extract. The essence is now clean enough for double-e-sensitivity extraction. Before recrystallization, the extraction didn't need elevated sensitivity. After recrystallization, it demands it — because the material is now pure enough that even tiny impurities would be detected.

---

### Line 10 / P2.9: STAGE 2 FINAL — Triple Extraction to Multiple Outputs

**EVA:** `teol.chor.olsheody.qokeol.shockhy.ol.sheeol.sheol.dm-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `teol` | ENERGY/TEMPORAL → eol | Temporal energy to essence-fluid. |
| `chor` | VOLATILE-HEAT → r | Volatile heat rotates. |
| `olsheody` | FLUID-MEDIUM → sheody | Fluid medium undergoes transition-heat-fixation. The liquid is being heat-treated. |
| `qokeol` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → eol | Extract essence to fluid. |
| `shockhy` | TRANSITION-HEAT → ckhy | Heat transition into valve. The heated extract passes through a valve. |
| `ol` | FLUID-MEDIUM | Bare fluid marker. |
| `sheeol` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → eol | Double-e essence transition to fluid. Elevated sensitivity. |
| `sheol` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → fluid | Regular essence transition to fluid. Normal sensitivity. |
| `dm` | FIX/STABILIZE → m | **FIX-TO-VESSEL.** The d(fix) + m(vessel) compound. Fixation directly into vessel. The m-terminal again marks vessel-containment (same pattern as -aiim on f87v). |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Temporal energy to fluid → volatile heat rotates → fluid heat-treats → extract essence to fluid → heat through valve → fluid → double-e essence transition → normal essence transition → **FIX INTO VESSEL.**

**Critical observation — the sheeol/sheol pair:** Back-to-back essence transitions: `sheeol` (double-e, elevated sensitivity) followed by `sheol` (normal sensitivity). The material passes through BOTH resolution levels. First the fine filter (double-e), then the standard filter. This is GRADED FILTRATION — filtering at high precision first, then at normal precision. The double-e pass catches fine impurities; the standard pass catches anything that slipped through.

The terminal `dm` (fix-to-vessel) echoes f87v's `-aiim` vessel-containment pattern. Stage 2 ends by fixing the product directly into a vessel. But note: `dm` has a dash (-) after it, not an equals sign (=). Stage 2 doesn't have a HARD seal — it feeds into Stage 3.

## STAGE 2 SUMMARY

Stage 2 (5 paragraphs, 40 tokens) = **RUN THE PROGRAM UNDER THE PARTS:**
- P2.10: Stage handoff — receive, reset to source, micro-seal

- P2.7: CRYSTALLIZE → verify → TRIPLE DISSOLVE → fluid endpoint
- P2.8: Fix dissolved crystal, double-e extract, endogenous salt formation
- P2.9: Temporal processing, graded filtration (double-e then standard), fix to vessel

**Dominant operations:** qo-/qoek- (transmute/extract, 7 instances), cho-/che- (volatile, 14 instances)
**Key discoveries:** `chokal` (heat-crystallization), doubled `qoekol` (thorough dissolution), `chosals` (endogenous salt), `sheeol`/`sheol` pair (graded filtration)
**Product:** Recrystallized, double-e-extracted, graded-filtered solution in vessel

## STAGE 3: REPEAT AT FINER/STIFFER STAGE (P3.11–P3.16)

### Line 11 / P3.11: STAGE 3 OPENING — Double-E Projection at Phase-Shift

**EVA:** `poeeor.sheoky.olkeey.cthol.poldy.s.okaldy-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `poeeor` | PROJECT/FLUID → oeeor | **DOUBLE-E WITHIN PROJECTION.** p(project) + o(heat) + ee(double-e) + or(source/rotation). The Stage 3 projection operates at ELEVATED SENSITIVITY from its first token. Compare Stage 1's opening `darsheoy` (fixation) and Stage 2's header `ychey` (reception). Stage 3 opens with PROJECTION AT DOUBLE-E. Each stage escalates. |
| `sheoky` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → phase → [active/energized] | Essence transitions through active phase-shift. |
| `olkeey` | FLUID-MEDIUM → keey | Fluid medium contains body-essence-active at double-e. ANOTHER double-e token — the second in 3 tokens. |
| `cthol` | CONDUIT/BIND-ENERGY → fluid | Conduit routes to fluid. |
| `poldy` | PROJECT/FLUID → fluid → [fixed/stabilized] | Project fluid, fix it, stabilize it. |
| `s` | SALT/FLOWING | **BARE SALT.** The single-character pause. *Salt.* Same punctuation marker as f87r P.4 and f87v P.2. |
| `okaldy` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → structure/matrix → [fixed/stabilized] | Phase-shift to structural matrix, fixed. The material phase-shifts into solid structure. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** PROJECT at double-e → essence phase-shifts actively → fluid at double-e → conduit routes → project-fix fluid → *salt* → phase-shift to structural matrix, fixed.

**Critical observation:** TWO double-e tokens in the opening paragraph (`poeeor`, `olkeey`). Stage 3 operates at CONSISTENTLY ELEVATED SENSITIVITY — not just at peak moments (like Stage 1's triple-e), but as the BASELINE. The refinement has progressed: Stage 1 reached triple-e at one critical point; Stage 3 STARTS at double-e and stays there.

The bare `s` (salt) appears again in its punctuation role. Three pages in, the pattern is established: the standalone `s` marks a transition between operations. It appears at the boundary between "project-fix fluid" and "phase-shift to structure." The salt moment divides fluid from solid.

### Line 12 / P3.12: QUADRUPLE EXTRACTION — The Most Intensive Processing

**EVA:** `qokal.chol.qokol.qokol.chol.cheey.ar.aiin.oldal-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `qokal` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → structure/matrix | Extract the structural essence. Pulling the structural principle out. |
| `chol` | VOLATILE-HEAT → l | Volatile heat to fluid. |
| `qokol` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → fluid | Extract to fluid. |
| `qokol` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → fluid | **EXACT REPETITION.** Same extraction, repeated. |
| `chol` | VOLATILE-HEAT → l | Volatile heat to fluid. **Also repeated** — same as position 2. |
| `cheey` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → essence-active | Double-e volatile essence, active. |
| `ar` | root/projection | Root. Bare. |
| `aiin` | double-life-cycle | Cycle complete. Bare. |
| `oldal` | FLUID-MEDIUM → fix-structure | Fluid fixed into structure. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Extract structure → heat-fluid → extract to fluid → extract to fluid AGAIN → heat-fluid AGAIN → double-e volatile → root → cycle complete → fluid fixes to structure.

**Critical observation — FOUR EXTRACTIONS in one paragraph:** `qokal` + `qokol` + `qokol` = three qo- operations, plus the implicit extraction in `cheey`. Stage 2 had triple transmutation (qoekol.qoekol.qockhol). Stage 3 has QUADRUPLE extraction. Each stage INCREASES the number of repeated operations.

The pattern `qokol.qokol.chol` mirrors Stage 2's `qoekol.qoekol.qockhol` — doubled identical operation followed by a variant. This is ESTABLISHED PRACTICE: repeat the exact operation twice, then vary. The doubling ensures thoroughness; the variation advances the process.

The paired `chol` at positions 2 and 5 creates a mirror: chol-qokol-qokol-chol. The extractions are FRAMED by volatile-heat-fluid transitions. Heat liquefies, extraction pulls, heat liquefies again.

### Line 13 / P3.13: VALVE INSPECTION AND SALT RETURN

**EVA:** `ykar.cheol.chol.chey.ckhey.sor.shear.ar.alsy-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `ykar` | MOIST-BODY → root/projection | Moist body at root. The wet container at its foundation. |
| `cheol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid | Volatile as fluid. |
| `chol` | VOLATILE-HEAT → l | Volatile heat to fluid. |
| `chey` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → y → [active/energized] | Active volatile essence. |
| `ckhey` | VALVE/BIND-VOLATILE → essence-active | Valve binds active volatile. QUALITY GATE — the valve inspects the product. |
| `sor` | SALT/FLOWING → source/rotation | Salt returns to source rotation. |
| `shear` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → root/projection | Essence transitions to root. Deep return. |
| `ar` | root/projection | Root. Bare. |
| `alsy` | structure/matrix → [salt-active] | Structure with active salt. The structural matrix has active salt within it. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Moist body at root → volatile fluid → heat fluid → active volatile → **VALVE INSPECTS** → salt returns to source → essence returns to root → root → salt-active structure.

**Critical observation:** After the intensive quadruple extraction (P3.12), P3.13 performs QUALITY CONTROL. The `ckhey` valve binds and inspects the active volatile. Then everything returns: salt to source (`sor`), essence to root (`shear`), root itself (`ar`). Three consecutive "return" tokens. The system RESETS after inspection.

The terminal `alsy` (structure/matrix → salt-active) introduces a new form: the salt principle is now ACTIVE WITHIN the structure. Not applied externally (like `sal`) or generated internally (like `chosals`), but ACTIVE — the salt is part of the living structure, energized and functional.

### Line 14 / P3.14: TEMPORAL EXTRACTION WITH ASTERISK ANOMALY

**EVA:** `tor.chey.qokol.cheol.chody.qokol.*chos.chol.dal-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `tor` | ENERGY/TEMPORAL → source/rotation | Temporal energy at source. Time begins. |
| `chey` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → y → [active/energized] | Active volatile essence. |
| `qokol` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → fluid | Extract to fluid. |
| `cheol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid | Volatile-fluid. |
| `chody` | VOLATILE-HEAT → dy → [fixed/stabilized] | Volatile heat fixed and stabilized. |
| `qokol` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → fluid | Extract to fluid AGAIN. Second extraction. |
| `*chos` | [partially illegible] + VOLATILE-HEAT → s | **EVA TRANSCRIPTION NOTE.** The asterisk (*) is EVA transcriber notation meaning "don't know / illegible" — the transcriber was uncertain about the glyph(s) preceding `chos`. This is NOT a scribal annotation in the original manuscript. The original likely has a normal glyph that was unclear in the available images. |
| `chol` | VOLATILE-HEAT → l | Volatile heat to fluid. |
| `dal` | FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix | Fix into structural matrix. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Time begins → active volatile → extract to fluid → volatile-fluid → volatile heat fixed → extract to fluid AGAIN → **[*]volatile-heat-salt** → heat to fluid → fix into structure.

**Critical observation — transcription uncertainty at *chos:** The `*` before `chos` is EVA convention for "illegible/uncertain" — the modern transcriber couldn't confidently identify the glyph(s) at this position. This is NOT an annotation in the original manuscript. We should treat `chos` itself as the readable portion (volatile-heat → salt) while noting that the preceding glyph is unknown. This means the actual token might be longer (e.g., a prefix + chos), which would change its morphological analysis.

The doubled `qokol` (positions 3 and 6) continues the pattern from P3.12: extract, extract again. Stage 3 is RELENTLESSLY extractive — pulling material out of solution over and over. Each extraction pulls a finer fraction.
