## STAGE 2: THE NON-VOYNICHESE INTRUSION (P2.4–P2.7)

### Line 4 / P2.4: THE ALIEN PARAGRAPH

**EVA:** `porachol.qody.qoteol.oldaq.gtgl.seg*.sg*.gltaq.gt*gl.*egl.gtglf*y.tar.cho.lkeopol.oeeor.ar-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `porachol` | PROJECT/FLUID → source/rotation | Project fluid at source rotation. Normal Voynichese opening. |
| `qody` | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → dy → [fixed/stabilized] | Transmute to fixation. Normal. |
| `qoteol` | TRANSMUTE-HEAT → eol | Heat transmutation to essence-fluid. Normal. |
| `oldaq` | FLUID-MEDIUM → daq | Fluid medium to fix-root-[q?]. Transitional — still partly Voynichese but `q` alone at the end is unusual. |
| `gtgl` | **[NON-VOYNICHESE]** | **NOT TRANSLATABLE IN EVA OR VML.** The letter `g` does not appear in standard Voynichese. This token uses characters from a DIFFERENT writing system. |
| `seg*` | SALT/FLOWING → eg [+ illegible glyph] | Partially Voynichese: s- (salt) + e + g(non-standard) + *(illegible). Hybrid token — standard prefix with non-standard continuation. |
| `sg*` | SALT/FLOWING → g [+ illegible glyph] | Same pattern: s- prefix with non-standard characters. |
| `gltaq` | **[NON-VOYNICHESE]** | Non-standard characters throughout. |
| `gt*gl` | **[NON-VOYNICHESE + illegible]** | Non-standard with transcription uncertainty. |
| `*egl` | [illegible glyph] + **[NON-VOYNICHESE]** | Starts illegible, continues non-standard. |
| `gtglf*y` | **[NON-VOYNICHESE + illegible]** | Contains `f` (which IS a Voynichese character) and `y` (also standard), but `g`, `t`, `l` sequence is non-standard. Note the embedded `f` — possibly the F-atom (formative/vegetative) within a non-Voynichese context. |
| `tar` | ENERGY/TEMPORAL → root/projection | Normal Voynichese resumes. |
| `cho` | VOLATILE-HEAT | Normal. |
| `lkeopol` | LAYER/STRUCTURE → keopol | Layer-structure compound. Normal. |
| `oeeor` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → essence-energy → [source/projecting] | Double-e heat activation. Normal. |
| `ar` | root/projection | Root. Normal. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** [Normal Voynichese: project-transmute-transmute-fluid] → **[7 NON-VOYNICHESE/HYBRID TOKENS]** → [Normal Voynichese resumes: temporal-volatile-layer-heat-root].

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — THE NON-VOYNICHESE INTRUSION:**

P2.4 contains a BLOCK of 7 consecutive tokens (`gtgl` through `gtglf*y`) that use characters not found in standard Voynichese. The `g` character in particular is essentially absent from the Voynichese alphabet. These tokens are SANDWICHED between normal Voynichese text — the paragraph opens and closes in standard language.

What are these tokens? Several possibilities, all of which must remain hypothetical:

1. **A different notation system:** The "multiple ingredient families" may include one ingredient whose NAME requires characters outside Voynichese — perhaps from Latin, Hebrew, Arabic, or another script. The scale-up panel proves universality; one ingredient family might have a non-Voynichese name.

2. **Numerical notation:** The `g`, `t`, `l` characters might represent NUMBERS in a pharmaceutical dosage notation. The repeated `gtgl` pattern is consistent with a numerical value being expressed multiple times (measurement, ratio, proportion).

3. **Scribal notation or marginalia:** These could be later additions, cross-references, or marks from a different hand/period, incorporated into the transcription as if they were main text.

4. **A different cipher layer:** The pharmaceutical section might use a SECOND encoding system for specific types of information (dosages, ingredient sources, practitioner identities) that the primary Voynichese doesn't encode.

The asterisks (`*`) within these tokens are EVA transcriber notation for illegible glyphs — the transcriber couldn't read them, which is unsurprising given the already non-standard nature of the characters.

**Critical observation — the salt hybrids:** `seg*` and `sg*` begin with standard s- (salt/flowing) before transitioning to non-standard characters. The salt prefix BRIDGES between Voynichese and the non-standard system. Whatever these tokens represent, the salt principle mediates between the two notation systems. Salt as TRANSLATOR between languages — a role consistent with salt as the universal structuring agent.

**We must flag this entire block as UNTRANSLATABLE and resist constructing VML interpretations of characters that are not Voynichese.** The temptation to force-fit these into the morphological framework would contaminate the analysis.

---

### Line 5 / P2.5: THE PHASE-SHIFT CASCADE — Five ok- Tokens

**EVA:** `daiin.olkey.okeol.okey.okeeol.qoor.ol.chor.cheky.chol.daiin.eol.cheol.kol.dam.olcheol.dal.cheol-`

**Token-by-token (selected highlights):**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `okeol` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eol | Phase-shift to essence-fluid. |
| `okey` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → essence-active | Phase-shift to active essence. |
| `okeeol` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → essence-energy → [fluid/elevated] | Phase-shift at double-e to elevated fluid. |
| `eol` | [bare suffix] | Essence-fluid standing alone. No prefix. |
| `olcheol` | FLUID-MEDIUM → cheol | Fluid medium carries volatile-fluid. Compound fluid-in-fluid. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Verify → fluid-body → PHASE-SHIFT → PHASE-SHIFT → PHASE-SHIFT (double-e) → transmute-source → fluid → volatile-heat → volatile-moist → heat-fluid → verify → bare essence-fluid → volatile-fluid → body-fluid → fix-vessel → fluid-volatile → fix-structure → volatile-fluid.

**Critical observation — the ok- cascade:** Three consecutive ok- (phase-shift) tokens: `okeol`, `okey`, `okeeol`. Each shifts to a DIFFERENT endpoint: essence-fluid, essence-active, essence-energy at double-e. The material is being phase-shifted through THREE DISTINCT STATES in rapid succession. This is MULTI-STATE PROCESSING — the same material occupying three different phase states within a single operation.

The triple phase-shift escalates sensitivity: okeol (standard) → okey (active) → okeeol (double-e, elevated). Each shift REFINES the target state. The scale-up panel doesn't just process at one level — it sweeps through a RANGE of phase states.

`eol` stands alone at position 12 — bare essence-fluid with no prefix. Like the bare `r` on f89r1, the foldout sections allow naked morphemes as standalone operations. Here: *essence-fluid* as a state declaration, not an operation performed on essence-fluid.

18 tokens — the longest paragraph on f89r2. The post-non-Voynichese recovery requires extensive processing to return the material to standard Voynichese operations.

**Critical observation — the extraction-phase-shift alternation:** The ok- and qok- prefixes ALTERNATE throughout this paragraph. Extract → phase-shift → extract → phase-shift. This is the scale-up panel's operational signature: it doesn't just extract OR shift — it ALTERNATES between them in rapid cycles. Each extraction feeds a phase-shift; each phase-shift enables the next extraction. The two operations are coupled.

THREE okey/okeey tokens in one paragraph, PLUS two qok- extractions. The extraction-phase-shift engine runs at 5 operations in 18 tokens = 28% of all tokens are either extraction or phase-shift. This paragraph IS the "Universal Extraction Machine" — its every other operation is extract or shift.

The sequence `qo.qol` reads: *Transmute. Transmute to fluid.* Two commands in succession, the second slightly more specified than the first. The scale-up panel issues ORDERS to the material: transform, then liquefy.

**Critical observation — raimor (recursive completion):** The compound `raimor` = rotation/source → aim(completion-vessel) → or(heat-rotation). The rotation reaches completion in a vessel, then ROTATES AGAIN (the terminal -or). This is a RECURSIVE LOOP marker: the rotation doesn't stop at completion — it feeds back into another rotation. The scale-up panel's Stage 3 contains self-reinforcing cycles.

Five systems — heat, rotation, transmutation, spirit, fixation — all reach completion in one paragraph. The scale-up panel doesn't close one system at a time — it closes ALL OF THEM at once.

**Critical observation — bare y:** The standalone `y` (active/energized) between the two `dair` tokens creates: `dair.y.dair=` — fix-root → *active* → fix-root-sealed. The material is root-fixed, ACTIVATED, then root-fixed AGAIN with the seal. The activation happens BETWEEN two fixations. The product is fixed, energized, then re-fixed while energized. It enters storage in an ACTIVE-FIXED state — locked but alive.

**Critical observation — doubled dair=:** The terminal is `dair.y.dair=` — fix-root TWICE with active state between. Compare f89r1's doubled dair at P3.14 terminal (`okar.dair.y.dair=` — same pattern!). The foldout pages share a TERMINAL FORMULA: fix-root → active → fix-root → seal. This is the foldout's signature closure: lock, energize, lock again.

## POST-SEAL OPERATIONS (P3.8–P3.9)

### Line 13 / P3.8: THE F-ATOM EXTRACTION AND DOUBLE EXPANSION

**EVA:** `kolches.sheol.qokeofy.sheey.opchear.opcheol.shody.sholdy.qokal.chey.oldy.sheodal.ytoldy-`

**Token-by-token (selected highlights):**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |

| `qokeofy` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → eofy | **THE F-ATOM WITHIN EXTRACTION.** qok(extract) + e(essence) + of(formative-source/vegetative) + y(active). The extraction INCLUDES the F-atom. Not "extract then apply growth principle" — the extraction ITSELF pulls the formative element actively. |
| `sheey` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → essence-active | Essence transitions at double-e, actively. |
| `opchear` | EXPAND/PROJECT → chear | **EXPANSION** of volatile-essence to root. The op- (expand) prefix projects volatile to its root. |
| `opcheol` | EXPAND/PROJECT → cheol | **SECOND EXPANSION** of volatile-essence to fluid. Back-to-back op- tokens: expand to root, then expand to fluid. DOUBLE EXPANSION. |

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — qokeofy (F-atom within extraction):**

This is the THIRD F-atom token in the pharmaceutical section:

| Token | Folio | Structure | How F-atom appears |
|-------|-------|----------|-------------------|
| `ofal` | f88r P3.15 | of + al | F-atom structures material (active) |
| `yfalaiin` | f88v P2.6 | y + fal + aiin | F-atom received by moisture (passive) |
| `qokeofy` | f89r2 P3.8 | qok + eof + y | **F-atom WITHIN extraction (operational)** |

Three modes:
1. **Active:** The F-atom acts on structure (ofal)
2. **Receptive:** Moisture receives the F-atom (yfalaiin)
3. **Operational:** The F-atom is extracted alongside essence (qokeofy)

`qokeofy` means: the extraction PULLS the formative principle along WITH the essence. The growth principle isn't applied after extraction — it's PART OF what gets extracted. The material's biological nature is so intimately integrated with its chemical essence that you can't extract one without the other.

**Critical observation — opchear / opcheol (double expansion):** Two consecutive op- (expand) tokens, targeting different endpoints:
- `opchear` = expand volatile-essence to ROOT
- `opcheol` = expand volatile-essence to FLUID

Expansion to root means: the volatile's territory extends to the material's foundation. Expansion to fluid means: the expanded volatile dissolves into liquid. The double expansion first DEEPENS (to root) then DISSOLVES (to fluid). The post-seal operation opens up the sealed product and redistributes it.

These op- tokens appeared on f87v (controlled expansion after sealing). Here they appear in the same position — POST-SEAL. The expansion protocol is consistent: after sealing, controlled expansion redistributes the product.

### Line 14 / P3.9: THE FINAL PROCESSING — Spirit Channel Closes

**EVA:** `daiin.cheoko.keol.daiin.dal.dair.qokeey.okeol.daiin.ykeody.okeeo.chs.cheey.ykeol.cho.chckhy-`

**Token-by-token (selected highlights):**

**Paragraph-level reading:** Verify → volatile phase → body-fluid → verify → fix-structure → root-fix → double-e extract → phase-shift fluid → verify → moist-body → phase-energy → **SPIRIT → SALT** → double-e volatile → moist-body fluid → bare volatile-heat → **SPIRIT THROUGH VALVE.**

**Critical observation — the spiritual closure:** The page's FINAL TOKEN is `chckhy` — spirit through valve. The last word of the scale-up panel sends the spiritual dimension through the quality gate. Throughout the pharmaceutical section, the ch- (spirit/channel) prefix has tracked alongside physical processing. Here, at the very end of the scale-up panel, the spirit dimension gets its own VALVE PASSAGE.

The `chs` token (spirit → salt) is also notable: the spirit reaches SALT. In VML terms, salt is the universal structuring agent. The spirit reaching salt means the spiritual dimension has been STRUCTURED — given form, made concrete. Spirit becomes salt: the immaterial becomes the structuring principle.

## WHAT THE SCALE-UP PANEL TELLS US

F89r2 proves the pharmaceutical method is UNIVERSAL:

1. **Dense operations:** 16-17 tokens per Stage 1 paragraph (vs 5-10 on f89r1). The minimal loop SCALES by packing more operations per cycle.

2. **Triple daiin gate:** Unprecedented triple verification before processing. Multiple ingredient families require stricter entry control.

3. **Non-Voynichese intrusion:** Something in the pharmaceutical section requires notation OUTSIDE the primary writing system. Whether numerical dosages, foreign ingredient names, or a second cipher layer, the manuscript acknowledges the limits of its own language.

4. **Phase-shift cascades:** Triple ok- sequences process material through multiple states simultaneously. The scale-up panel doesn't process one state at a time — it sweeps through state-space.

5. **F-atom within extraction:** The growth principle can't be separated from the chemical essence — `qokeofy` pulls them out TOGETHER. Biology and chemistry are inseparable at this level of refinement.

6. **Convergent completion:** Five systems (heat, rotation, transmutation, spirit, fixation) reach completion simultaneously. The terminal paragraph closes ALL operational dimensions at once.

7. **Foldout terminal formula:** `dair.y.dair=` (fix-root → active → fix-root → seal) is shared between f89r1 and f89r2. The foldout has a signature closure pattern.

8. **Spiritual closure:** The page's last token sends spirit through the valve. The scale-up panel doesn't forget the spiritual dimension — it processes it through quality control alongside the physical product.

---
# VML PHARMACEUTICAL SECTION — FOLIO F89V1

## PROCESS STABILIZATION: Consistent Cycling
### Verso sub-page 1 of the Pharmaceutical Foldout

---

## POSITION AND SIGNIFICANCE

F89v1 is the third sub-page of the foldout — the VERSO of the first leaf. The source calls it: "Process stabilization page — ensures repeated cycling produces consistent results through controlled gating."

Where f89r1 defined the kernel and f89r2 proved universality, f89v1 ensures CONSISTENCY. The minimal loop, scaled up across ingredient families, must now produce the SAME result every time. This is quality control for mass production — the pharmaceutical equivalent of standardization.

---

## STRUCTURAL ARCHITECTURE

**Single Stage (16 paragraphs):** P1.1 → P1.2 → P1.3 → P1.4 → P1.5 → P1.6 → P1.7 → P1.9 → P1.10 → P1.11 → P1.12 → P1.13 → P1.14 → P1.15 → P1.16 → [no P1.8 in sequence]

Terminal seals:
- `odaiin=` (P1.7) — heat-activated verification, sealed. MID-PAGE SEAL.
- `ochyqokaiin=` (P1.11) — heat-volatile-active extraction-cycle, sealed. SECOND SEAL.
- `choldy=` (P1.16) — volatile-heat-fluid-fixed, sealed. THIRD/FINAL SEAL.

**CRITICAL STRUCTURAL OBSERVATION:** F89v1 is the ONLY page in the pharmaceutical section with ALL PARAGRAPHS IN A SINGLE STAGE. Every previous page had 2-3 stages (numbered P1.x, P2.x, P3.x). Here everything is P1.x. There are no stage transitions.

But there ARE three sealed paragraphs (P1.7=, P1.11=, P1.16=), creating implicit sub-sections:
- Section A (P1.1–P1.7): 7 paragraphs → sealed at P1.7
- Section B (P1.9–P1.11): 3 paragraphs → sealed at P1.11
- Section C (P1.12–P1.16): 5 paragraphs → sealed at P1.16

Note: P1.8 is missing from the paragraph sequence — the numbering jumps from P1.7 to P1.9. Either P1.8 is physically elsewhere, was omitted, or the numbering reflects a different organizational logic on foldout versos.

The SINGLE-STAGE architecture is the point: stabilization means running the SAME stage over and over without escalation. The material doesn't progress through stages — it CYCLES within one stage until consistent.

---

## SECTION A: F-ATOM OPENING AND CRYSTALLIZATION (P1.1–P1.7)

### Line 1 / P1.1: THE F-ATOM OPENS THE PAGE

**EVA:** `kol.dal.sfal.cfhey.ofcheol.opolsy.daiin.qopol.oldaiin.octhody-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `kol` | BODY/CONTAIN → fluid | Body contains fluid. Standard container opening. |
| `dal` | FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix | Fix structure. |
| `sfal` | SALT/FLOWING → fal | **SALT-TO-F-ATOM.** s(salt) + fal(formative-structure). Salt flows to the formative/vegetative principle. The VERY THIRD TOKEN of this page sends salt to the F-atom. |
| `cfhey` | [cfh- cluster — untranslatable] | The cfh- cluster. Related to cph- but with `f` instead of `p`. Both remain untranslatable, but cfh- appears alongside F-atom tokens, suggesting a connection. |
| `ofcheol` | FORMATIVE-SOURCE/VEGETATIVE → cheol | **F-ATOM DELIVERS VOLATILE-FLUID.** of(formative/vegetative) + che(volatile-essence) + ol(fluid). The F-atom produces volatile essence in fluid form. This is the F-atom as OUTPUT SOURCE — it GENERATES volatile fluid. |
| `opolsy` | EXPAND/PROJECT → fluid → [salt-active] | Expand/project fluid with active salt. The volatile fluid from the F-atom is expanded and salted. |
| `daiin` | FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle | Verify. |
| `qopol` | TRANSMUTE-FLUID → fluid | Transmute fluid. Redundant transmutation — already fluid, transmuted to fluid. The FORM changes while the STATE stays the same. |
| `oldaiin` | FLUID-MEDIUM → daiin → [fix-complete] | Fluid reaches fix-completion. |
| `octhody` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → cthody | Heat activates through conduit-heat-fixation. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Body-fluid → fix-structure → **SALT TO F-ATOM** → [cfh- cluster] → **F-ATOM PRODUCES VOLATILE-FLUID** → expand with salt → verify → transmute fluid → fluid verifies → heat-conduit activates.

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — F-atom opens the page:**

F89v1 is the FIRST pharmaceutical page where the F-atom appears in the OPENING PARAGRAPH. Compare:

| Page | F-atom position | Token | Role |
|------|----------------|-------|------|
| f88r | P3.15 (penultimate, Stage 3) | `ofal` | Structures material |
| f88v | P2.6 (mid-Stage 2) | `yfalaiin` | Received by moisture |
| f89r2 | P3.8 (post-seal) | `qokeofy` | Within extraction |
| **f89v1** | **P1.1 (OPENING)** | **`sfal`, `ofcheol`** | **Salt delivers to F-atom; F-atom SOURCES volatile** |

The F-atom has been MIGRATING forward through the pages: late Stage 3 → mid Stage 2 → post-seal → **OPENING**. By f89v1, the formative/growth principle has reached the BEGINNING of the process. It's no longer a late-stage addition — it's a STARTING CONDITION.

Two F-atom tokens in the opening paragraph:
1. `sfal` = salt delivers TO the F-atom (input)
2. `ofcheol` = F-atom produces volatile-fluid (output)

The F-atom is now a PROCESSING NODE: it receives salt, outputs volatile. It's not passive (f88v's reception) or auxiliary (f88r's structuring) — it's an active component of the extraction machine.

**Critical observation — cfhey:** The cfh- cluster appears alongside the F-atom tokens. On f87v, cph- appeared 4 times without clear context. Here cfh- sits between `sfal` (salt-to-F-atom) and `ofcheol` (F-atom output). The cfh-/cph- cluster may represent a REAGENT or CATALYST associated with the F-atom — something that mediates between salt and the formative principle. This remains hypothesis, not confirmed structure.

### Line 14 / P1.7: SECTION A TERMINAL — Crystallization Confirmed, Compound Seal

**EVA:** `osheo.kaiin.saiin.ol.shodaiin.qokar.aiin.chekal.daiin.dar-qokar.odaiin=`

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `osheo` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → sheo | Heat activates transition-energy. |
| `kaiin` | BODY/CONTAIN → double-life-cycle | Body completes cycle. |
| `saiin` | SALT/FLOWING → double-life-cycle | Salt verifies. |
| `shodaiin` | TRANSITION-HEAT → daiin → [fix-complete] | Heat transition reaches fix-completion. |
| `qokar` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → root/projection | Extract to root. |
| `chekal` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → active-solid-matrix | **THE CRYSTALLIZATION TOKEN.** chekal = volatile-essence → crystal. The DIRECT crystallization pathway from f87r. After all the cycling, the material crystallizes. |
| `daiin` | FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle | Verify crystal. |
| `dar-qokar` | FIX/STABILIZE → root/projection | **COMPOUND HYPHENATED TOKEN.** dar(fix-root) HYPHEN qokar(extract-root). Two operations LINKED by a hyphen. Fix at root, then extract at root — the hyphen means these are SEQUENTIAL but BONDED. Not fused (like daldaiin) but explicitly linked. |
| `odaiin=` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → daiin → [fix-complete] **[TERMINAL SEAL]** | **SECTION A CLOSES.** Heat-activated verification, sealed. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Heat activates → body completes → salt verifies → heat-transition completes → extract to root → **CRYSTALLIZE** → verify → **FIX-ROOT THEN EXTRACT-ROOT** → **HEAT-VERIFIED. SEALED.**

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — chekal in the stabilization context:**

The crystal forms in Section A's terminal paragraph. The stabilization page's first 7 paragraphs build up to crystallization — all that cycling, returning to source, fixing at root — produces a CRYSTAL. The crystal is the PROOF OF CONSISTENCY: only stable, consistently-cycled material forms a proper crystal. Impurities, inconsistencies, and variations prevent clean crystal formation.

Crystallization as QUALITY METRIC: if the material crystallizes cleanly, the stabilization cycling worked. If it doesn't, the material is inconsistent.

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — dar-qokar (hyphenated compound):**

This is the first HYPHENATED TOKEN in the pharmaceutical section. Previous compound tokens were fused (daldaiin, chodaiin) or sequential (dal.sal.dal). `dar-qokar` uses a HYPHEN to bind two operations: fix-root LINKED TO extract-root. The hyphen is a new punctuation mark — neither the space (`.`) between tokens nor the fusion of compound tokens, but an explicit LINKAGE.

The hyphen says: these two operations are BONDED but not identical. Fix the root, then extract from the root. The fixation and extraction happen at the same location (root) in immediate sequence. The hyphen couples them.

### Line 2 / P1.10: DOUBLED ykeey — Intensive Moist-Body Activation

**EVA:** `ykeey.ykeey.odal.shoky.okal.chody.okoaiin.dal.chdy.dal.daldy-`

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `ykeey` | MOIST-BODY → essence-active | Moist body at double-e essence, active. |
| `ykeey` | MOIST-BODY → essence-active | **IDENTICAL REPETITION.** The same token appears twice consecutively. In Voynichese, word repetition is noted as a significant statistical feature — some words appear up to five times in a row. Here: `ykeey.ykeey` doubles the moist-body double-e activation. INTENSIVE repetition. |
| `odal` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → fix-structure | Heat activates structural fixation. |
| `okoaiin` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → oaiin | Phase-shift to heat-completion-cycle. |
| `daldy` | FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix → [fixed/stabilized] | Fix structure, fixed. Redundant fixation. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** **MOIST-BODY DOUBLE-E → MOIST-BODY DOUBLE-E** → heat-fix-structure → heat-transition → phase-shift-structure → heat fixed → phase-complete → fix-structure → spirit-fixed → fix-structure → fix-structure-fixed.

**Critical observation — ykeey.ykeey:** Doubled identical token — the stabilization page REPEATS ITSELF. This is consistent cycling made literal: the same operation runs twice. The material's moist body is activated at double-e sensitivity, then activated AGAIN at the same sensitivity. The repetition is the stabilization: do it again to make sure.

Triple dal at paragraph end: `dal.chdy.dal.daldy` — fix-structure, spirit-fixed, fix-structure, fix-structure-fixed. FOUR consecutive structural fixation tokens. The paragraph LOCKS the structure with overwhelming redundancy.

---

### Line 3 / P1.11: SECTION B TERMINAL — The Compound Seal

**EVA:** `dcheoey.daiin.cthol.daiin.daldy.okeor.ytey.keor.chey.ty.ochyqokaiin=`

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `dcheoey` | FIX-VOLATILE → eoey | Fix volatile at essence-heat-essence-active. Dense compound fixation. |
| `cthol` | CONDUIT/BIND-ENERGY → fluid | Conduit to fluid. |
| `okeor` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eor | Phase-shift to essence-source/rotation. |
| `ytey` | MOIST-ENERGY → essence-active | Moist energy at essence, active. |
| `keor` | BODY/CONTAIN → eor | Body contains essence-rotation. |
| `ty` | ENERGY/TEMPORAL → y → [active/energized] | Temporal active. Ultra-compressed: 2 characters. |
| `ochyqokaiin=` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → volatile-active **[TERMINAL SEAL]** | **MASSIVE COMPOUND SEAL.** If read as morphemes: o(heat) + ch(volatile) + y(active) + qok(extract) + aiin(completion-cycle). Heat-volatile-active PLUS extract-completion-cycle, SEALED. Two complete operations fused into one terminal token. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Fix-volatile → verify → conduit-fluid → verify → fix-structure-fixed → phase-shift-source → moist-energy → body-source → volatile active → temporal active → **HEAT-VOLATILE-EXTRACT-COMPLETION. SEALED.**

**Critical observation — ochyqokaiin=:** This is the longest single terminal token in the pharmaceutical section: 12 characters encoding at minimum 5 morphemes. The seal FUSES heating, volatilizing, activating, extracting, and cycle-completing into ONE WORD. The stabilization page's mid-section closes by expressing the entire operational cycle in a single compound. Consistent cycling compressed to its essence.

## SECTION C: GATED EXTRACTION AND FINAL STABILIZATION (P1.12–P1.16)

### Line 4 / P1.12: PHASE-SHIFT DOMINANCE — Three okal Tokens

**EVA:** `kchol.qockhy.okaldy.okal.dal.chodar.okaiin.dalm-`

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `kchol` | BODY-VOLATILE → fluid | Body-volatile to fluid. |
| `okaldy` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → structure/matrix → [fixed/stabilized] | Phase-shift to fixed structure. |
| `okal` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → structure/matrix | Phase-shift to structure. |
| `chodar` | VOLATILE-HEAT → fix-root | Volatile heat reaches fix-root. |
| `okaiin` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → double-life-cycle | Phase-shift to completion. |
| `dalm` | FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix + m(vessel) | Fix-structure-vessel. Structure fixed into vessel. |

THREE ok- (phase-shift) tokens: `okaldy`, `okal`, `okaiin`. Each targets a different endpoint: fixed-structure, structure, completion. The phase-shift cascading from f89r2 continues — multiple state shifts in rapid succession.

`dalm` = fix-structure into vessel. The -m terminal (vessel) marks containment. The fixed structure enters a vessel. This is the first dalm in the pharmaceutical section — a new compound that fixes structure AND delivers to vessel simultaneously.

### Line 5 / P1.13: ANOMALOUS qkol AND COMPOUND FIXATION

| `daram` | FIX/STABILIZE → root/projection → [union/vessel] | Fix at root in vessel. |
| `dolchey` | FIX-FLUID → chey | Fix-fluid through volatile-essence-active. Compound: dol(fix-fluid) + chey(volatile-active). |
| `dalshdy` | FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix + sh + dy | **COMPOUND FIX-STRUCTURE-TRANSITION-FIX.** dal(fix-structure) + sh(transition) + dy(fix-active). The structure is fixed, transitioned, and fixed again in one compound. Triple operation in one token. |

**Critical observation — dalshdy:** This compound fuses THREE operations: fix-structure + transition + fix-active. The structure is locked, moved, and locked again. Like `daldaiin` fused fix with verify, `dalshdy` fuses fix-transition-fix. The stabilization page creates MULTI-FIX compounds that ensure the structure survives processing transitions.

Only 8 tokens — the SHORTEST paragraph on f89v1. Section C opens with compression.

13 tokens. Double identical extraction (`qokol.sheol.qokol`), vessel delivery, then double-e transmutation and salt. The stabilization page extracts, delivers, and validates in efficient sequence.

9 tokens. One transcription gap (edai*). The paragraph is unremarkable except for the gap — we flag it and move on without speculation.

**Paragraph-level reading:** Active conduit → source-fluid → active volatile → phase-shift volatile → **SALT AT ROOT-COMPLETE** → verify → phase-shift to structure → **VOLATILE-HEAT-FLUID-FIXED. SEALED.**

Only 8 tokens — matching P1.13 as the shortest paragraph. The stabilization page's final seal is BRIEF. No elaborate closure sequence, no convergent multi-system completion (like f89r2). Just: conduit, source, volatile, shift, salt-root, verify, shift, seal.

The brevity IS the point. After 16 paragraphs of consistent cycling, the close is routine. The material is stable. No drama needed.

| Compound fusions | dalshdy, ochyqokaiin, dar-qokar — multi-operation compounds |
| Crystallization as quality metric | chekal (P1.7) — crystal confirms consistent cycling |
| Patience markers | oiir (P1.9) — triple-i for maximum duration |

|---------|-----------|------------------|---------------|

| B (P1.9–P1.11) | 3 | 5 | 1.7 |
| C (P1.12–P1.16) | 5 | 4 | 0.8 |
| **Total** | **15** | **20** | **~1.3** |

LOWER verification density than f89r2 (2.3/para) or f88r (1.4/para). The stabilization page trusts its cycling. Consistent material needs less checking.

Three F-atom tokens on one page — the highest density in the pharmaceutical section. And two are in the OPENING PARAGRAPH. The stabilization page is F-atom RICH.

## THE STABILIZATION PAGE WITHIN THE FOLDOUT

The four foldout sub-pages form a progression:

| Sub-page | Function | F-atom | Key feature |
|----------|----------|--------|-------------|
| f89r1 | Minimal loop kernel | Absent | Fused operations (daldaiin) |
| f89r2 | Scale-up (universality) | Post-seal (qokeofy) | Non-Voynichese intrusion, triple daiin |
| **f89v1** | **Stabilization (consistency)** | **OPENING (sfal, ofcheol)** | **Single-stage cycling, crystallization as QC** |
| f89v2 | [next] | [tbd] | [tbd] |

The F-atom has migrated from ABSENT (f89r1) → POST-SEAL (f89r2) → OPENING (f89v1). The growth principle moves progressively earlier in the process as the foldout develops.

The foldout tells a manufacturing story:
1. **Define** the basic operation (f89r1)
2. **Prove** it works on everything (f89r2)
3. **Stabilize** it for consistent production (f89v1)
4. **[Final panel]** (f89v2)

What does the fourth panel add? The manufacturing sequence so far is: design → universality → consistency. The missing piece is either FINALIZATION (packaging for use), SPECIFICATION (exact parameters), or VALIDATION (testing the finished product).

**NEXT: F89V2 — Foldout Verso sub-page 2 (Final Panel)**

---
# VML PHARMACEUTICAL SECTION — FOLIO F89V2

## CLOSURE AND COMPATIBILITY: Robust Substitution
### Verso sub-page 2 of the Pharmaceutical Foldout — FINAL PANEL

---

## POSITION AND SIGNIFICANCE

F89v2 is the fourth and FINAL sub-page of the pharmaceutical foldout. The source calls it: "The closure + compatibility page: the process is robust to part substitution (inventory labels), but the program stays invariant."

This is the manufacturing story's conclusion. The foldout has progressed through: kernel definition (f89r1) → scale-up/universality (f89r2) → stabilization/consistency (f89v1) → **closure/compatibility** (f89v2). The final panel demonstrates that the standardized process can accept DIFFERENT INGREDIENTS while producing the same result. The machine is invariant; the inputs are variable.

---

## STRUCTURAL ARCHITECTURE

**Stage 1 (4 paragraphs):** P1.1 → P1.2 → P1.3 → P1.4
Terminal seal: `chkam=` (P1.4) — spirit-body-vessel.

**Stage 2 (9 paragraphs):** P2.10 → P2.11 → P2.12 → P2.13 → P2.5 → P2.6 → P2.7 → P2.8 → P2.9
Terminal seals:
- `daiin=` (P2.13) — standard verification seal at paragraph 4 of Stage 2
- `darails=` (P2.8) — fix-root-complete-fluid-salt, sealed

**LOST SYNCH MARKERS:** Two paragraphs carry the annotation `{lost synch}`:
- P2.10 ends with `{lost synch}`
- P2.9 ends with `{lost synch}`

These are TRANSCRIBER NOTES, not original manuscript features. `{lost synch}` means the transcriber lost synchronization between their transcription and the manuscript text — they weren't sure they were reading the lines in the right order, or that word breaks were being placed correctly. This is common on foldout pages where the text layout is non-standard and line-following becomes uncertain.

We flag these paragraphs as having REDUCED TRANSCRIPTION RELIABILITY. The tokens may be accurate individually, but their sequence and word-boundary placement are uncertain.

**Stage proportions:** Stage 1 is SHORT (4 paragraphs), Stage 2 is LONG (9 paragraphs). This inverts f89r2's pattern (where Stage 1 was 3 and Stage 3 was 7+2). The final panel front-loads a brief setup then runs an extended processing phase.

---

## STAGE 1: F-ATOM CYCLING AND SPIRIT-VESSEL CLOSURE (P1.1–P1.4)

### Line 1 / P1.1: THE F-ATOM CYCLE — qofoiin and ofaiin

**EVA:** `kosar.sheol.raiin.koiin.chtodaiin.pdin.choty.qofoiin.dy.qopdal.dair.ofaiin.ol.cfheol.dam-`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `kosar` | BODY/CONTAIN → osar | Body contains heat-salt-root. Dense opening. |
| `sheol` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → fluid | Essence to fluid. |
| `raiin` | ROTATION/SOURCE → double-life-cycle | Rotation completes full cycle. |
| `koiin` | BODY/CONTAIN → oiin | Body contains heat-double-i (patient). |
| `chtodaiin` | CHANNEL/SPIRIT → todaiin | **SPIRIT CHANNEL reaches temporal fixation-completion.** ch(spirit) + to(temporal) + daiin(fix-complete). The spirit dimension completes its temporal fixation cycle. |
| `pdin` | PROJECT/FLUID → din | Project fluid to fix-in. Compressed. |
| `choty` | VOLATILE-HEAT → ty | Volatile heat to temporal-active. |
| `qofoiin` | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → foiin | **F-ATOM TRANSMUTATION.** qo(transmute) + f(formative) + oiin(heat-double-i-patience). The F-atom is TRANSMUTED with patient heat. The growth principle undergoes fundamental transformation through prolonged heating. |
| `dy` | FIX/STABILIZE → y → [active/energized] | Fix active. |
| `qopdal` | TRANSMUTE-FLUID → fix-structure | Transmute fluid into fixed structure. |
| `dair` | FIX/STABILIZE → complete-root | Fix at root. |
| `ofaiin` | FORMATIVE-SOURCE/VEGETATIVE → double-life-cycle | **F-ATOM COMPLETES CYCLE.** of(formative) + aiin(double-life-cycle). The F-atom's own cycle reaches completion. Not the material's cycle — the GROWTH PRINCIPLE ITSELF has completed its transformative journey. |
| `ol` | FLUID-MEDIUM | Bare fluid. |
| `cfheol` | [cfh- cluster] | The cfh- element in fluid form. Still untranslatable, but consistently appearing alongside F-atom tokens. |
| `dam` | FIX/STABILIZE → union/vessel | Fix into vessel. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Body contains → essence-fluid → rotation-cycle → body-patience → **SPIRIT TEMPORALLY COMPLETES** → project fluid → volatile-heat-temporal → **F-ATOM TRANSMUTED WITH PATIENCE** → fix active → transmute fluid to structure → root-fix → **F-ATOM CYCLE COMPLETES** → fluid → [cfh- cluster] → fix to vessel.

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — F-atom cycling (qofoiin + ofaiin):**

Two F-atom tokens in the opening paragraph:
1. `qofoiin` = the F-atom is TRANSMUTED with patient heat (input — the growth principle undergoes transformation)
2. `ofaiin` = the F-atom's own cycle COMPLETES (output — the transformation finishes)

This is the F-atom's SIXTH mode and most sophisticated yet:

| Token | Folio | Mode | Description |
|-------|-------|------|-------------|
| `ofal` | f88r | Structural | F-atom structures material |
| `yfalaiin` | f88v | Receptive | Moisture receives F-atom |
| `qokeofy` | f89r2 | Extractive | F-atom within extraction |
| `sfal` | f89v1 | Delivery | Salt delivers to F-atom |
| `ofcheol` | f89v1 | Generative | F-atom produces volatile |
| `fcheody` | f89v1 | Operative | F-atom acts on volatile |
| **`qofoiin`** | **f89v2** | **Transformative** | **F-atom itself is transmuted** |
| **`ofaiin`** | **f89v2** | **Completive** | **F-atom's cycle finishes** |

The final panel adds the MOST ADVANCED F-atom operations: the growth principle itself is CHANGED (qofoiin) and COMPLETES its own cycle (ofaiin). The F-atom is no longer just acting on material — it's undergoing its own transformation. On the closure page, the biological principle matures.

**Critical observation — cfheol alongside F-atom:** The cfh- cluster appears AGAIN paired with F-atom tokens, as on f89v1 (P1.1). Across the foldout:
- f89v1 P1.1: `sfal...cfhey...ofcheol`
- f89v2 P1.1: `qofoiin...ofaiin...cfheol`

The cfh- element consistently appears in the same paragraph as F-atom tokens. It may be: (1) a reagent that activates the F-atom, (2) a product of F-atom processing, (3) the F-atom in a different state, or (4) coincidental co-occurrence. We cannot determine which without more data. But the pattern is consistent across both verso panels.

15 tokens — the densest paragraph in Stage 1. Two ckh- (valve) tokens, two ok- (phase-shift) tokens, two ot- (temporal drive) tokens. Everything runs in PAIRS. The closure page doubles its infrastructure: two valves, two phase-shifts, two temporal drives. Redundant gating for the final product.

**Token-by-token (selected highlights):**

| `qol` | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → l | Bare transmutation to fluid. |

15 tokens. The paragraph is VOLATILE-HEAVY: `chor`, `cheos`, `cheey`, `chody`, `cheor`, `chey`, `chody` — SEVEN ch- tokens in 15 (47%). Nearly half the paragraph is volatile operations. The closure page processes volatile essence at maximum intensity.

The `chs` token (spirit → salt) repeats from f89r2. The spirit-to-salt resolution is NOT a one-time event but a CONSISTENT ENDPOINT across the foldout's final panels.

### Line 4 / P1.4: STAGE 1 TERMINAL — Spirit-Body-Vessel

**EVA:** `dair.or.cheol.chom.qol.cheol.lor.cheo.daiin.chkam=`

**Token-by-token:**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `dair` | FIX/STABILIZE → complete-root | Root-fix opens terminal. |
| `or` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → r | Bare heat-rotation. 2 characters. |

| `chom` | VOLATILE-HEAT → m | Volatile heat to vessel. |

| `cheol` | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid | Volatile to fluid. Repeated. |

**Paragraph-level reading:** Root-fix → heat-rotate → volatile-fluid → volatile to vessel → transmute-fluid → volatile-fluid → layer at source → volatile-heat → verify → **SPIRIT ENTERS BODY IN VESSEL. SEALED.**

**Critical observation — chkam=:** The terminal token encodes the endpoint: spirit (ch-) enters body (k-) in vessel (am/m). Compare earlier terminals:
- f89r1: `chodaiin=` (volatile-heat verified)
- f89r2: `dair=` (root-fixed)
- f89v1: `choldy=` (volatile-heat-fluid fixed)
- **f89v2 Stage 1: `chkam=` (spirit-body-vessel)**

Each foldout sub-page seals a DIFFERENT DIMENSION:
1. Energy verified (f89r1)
2. Root fixed (f89r2)
3. Fluid state fixed (f89v1)
4. **Spirit embodied** (f89v2)

The final panel's Stage 1 seal doesn't check the chemistry — it EMBODIES THE SPIRIT. The spiritual dimension receives its final housing.

## STAGE 2: ROBUST PROCESSING AND REPEATED PATTERNS (P2.10–P2.9)

### Line 5 / P2.10: FIRST LOST SYNCH — Reduced Reliability

**EVA:** `qokor.okeor.otol.sheey.dal.daiin.dol.dair.chey.okaiin.shy.daiin-{lost synch}`

**Token-by-token (selected highlights):**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `qokor` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → source/rotation | Extract essence at source. |
| `okeor` | PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eor | Phase-shift to essence-rotation. |
| `otol` | TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → fluid | Temporal heat to fluid. |
| `sheey` | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → essence-active | Double-e transition. |
| `dol` | FIX-FLUID | Fix fluid. |
| `shy` | VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → y → [active/energized] | Vigorous active flow. |

**{lost synch} flag:** The transcriber lost synchronization at this paragraph's end. The tokens individually may be correct, but their sequence/boundaries may not precisely match the manuscript. We analyze with reduced confidence.

12 tokens of standard pharmaceutical vocabulary. Nothing anomalous in the token content — the `{lost synch}` issue is about READING ORDER, not about the tokens themselves being strange.

---

### Line 6 / P2.11: DEEP EXTRACTION — qokorar (Extended Root)

**EVA:** `odor.sheos.aiin.daikeody.qokorar.sheody.qoko.ltcheody.otal-`

**Token-by-token (selected highlights):**

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `odor` | HEAT/ACTIVATE → fix-source | Heat activates fixation at source. |
| `daikeody` | FIX/STABILIZE → aikeody | **Extended compound:** dai(fix-root) + ke(body-essence) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Fix-root through body-essence to heat-fixation, active. FOUR operational morphemes. |
| `qokorar` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → source/rotation → [rooted/projection] | **DOUBLE-ROOT EXTRACTION.** qok(extract) + or(heat-source) + ar(root). The extraction goes to source AND root — two levels of depth in one token. Compare standard `qokar` (extract to root). `qokorar` extracts to source-root-projection. DEEPER than root. |
| `qoko` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → o | **BARE EXTRACTION.** qok(extract) + o(heat). Extract to heat. Minimal. Like bare qo (transmute) — the foldout strips extraction to its stem. |
| `ltcheody` | LAYER/STRUCTURE → tcheody | Layer-structure routes through temporal-volatile-heat-fixation. |
| `otal` | TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → structure/matrix | Temporal heat drives to structure. |

**Critical observation — qokorar:** The extraction reaches BEYOND root depth. Previous deepest: `qokar` (extract to root). Now: `qokorar` = extract → source → root. Two depth-markers stacked. The closure page reaches the material's ULTIMATE FOUNDATION. If root is the deepest you can normally go, qokorar reaches the root OF the root.

**Critical observation — qoko:** Bare extraction stem, like the bare `qo` (transmute) on f89r1 and f89r2. The foldout consistently strips prefixed operations to their bare forms. `qoko` = *extract to heat*. An imperative: pull it out, heat it.

14 tokens. 2. `eeeyl` (f89r1): bare triple-e, intrinsic sensitivity
3. **`oeear` (f89v2): heat-activated triple-e at root**

Three triple-e modes:
1. **Applied by operation** (doleeey — fixation applies triple-e)
2. **Intrinsic to material** (eeeyl — material IS triple-e)
3. **Heat-activated at depth** (oeear — heat drives triple-e to root)

Mode 3 is the most aggressive: the heat doesn't just reach triple-e — it drives that sensitivity to ROOT DEPTH. Maximum sensitivity at maximum depth. The closure page reaches the material's absolute foundation at maximum resolution.

**Critical observation — skory (salt-body):** The sk- combination (salt + body) creates a SALT-INSIDE-BODY compound. Salt has been an external agent throughout — structuring, flowing, verifying FROM OUTSIDE. `skory` puts salt INSIDE the body. On the closure page, salt is no longer separate from the material. It's incorporated.

Between the `dar` tokens: salt punctuation, transcription gap, moist-body, phase-shifts, and structural fixes. Each `dar` locks the product after a different set of operations. Fix → [processing] → fix → [processing] → fix.

**Bare `am` terminal:** The paragraph ends with just `am` — vessel. Two characters. No prefix. The vessel as a DESTINATION, stated without qualification. *Into vessel.* The closure page's terseness at delivery points mirrors the foldout's overall tendency toward bare morphemes.

The sequence `dairy.sheos` appears TWICE in this paragraph:
1. `dairy.sheos.p*y`
2. `dairy.sheos.pkeoepoain`

Same two tokens, IDENTICAL, followed by different projection tokens. This is a TEMPLATE PATTERN: the same preparation (root-fix-active → essence-to-salt) is applied to DIFFERENT PROJECTIONS. The "robust substitution" described in the page title is VISIBLE HERE: the same processing sequence applied to interchangeable targets.

This is the foldout's thesis made explicit: the program (`dairy.sheos`) stays invariant while the parts (`p*y` vs `pkeoepoain`) are substituted. The closure page DEMONSTRATES ingredient substitution within a fixed protocol.

**Critical observation — pkeoepoain:** The 10-character compound with DOUBLE PROJECTION (p...p) and cycling essence-heat-essence. This is the most complex single compound in the pharmaceutical section. It encodes an entire processing sub-cycle in one token: project body-essence-heat-essence-project-heat-complete. A miniature recipe inside a word.

**{lost synch} flag:** The transcriber lost synchronization again. The repeated `dairy.sheos` pattern and the massive compound suggest the text at this point may be unusually dense or the line layout confusing. We treat with appropriate caution.

### Shared Foldout Patterns

- **Bare single-character tokens:** s (salt), r (rotation), y (active) — across all 4 panels
- **Anomalous q- prefix:** q without o- appears on f89r1, f89r2, f89v1 — foldout notation variant
- **dair terminal formula:** `dair.y.dair` or doubled dair appears on f89r1, f89r2, f89v2
- **Spirit-to-salt resolution:** `chs` on f89r2 and f89v2 — spirit becomes structuring principle
- **cfh-/cph- alongside F-atom:** f89v1 and f89v2 — mystery cluster co-occurs with growth principle
- **Lost synch only on f89v2:** Transcription difficulty concentrated on the final panel

## WHAT THE CLOSURE PAGE TELLS US

F89v2 completes the pharmaceutical foldout by demonstrating:

1. **F-atom maturation:** The growth principle undergoes its OWN transformation (qofoiin) and completes its OWN cycle (ofaiin). The biological dimension matures alongside the chemical.

2. **Robust substitution:** The `dairy.sheos` pattern repeats with different projection targets, proving the same protocol works with interchangeable ingredients.

3. **Comprehensive sealing:** `darails=` specifies four conditions (root, complete, fluid, salt) in one terminal. The finished product's state is fully declared.

4. **Spirit embodiment:** `chkam=` seals spirit into body within vessel. The medicine contains an active spiritual dimension with its own projection port (chypor).

5. **Triple-e at depth:** `oeear` drives triple-e sensitivity to root through heat activation. Maximum resolution at maximum depth.

6. **Salt incorporation:** `skory` puts salt INSIDE the body. Salt is no longer external infrastructure — it's part of the product's substance.

7. **Transmutation = delivery:** `qodam` fuses transformation with containment. The act of changing is the act of being received.

The foldout's complete message: **Define the core operation → prove it works on everything → stabilize it for consistency → demonstrate it accepts interchangeable parts.** This is a MANUFACTURING PROTOCOL for a universal pharmaceutical machine.

# VML PHARMACEUTICAL SECTION — FOLIOS F90R1, F90R2, F90V1, F90V2

## THE JAR/CONTAINER RECIPE: From Universal Machine to Specific Application
### First Post-Foldout Recipe Group

---

## POSITION AND SIGNIFICANCE

The f90 group (4 sub-pages on one physical folio) is the FIRST RECIPE AFTER THE FOLDOUT. Where f87r–f88v established pharmaceutical infrastructure and f89r1–f89v2 defined the universal manufacturing protocol, f90 APPLIES that protocol to a specific product.

The source descriptions tell the story:
- **f90r1:** "Minor Cycle — Circulate → Clarify → Stabilize" — the minimal complete recipe
- **f90r2:** "Extraction Complement — Time + Repetition" — the temporal dimension
- **f90v1:** "Polish Panel — Reproducible Identity" — ensuring identical output
- **f90v2:** "Process Hygiene — Purity as Recursion" — purity through iteration

Visual description: "Jar illustrations showing actual apparatus — vessels, tubes, connections." The illustrations depict PHYSICAL EQUIPMENT for the first time in the pharmaceutical section.

This is the foldout's universal machine INSTANTIATED: specific vessels, specific timings, specific clarification steps. Theory becomes practice.

---

## STRUCTURAL ARCHITECTURE

### A New Paragraph Format

All four f90 sub-pages use UNNUMBERED PARAGRAPHS (P.1, P.2... not P1.1, P2.5 etc.). This is a departure from the staged architecture of f87r–f89v2. The jar recipes don't have formal stages — they have SEQUENTIAL STEPS in a single continuous process.

| Sub-page | Paragraphs | Terminal | Description |
|----------|-----------|----------|-------------|
| f90r1 | 9 (P.1–P.9) | `okam=` | Phase-shift to vessel. SEALED. |
| f90r2 | 5 (P.1–P.5) | `daiin=` | Standard verification. SEALED. |
| f90v1 | 11 (P.1–P.11) | `daiin=` (P.6, P.11) | Two seals — mid and terminal. |
| f90v2 | 8 (P.1–P.8) | `okeey=` (P.4), `daiin=` (P.8) | Two seals — mid and terminal. |

**Total: 33 paragraphs across 4 sub-pages.** Compare the foldout's 56+ paragraphs. The jar recipe is MORE COMPACT — roughly 60% the size of the foldout. Theory is verbose; practice is lean.

---

## F90R1: THE MINOR CYCLE — Circulate → Clarify → Stabilize

### Opening: poleeol — Project Double-E Fluid

**EVA P.1:** `poleeol.qokeol.qokchod.choly.cthom-`

| Token | Translation | What It Does |
|-------|------------|-------------|
| `poleeol` | PROJECT/FLUID → fluid (with double-e) | **DOUBLE-E PROJECTION.** pol(project-fluid) + ee(double-e sensitivity) + ol(fluid). The recipe opens by projecting fluid at ELEVATED SENSITIVITY. The very first operation of the first practical recipe starts at double-e. The foldout achieved sensitivity through cycles; the jar recipe STARTS with it. |
| `qokeol` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → eol | Extract to fluid. |
| `qokchod` | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → chod | Extract volatile-heat-fixation. |
| `choly` | VOLATILE-HEAT → ly | Volatile heat to fluid-active. |
| `cthom` | CONDUIT/BIND-ENERGY → vessel | **CONDUIT TO VESSEL.** Fifth token delivers to vessel. The opening paragraph goes: project → extract → extract → heat → DELIVER. Five steps from start to vessel. |

**Critical observation — 5 tokens only:** The shortest opening paragraph in the pharmaceutical section, MATCHING f89r1's 5-token opener. The jar recipe's first step is AS COMPRESSED as the foldout kernel. Theory and practice share the same opening density.

### P.2–P.3: Temporal Grounding and Structural Assembly

**EVA P.3:** `dair.shkeea.s.sary.okar.ykarshy.lkaldy-`

| Token | Translation | What It Does |

## THE F90 GROUP AS A UNIT

### Sensitivity Escalation Across Four Sub-Pages

| Sub-page | Maximum sensitivity | Token | Context |
|----------|-------------------|-------|---------|
| f90r1 | Double-e | poleeol, ykeey | Opening projection, processing |
| f90r2 | Triple-e | qokeear | Extraction to root |
| f90v1 | Triple-e | oleees, keeey, okeeey, keeeol | Medium, body, operation, product |
| f90v2 | Double-e + mega-compound | oteeysaiin | Compressed processing |

**f90v1 is the TRIPLE-E PAGE.** Four different triple-e tokens — as medium, as body, as operation, as product. The polish panel works ENTIRELY at maximum sensitivity.

### F-Atom / cfh- / cph- Distribution

| Sub-page | F-atom tokens | cfh-/cph- tokens | Co-occurrence |
|----------|--------------|-----------------|---------------|
| f90r1 | qofchol, chofy | chocfhor | YES — same paragraph (P.4) |
| f90r2 | — | — | Absent |
| f90v1 | — | cfheos (P.3) | cfh- alone |
| f90v2 | ofchedal | cphdachy, qocfhey | YES — same paragraph (P.1) |

F-atom and cfh-/cph- continue to CO-OCCUR on the pages where both appear. The correlation is strengthening.

### Verification Density

| Sub-page | Paragraphs | daiin/saiin count | Per paragraph |
|----------|-----------|------------------|---------------|
| f90r1 | 9 | 1 (P.4: chodaiin) | 0.11 |
| f90r2 | 5 | 6 | 1.2 |
| f90v1 | 11 | 6 | 0.55 |
| f90v2 | 8 | 4 | 0.5 |
| **Total** | **33** | **17** | **~0.5** |

DRAMATICALLY LOWER than the foldout (~2.0/para) or main recipe pages (~1.4/para). The jar recipes TRUST the material. The foldout verified intensively to establish reliability; the jar recipes inherit that reliability and verify minimally.

### What the Jar Recipes Tell Us

The f90 group translates the foldout's universal machine into practice:

1. **Compression:** 33 paragraphs vs. 56+ on the foldout. 3-5 token terminals vs. elaborate closures. The recipe is leaner than the theory.

2. **Starting at elevated sensitivity:** `poleeol` opens at double-e. The recipe doesn't build up to sensitivity — it begins there.

3. **Triple-e as tool and product:** `oleees` (medium), `keeey`/`keeeol` (body/product), `okeeey` (operation). Triple-e is both the polishing medium AND the polished product.

4. **Minimal verification:** ~0.5 daiin/paragraph vs. 2.0 on the foldout. Trust built by the foldout carries forward.

5. **Purity through cascading transitions:** Five she- tokens in one paragraph. Multiple state changes IS purification.

6. **Bare morphemes as imperatives:** s, r, sh — the jar recipe's operators issue single-character commands.

7. **F-atom within heat:** `chofy` puts the growth principle inside the volatile heat. The biological principle travels with the energy.

---

**F90 GROUP COMPLETE.**

**NEXT: F93R — Stable Herb Recipe: Oscillation Extraction (Plant-Recipe Hybrid)**

Note: The manuscript jumps from f90v2 to f93r — folios f91 and f92 either don't exist, are blank, or belong to a different section. The source material provides f93r as the next pharmaceutical folio.
