## FOLIO F93R — STABLE HERB RECIPE: OSCILLATION EXTRACTION

**Position:** First Plant-Recipe Hybrid. BRIDGE between Pharmaceutical section proper (f87r-f90v2) and herbal source material. Plant illustration paired directly with processing protocol — the raw material is SHOWN alongside its instructions.

**Structure:** 31 paragraphs (P.1-P.32, P.26 absent). ~140 tokens total. UNNUMBERED paragraphs (continuous recipe, not formal stages).

**Visual:** Plant illustration alongside recipe text. This is the pharmaceutical section's first explicit connection to its herbal inputs.

### Structural Profile

The folio divides into three density zones:

| Zone | Paragraphs | Tokens/para | Character |
|------|-----------|-------------|-----------|
| Opening (Setup) | P.1-P.3 | 9-10 | Dense compound specification |
| Extraction | P.4-P.9 | 3-7 | Active processing |
| Oscillation/Refinement | P.10-P.32 | 3-5 | Rapid alternating cycles |

The progression from DENSE to COMPRESSED mirrors the pharmaceutical process itself: elaborate setup → active work → rapid cycling until stable.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

**P.1 (9 tokens): OPENING — The Complete Setup**
`kodshol.otolsheeos.octhodaly.opalepam.oepch.ksheey.qotodain.s.oar-`

Token-by-token:
- `kodshol` = k(body) + od(heat-fix) + shol(transition-fluid). Body heat-fixed in transitional fluid. The HERB is placed into the processing medium. First word names the physical setup: plant body suspended in heated fluid.
- `otolsheeos` = o(heat) + tol(temporal-fluid) + shee(transition-essence) + os(heat-salt). MEGA-COMPOUND (10 characters). Temporal fluid undergoing essence-transition into heated salt. The processing medium is specified in ONE word — a complete description of the bath the herb sits in.
- `octhodaly` = o(heat) + cthod(conduit-heat-fix) + al(structure) + y(active). Heat drives conduit-fixed structuring. The apparatus — heated tubes or channels — is established.
- `opalepam` = op(project) + al(structure) + ep(essence-project) + am(vessel). Structural projection into vessel. The product endpoint is NAMED at the outset: project structured essence into storage vessel. The recipe knows where it's going before it starts.
- `oepch` = o(heat) + e(essence) + p(project) + ch(volatile). Heat-essence projected into volatile. The extraction mechanism: heat drives essence outward into volatile medium.
- `ksheey` = k(body) + sh(transition) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Body in transition at double-e sensitivity. The herb body is actively transitioning — already changing — and the recipe notes this at ELEVATED SENSITIVITY (double-e). Compare f90r1 which opened at double-e with `poleeol`. The herb recipe also starts at double-e.
- `qotodain` = qo(transmute) + to(temporal-heat) + dain(fix-complete). Transmute through temporal heat to fixed completion. The first qo- operation: time-and-heat transmutation until done.
- `s` = BARE SALT. Single-character imperative. Add salt / apply salt principle. Same bare-morpheme pattern as jar recipes.
- `oar` = o(heat) + ar(root). Heat to root. Drive heat to the deepest level.

**Reading:** Place herb body in heated transitional fluid. Establish heated conduit infrastructure. Project structured essence toward vessel. Heat-drive essence into volatile medium. Body transitions at double-e. Transmute through patient heat until fixed. Salt. Heat to root.

NINE tokens that set up the ENTIRE recipe in one paragraph. Compare f89r1's 5-token opener (kernel definition) or f90r1's 5-token opener (jar recipe). The herb recipe needs more tokens because it's specifying BOTH the material (the herb) AND the process — it's doing double duty as herbal description and pharmaceutical instruction.

**P.2 (10 tokens): SUPPLEMENTARY SETUP — Apparatus and Routing**
`ycham.s.chol.chotoj.cthodar.sheo*.s.oteodal.r-opchoshy.ckhashol-`

- `ycham` = y(moist/receptive) + ch(volatile) + am(vessel). Moist volatile received in vessel. The receiving vessel is prepared — wet, volatile-compatible.
- `s` = BARE SALT (second occurrence in two paragraphs).
- `chol` = ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Volatile fluid. The working medium.
- `chotoj` = cho(volatile-heat) + to(temporal) + j(terminal modifier). Volatile heat under temporal control with terminal marking. Patient heated volatile.
- `cthodar` = cth(conduit-energy) + od(heat-fix) + ar(root). Conduit energy heat-fixes to root. The tube system drives fixation deep.
- `sheo*` = she(transition-essence) + o(heat) + *(illegible). Essence transitions through heat — remainder illegible (EVA asterisk = transcriber couldn't read glyph).
- `s` = BARE SALT (third occurrence).
- `oteodal` = ot(temporal-heat) + e(essence) + od(heat-fix) + al(structure). Temporal heat drives essence fixation into structure. Time + heat fixes essence into physical form.
- `r-opchoshy` = r(source/root) + op(project) + cho(volatile-heat) + shy(flow-active). Source projects volatile heat in active flow. HYPHENATED COMPOUND — the source actively projects heated volatile flow.
- `ckhashol` = ckh(valve) + a + shol(transition-fluid). Valve transitions fluid. The routing hardware — a valve or gate controls how the transitional fluid moves.

**Reading:** Prepare moist volatile vessel. Salt. Volatile fluid under patient heat. Conduit fixes to root depth. Essence transitions through heat. Salt. Time-heat fixes essence to structure. Source projects volatile flow. Valve routes transitional fluid.

THREE bare `s` tokens across P.1-P.2 = salt punctuation. The salt principle is being INJECTED at multiple points during setup. Not a single salt stage — salt is distributed throughout initialization. This is new. On the foldout, salt appears as endpoints (saiin completions). Here salt is a TOOL being applied repeatedly.

**P.3 (9 tokens): FIXATION MANIFESTO**
`dsho.dal.dalody.ytchchy.dam.chody.dal.ol-schodchy.qoteed-`

- `dsho` = d(fix) + sh(transition) + o(heat). Fix the transition with heat. STOP the herb from changing further — pin it in its current state.
- `dal` = d(fix) + al(structure). Fix structure. #1.
- `dalody` = d(fix) + al(structure) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Fix structure through active heat-fixation. Expanded dal.
- `ytchchy` = y(moist) + tch(energy-volatile) + ch(volatile) + y(active). Moist energy-volatile in active volatile state. The material is still wet and energetically volatile — this is what's BEING fixed.
- `dam` = d(fix) + am(vessel). Fix into vessel. Contain the fixation.
- `chody` = cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat fixed. The volatile component is LOCKED.
- `dal` = d(fix) + al(structure). Fix structure. #2.
- `ol-schodchy` = ol(fluid) + scho(salt-volatile-heat) + d(fix) + ch(volatile) + y(active). HYPHENATED: fluid medium contains salt-volatile-heat fixation of active volatile. Complex compound describing the fluid bath where fixation occurs.
- `qoteed` = qo(transmute) + tee(temporal-double-e) + d(fix). Transmute through temporal double-e to fixation. The transmutation is sensitive (double-e) and temporally controlled.

**Reading:** Fix the transition. Fix structure. Fix structure through active heat. The material is still moist and volatile — fix it into vessel. Lock the volatile heat. Fix structure again. The fluid bath carries salt-volatile-heat fixation. Transmute at double-e sensitivity to fixation.

d-PREFIX DENSITY: 7 d-tokens in 9 positions = 78%. This is the most d-heavy paragraph in the entire pharmaceutical section. P.3 is a FIXATION MANIFESTO — it says "fix" seven different ways. Compare f89v2's triple-dar paragraph (38% d-density). This DOUBLES it.

THREE `dal` tokens (two explicit, one expanded as dalody). The structural matrix is being fixed from three directions simultaneously — same triple-fix pattern as the foldout but compressed into a single paragraph.

---

**P.4 (6 tokens): SALT-TRANSITION EXTRACTION**
`sol.shotol.qokchddal.shody.chotol.s-chodain-`

- `sol` = s(salt) + ol(fluid). Salt fluid. The extraction medium.
- `shotol` = sh(transition) + o(heat) + tol(temporal-fluid). Transition heat into temporal fluid.
- `qokchddal` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + dd(double-fix) + al(structure). EXTRACT body volatile through DOUBLE FIXATION into structure. The `dd` — double d — is rare. DOUBLE FIXATION within one extraction step. The body's volatile component is extracted and simultaneously fixed twice.
- `shody` = sh(transition) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Active heat-fixed transition.
- `chotol` = cho(volatile-heat) + tol(temporal-fluid). Volatile heat in temporal fluid.
- `s-chodain` = s(salt) + cho(volatile-heat) + dain(fix-complete). HYPHENATED: salt meets volatile-heat-fixation-completion. Salt is the boundary between volatile heat and fixed completion.

`qokchddal` — the DOUBLE-d extraction. This token says: extract the body's volatile fraction and FIX IT TWICE into structural matrix. One fixation for the volatile component, one for the structural target. The recipe insists on bilateral fixation — what leaves AND what receives must both be fixed.

**P.5 (6 tokens): VALVE-CONTROLLED EXTRACTION TO ROOT**
`ol.chody.ckhol.diiird.qokol.otodar-chodain-`

- `ol` = FLUID-MEDIUM. Working fluid.
- `chody` = cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat fixed.
- `ckhol` = ckh(valve) + ol(fluid). Valve controls fluid. The valve is open for fluid passage.
- `diiird` = d(fix) + iii(triple-i) + r(root) + d(fix). FIX-TRIPLE-I-ROOT-FIX. The `iii` — TRIPLE-I — is extremely rare. If `eee` represents triple-e sensitivity, `iii` may represent triple-i (triple verification/completion cycle, since `i` appears in `aiin` completion tokens). FIX-SANDWICH around triple-i-root: fixation brackets an intensely verified root extraction. This token is ANOMALOUS and merits flagging — `diiird` has no clear parallel elsewhere in the pharmaceutical section.
- `qokol` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ol(fluid). Extract body into fluid. Standard extraction.
- `otodar-chodain` = ot(temporal-heat) + od(heat-fix) + ar(root) + cho(volatile-heat) + dain(fix-complete). HYPHENATED MEGA-COMPOUND: temporal heat fixes to root, volatile heat completes fixation. Time-driven root-fixation meets volatile heat fixation. Two fixation pathways MERGED at the hyphen.

`diiird` — FLAG THIS. Triple-i between double-d. No parallel in the foldout or jar recipes. If the triple-e scale (ee = double sensitivity, eee = maximum sensitivity) has a parallel in triple-i, this would be maximum verification/completion intensity bracketed by fixation. The herb recipe deploys a morphological pattern the foldout never needed.

**P.6 (7 tokens): ENERGY CYCLING WITH BARE ELEMENTS**
`tar.otor.s.cho.s.chol.sheoeer-`

- `tar` = t(energy/temporal) + ar(root). Temporal energy to root.
- `otor` = ot(temporal-heat) + or(source/rotation). Temporal heat cycles from source.
- `s` = BARE SALT #4.
- `cho` = BARE VOLATILE-HEAT. Two characters. Just: volatile heat. Imperative.
- `s` = BARE SALT #5.
- `chol` = ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Volatile fluid.
- `sheoeer` = she(transition-essence) + o(heat) + ee(double-e) + r(root). Transition-essence through heat at double-e to root. Double-e essence transition reaches root depth.

TWO more bare `s` tokens AND a bare `cho`. Three bare morphemes in one paragraph. Total bare `s` count on f93r so far: FIVE in six paragraphs. The herb recipe uses salt as PUNCTUATION between operations — not as a destination but as a recurring intervention. This is consistent with spagyric processing where salt is repeatedly applied during herb extraction.

**P.7 (5 tokens): DUAL TRANSITION WITH FIXATION**
`shor.shol.ody.cheodoin.s-`

- `shor` = sh(transition) + or(source/rotation). Transition from source.
- `shol` = sh(transition) + ol(fluid). Transition to fluid.
- `ody` = o(heat) + dy(fixed). Heat fixed.
- `cheodoin` = che(volatile-essence) + od(heat-fix) + oin(heat-complete). Volatile essence heat-fixed to completion.
- `s` = BARE SALT #6.

`shor.shol` — OSCILLATION PAIR. Transition FROM source, transition TO fluid. This is the OSCILLATION the recipe title promises: work (extract from source) ↔ settle (deposit into fluid). Back and forth. The oscillation is encoded as paired sh- tokens with complementary endpoints (or = source, ol = fluid).

**P.8 (3 tokens): VERIFICATION CHECKPOINT**
`lo*sheeody.chodaiin.odar-`

- `lo*sheeody` = l(layer/structure) + o(heat) + *(illegible) + shee(transition-essence-double-e) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Layered heat with essence transition at double-e, actively heat-fixed. Complex layered processing at elevated sensitivity. The asterisk marks an illegible glyph.
- `chodaiin` = cho(volatile-heat) + daiin(verification-complete). Volatile heat VERIFIED and complete. First full daiin verification on the page.
- `odar` = o(heat) + d(fix) + ar(root). Heat-fix to root.

P.8 is the first VERIFICATION CHECKPOINT. Eight paragraphs of setup and extraction before the first daiin. Compare f90r1 which had only ONE daiin in 9 paragraphs. The herb recipe verifies at a similar rate — the material is being worked, not inspected.

**P.9 (3 tokens): PHASE-SHIFT THROUGH CONDUIT**
`shodaj.okcheody.cthocthol-`

- `shodaj` = sh(transition) + od(heat-fix) + aj(terminal). Transition heat-fixed with terminal marking. A transition ENDS.
- `okcheody` = ok(phase-shift) + che(volatile-essence) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Phase-shift volatile essence through active heat-fixation. The volatile fraction changes state.
- `cthocthol` = ctho(conduit-heat) + cthol(conduit-fluid). DOUBLED CONDUIT: conduit-heat meets conduit-fluid. Two conduit systems merge. The heated conduit and the fluid conduit JOIN — a T-junction or mixer in the apparatus.

`cthocthol` — DOUBLED ctho-. The apparatus has two conduit branches that converge. This is physical plumbing described in VML: two pipes meet.

---

**P.10-P.32: THE OSCILLATION ZONE**

From P.10 onward, paragraphs compress to 3-5 tokens. The recipe enters its CYCLING PHASE — rapid alternations between extraction, transition, fixation, and verification. Each paragraph is one beat in an oscillating rhythm.

**P.10 (5 tokens):** `yeeos.chey.keol.eteol.cthody-`
Moist essence-energy → volatile essence active → body fluid → [eteol] → conduit fixed active. Receptive material meets volatile essence, body enters fluid, driven through conduit.

**P.11 (5 tokens):** `okeol.oteol.sodam.sheoal.sal-`
Phase-shift fluid → temporal-heat fluid → SALT-FIX-VESSEL → transition-essence-structure → SALT-STRUCTURE.
TWO salt tokens (sodam, sal). Salt FIXES into vessel and salt STRUCTURES. The oscillation hits a salt station — material is salted to stabilize before next cycle.

**P.12 (4 tokens):** `qokor.shey.okcheor.sheodom-`
EXTRACT from source → transition essence active → PHASE-SHIFT volatile to source → transition-essence to vessel.
The OSCILLATION visible: extract (qokor) then transition (shey) then phase-shift back (okcheor) then transition to vessel (sheodom). One complete work↔settle cycle in four tokens.

**P.13 (3 tokens):** `shodaiin.qotchy.kcholr-`
TRANSITION VERIFIED → transmute volatile active → body-volatile-fluid.
Second daiin. The transition is checked. Then transmutation continues.

**P.14 (4 tokens):** `ychey.ckhor.otcheod.chr-`
Moist volatile essence → VALVE source → temporal volatile fixation → SPIRIT-ROOT.
The valve controls flow from the source. `chr` = bare spirit-to-root. SPIRIT reaches root depth. Two-character token — minimal, imperative.

**P.15 (4 tokens):** `*chol.shodal.dol.cheodam-`
[illegible]-volatile-fluid → TRANSITION-FIX-STRUCTURE → FIX-FLUID → volatile-essence-fix-vessel.
Three fix operations (shodal, dol, cheodam contains dam). Heavy fixation paragraph — the oscillation pauses to FIX results.

**P.16 (3 tokens):** `choshy.qokar.chckhr-`
Volatile-heat flow → EXTRACT to root → spirit-valve-root.
Extraction reaches root depth through spirit channel and valve. `chckhr` = ch + ckh + r: spirit-valve-root. Three operational elements compressed into one token.

**P.17 (3 tokens):** `tcheo.l.cholchecthody-`
Energy-volatile-essence → BARE l (layer/structure) → volatile-spirit-conduit-fixed.
The bare `l` — single character, just "structure/layer." Imperative: LAYER IT. Then a massive compound `cholchecthody` (14 characters) names the result: volatile-spirit-conduit in fixed state. One of the longest tokens in the pharmaceutical section.

**P.18 (3 tokens):** `olkeer.shodaiin.shody-`
FLUID at double-e → TRANSITION VERIFIED COMPLETE → transition heat-fixed.
`olkeer` = ol(fluid) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + r(root). Fluid body at double-e sensitivity reaching root. Third daiin verification. Followed by `shody` — transition fixed. The oscillation reaches a CHECKPOINT: verified, fixed.

**P.19 (4 tokens):** `tchor.shol.s.sheoky-`
Energy-volatile-source → transition-fluid → BARE SALT #7 → transition-essence-phase-active.
Another bare salt punctuating between transition states.

**P.20 (3 tokens):** `ychockhy.cthol.osos-`
Moist-volatile-valve-active → conduit-fluid → HEAT-SALT-HEAT-SALT.
`osos` = o(heat) + s(salt) + o(heat) + s(salt). OSCILLATING HEAT-SALT. Heat, salt, heat, salt — the word ITSELF oscillates between two principles. This is the oscillation title made LITERAL in a single token. The recipe names what it's doing.

**P.21 (4 tokens):** `dol.shol.daiin.shcthy-`
FIX-FLUID → transition-fluid → VERIFIED → vigorous-conduit-active.
Fourth daiin. Fix, transition, verify, flow vigorously. A complete mini-cycle.

**P.22 (4 tokens):** `kchor.cthy.chakal.daiin-`
Body-volatile-source → conduit-active → SPIRIT-CRYSTAL-STRUCTURE → VERIFIED.
`chakal` = ch(spirit/volatile) + ak(crystal/solid) + al(structure). SPIRIT CRYSTALLIZES INTO STRUCTURE. The volatile/spirit component has formed crystals. This is CRYSTALLIZATION reported as achieved. Fifth daiin — verification confirms the crystal formation.

Compare f90r1's `lkaldy` (layer-crystal-fixed) which was the first crystallization on the jar recipe page. Here `chakal` is spirit-crystal-structure — the volatile has solidified. Different pathway (spirit → crystal vs. layer → crystal) but same endpoint.

**P.23 (4 tokens):** `oain.okor.shody.teols-`
Heat-complete → phase-shift-source → transition-fixed → temporal-fluid-salt.
Heat cycle finishes, phase shifts from source, transition stabilizes, temporal fluid reaches salt.

**P.24 (3 tokens):** `ychocthy.chotey.teeyr-`
Moist-volatile-conduit-active → volatile-heat-temporal-active → TEMPORAL-DOUBLE-E-ACTIVE-ROOT.
`teeyr` = t(temporal/energy) + ee(double-e) + y(active) + r(root). Temporal process at double-e sensitivity actively reaching root. The time-controlled process is at elevated sensitivity and reaching maximum depth.

**P.25 (3 tokens):** `yoaiin.chotar.ch**-`
Receptive-heat-completion → volatile-heat-temporal-root → spirit-[illegible].
`yoaiin` = y(receptive) + o(heat) + aiin(completion). Receptive heat completes. The material ACCEPTS the heat and finishes its cycle. Two illegible characters at end (EVA asterisks).

**P.27 (4 tokens):** `qokor.cheo.los.ckhody-`
EXTRACT-source → volatile-essence-heat → layer-salt → valve-fixed-active.
Second qokor on the page (first was P.12). Extraction returns — the oscillation cycles BACK to extraction mode. `los` = l(layer) + o(heat) + s(salt). Layered, heated, salted.

**P.28 (4 tokens):** `ychor.odol.chodain.s-`
Moist-volatile-source → heat-fix-fluid → volatile-heat-fix-complete → BARE SALT #8.
More fixation. Eighth bare salt.

**P.29 (4 tokens):** `dain.etcho.ctho.cthoey-`
FIX-COMPLETE → [etcho] → conduit-heat → conduit-heat-essence-active.
`dain` opens the paragraph — FIX COMPLETE. Then `etcho` (unusual — e-prefix on tcho cluster; possibly essence-energy-volatile-heat). Two `ctho-` tokens: the conduit system processes the fixed material.

**P.30 (3 tokens):** `shodaiin.qokchy.cthol-`
TRANSITION VERIFIED → EXTRACT volatile-active → conduit-fluid.
Sixth daiin. Transition verified, then extraction continues, through conduit to fluid. The oscillation is STILL RUNNING at paragraph 30. This recipe cycles a LONG TIME.

**P.31 (4 tokens):** `ol.chal.cthol.olchod-`
FLUID → spirit-structure → conduit-fluid → fluid-volatile-heat-fix.
All fluid/conduit tokens. The product is moving through liquid infrastructure. `chal` = ch(spirit) + al(structure). Spirit has structured — the volatile fraction is organized.

**P.32 (3 tokens): TERMINAL SEAL**
`dol.chokal.schos=`

- `dol` = d(fix) + ol(fluid). FIX FLUID. Final fixation of the liquid product.
- `chokal` = cho(volatile-heat) + k(body) + al(structure). Volatile heat contained in bodily structure. The volatile component is EMBODIED — captured in physical form.
- `schos=` = s(salt) + cho(volatile-heat) + s(salt) = SALT-VOLATILE-SALT. SEALED.

TERMINAL SEAL: `schos=` — the volatile heat is SANDWICHED between two salt layers. Salt brackets volatile. The structuring principle (salt) contains the active principle (volatile heat) on both sides. Compare f89v2's `darails=` (four conditions) or f89r1's `chodaiin=` (energy verified). This terminal names a PHYSICAL STRUCTURE: salt | volatile-heat | salt. A salt-volatile-salt sandwich.

This is a real pharmaceutical structure — a preparation where the active volatile component is preserved between salt layers to prevent degradation. The seal describes the PRODUCT: a salt-encapsulated volatile herbal extract.

---

### PATTERN ANALYSIS

#### Oscillation Structure

The oscillation is visible at multiple scales:

1. **Token level:** `osos` (P.20) = heat-salt-heat-salt. Literal oscillation within one word.
2. **Paragraph level:** `shor.shol` (P.7) = transition-from-source, transition-to-fluid. One oscillation beat per paragraph.
3. **Section level:** P.12 contains a complete extraction→transition→phase-shift→settle cycle in 4 tokens. P.27 repeats the extraction (second `qokor`), showing the cycle RETURNING.

The oscillation is the recipe's central operation: repeatedly extract from the herb, settle into fluid, extract again, settle again, until the volatile fraction is fully transferred and stabilized.

#### Verification Density

| Token | Paragraph | Position |
|-------|----------|----------|
| chodaiin | P.8 | First verification — after 8 para setup |
| shodaiin | P.13 | Transition verified |
| shodaiin | P.18 | Transition verified + fixed |
| daiin | P.21 | Standalone verification |
| daiin | P.22 | Crystal formation verified |
| shodaiin | P.30 | Late transition verified |

**6 daiin/saiin in 31 paragraphs = 0.19/para.** LOWEST verification density in the pharmaceutical section. Lower than even the jar recipes (0.5/para). The herb recipe trusts its oscillation process — it barely checks. The foldout's ~2.0/para verification intensity exists so that HERE, at the practical herb recipe level, almost no verification is needed.

#### d-Prefix (Fixation) Density

Fixation tokens appear in: P.1 (qotodain), P.3 (dsho, dal, dalody, dam, dal = 5 tokens), P.4 (qokchddal, s-chodain), P.5 (diiird, otodar-chodain), P.7 (cheodoin), P.8 (chodaiin, odar), P.11 (sodam), P.15 (shodal, dol, cheodam), P.21 (dol, daiin), P.22 (daiin), P.28 (odol, chodain), P.29 (dain), P.32 (dol).

~25 d-prefix tokens across 31 paragraphs. BUT they cluster: P.3 alone has 5 (the fixation manifesto), P.4-P.5 have 4 (the extraction-fixation zone). Fixation is FRONT-LOADED — the recipe fixes heavily at the start, then relies on the oscillation to maintain stability.

#### Bare Morphemes

| Morpheme | Count | Paragraphs |
|----------|-------|-----------|
| `s` (salt) | 8 | P.1, P.2(×2), P.6(×2), P.7, P.19, P.28 |
| `cho` (volatile-heat) | 1 | P.6 |
| `l` (layer/structure) | 1 | P.17 |
| `ch` (spirit) | 1 | P.25 |
| `r` (source) | — | (appears in P.2 hyphenated compound) |

EIGHT bare `s` tokens. The herb recipe uses salt as its primary intervention tool — a punctuation mark between operations. Every few paragraphs: SALT. This is consistent with spagyric herb processing where salt is repeatedly applied to extract, preserve, and structure the plant material.

#### sh- (Transition) Density

Transition tokens appear in nearly every paragraph: shodaiin (×3), shol (×5), shor (×2), shody (×3), sheo- (×5), dsho, shotol, sheoeer, shcthy, sheoky... 

**~25 sh- tokens across 31 paragraphs ≈ 0.8 per paragraph.** The herb recipe is TRANSITION-DOMINATED. Compare the foldout which was verification-dominated (daiin-heavy) and the jar recipes which were extraction-dominated (qo-heavy). The herb recipe's character is defined by constant transition — the material is always MOVING between states, never resting. This IS the oscillation: perpetual transition.

#### F-Atom / cfh- / cph- Clusters

**ABSENT.** No f-atom tokens, no cfh- or cph- clusters appear on f93r. The biological growth principle is not invoked in this herb recipe. This makes sense: the herb is the RAW INPUT. It has not yet been processed by the pharmaceutical machine. The F-atom appears only in the manufactured product, not the raw material. The herb recipe extracts FROM the plant; the foldout and jar recipes work ON the extract. The F-atom lives in the extract, not the herb.

#### Terminal Seal: schos=

`s-cho-s` = salt-volatile_heat-salt.

This is a STRUCTURAL FORMULA describing the finished product:

```
SALT → VOLATILE-HEAT → SALT
  (outer)  (active core)  (outer)
```

A salt-encapsulated volatile extract. The terminal seal IS the product description. It names what sits in the jar: the plant's volatile-heat fraction, preserved between two applications of the salt principle.

Compare previous terminals:
- f89r1: `chodaiin=` (energy verified)
- f89r2: `dair=` (root fixed)
- f89v1: `choldy=` (fluid state fixed)
- f89v2: `darails=` (root + complete + fluid + salt)
- f90r1: `okam=` (phase-shift into vessel)
- f90v2: `okeey=` (phase-shift at sensitivity)
- f93r: `schos=` (salt-volatile-salt sandwich)

The herb recipe terminal is the first to describe a PHYSICAL STRUCTURE rather than a process state. It names the product's architecture.

---

### What F93R Tells Us

1. **The Bridge Works Both Ways.** F93r connects the herbal section (raw plants) to the pharmaceutical section (processed medicines) by showing BOTH the plant and its processing protocol. The VML operates identically whether describing herbal inputs or pharmaceutical outputs — the same morphological system, the same operational prefixes, the same grammatical structure.

2. **Oscillation is the Herb Recipe's Engine.** Where the foldout uses verification (daiin) and the jar recipes use extraction (qo-), the herb recipe uses transition (sh-). The material is ALWAYS in transition, oscillating between states, never at rest until the terminal seal.

3. **Salt as Distributed Intervention.** Eight bare `s` tokens scattered across the recipe. Salt isn't a final endpoint — it's a tool applied throughout processing. This matches spagyric practice where salt (ash, mineral residue) is repeatedly introduced during plant extraction.

4. **The Fixation Manifesto (P.3).** 78% d-density in one paragraph. The recipe FRONT-LOADS fixation: fix everything at the start, then let the oscillation run. This is the opposite of the foldout, which builds toward fixation progressively.

5. **No F-Atom.** The biological growth principle is absent from the raw herb recipe. It appears only in processed products. The F-atom is something MANUFACTURED, not something extracted.

6. **Product as Structure.** The terminal seal `schos=` names a physical architecture: salt-volatile-salt. The recipe doesn't end with a process verification — it ends with a product specification.

7. **Minimum Verification, Maximum Transition.** 0.19 daiin/para (lowest in pharmaceutical section) but 0.8 sh-/para (transition density). The herb recipe WORKS more than it CHECKS. The oscillation IS the quality control — if the material stabilizes through repeated cycling, it's done.

---

**F93R COMPLETE.**

**NEXT: F93V — Refinement Companion: Clean Clamped Endpoint**

## FOLIO F93V — REFINEMENT COMPANION: CLEAN CLAMPED ENDPOINT

**Position:** Verso of f93r. Companion refinement protocol for the same herb. Where f93r extracted through oscillation, f93v REFINES the extract through projection and circulation until it reaches a clean, clamped endpoint.

**Structure:** 10 paragraphs (P.1-P.10). ~90 tokens total. DRAMATICALLY denser than f93r's 31 sparse paragraphs. The refinement companion COMPRESSES its information — fewer paragraphs, more tokens per paragraph.

**Critical structural feature:** P.10 (`ychol.chs.ckhy.scheeol=`) carries the TERMINAL marker (=) but appears as Line 2 in the process flow. This means the terminal sits physically near the top of the page, adjacent to the plant illustration — a LABEL or CAPTION that names the finished product before the recipe text elaborates the process below.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

**P.1 (10 tokens): GALLOWS OPENING — Triple Projection**
`porsheody.qoteeo.qosho.cphy.opchody.opor.opchy.otchdal.or.shodaiin-`

- `porsheody` = p(project) + or(source) + she(transition-essence) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). PROJECT from source: essence actively transitioning through heat-fixation. The p- gallows opens the folio — confirmed by mainstream research as a paragraph/page discourse marker. The gallows INITIATES the refinement.
- `qoteeo` = qo(transmute) + tee(temporal-double-e) + o(heat). Transmute through temporal double-e sensitivity with heat. The first transmutation operates at ELEVATED sensitivity — this recipe starts hot and precise.
- `qosho` = qo(transmute) + sh(transition) + o(heat). Transmute the transition through heat. Second qo- token — transmute what's transitioning.
- `cphy` = cp(conduit-project) + h(heat?) + y(active). Conduit-projection active. RARE token — cp- prefix appears in pharmaceutical section as specialized conduit-projection. Flag as cph- CLUSTER — the cfh-/cph- signature.
- `opchody` = op(project) + cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). PROJECT volatile heat to fixation. First op- projection.
- `opor` = op(project) + or(source/rotation). PROJECT to source. Second op- projection — send material BACK to source for another pass.
- `opchy` = op(project) + ch(volatile) + y(active). PROJECT volatile active. Third op- projection.
- `otchdal` = ot(temporal-heat) + ch(volatile) + d(fix) + al(structure). Temporal heat volatilizes, fixes into structure.
- `or` = o(heat) + r(source). Heat to source.
- `shodaiin` = sh(transition) + od(heat-fix) + aiin(verification-complete). TRANSITION VERIFIED.

TRIPLE op- PROJECTION: opchody → opor → opchy. Three projections in sequence. The refinement companion PROJECTS the material outward three times — through volatile heat, back to source, through volatile again. This is CIRCULATION BY PROJECTION. Where f93r oscillated (sh-sh-sh), f93v projects (op-op-op). Different mechanism, same goal: repeatedly move the material through the processing system.

TWO qo- tokens (qoteeo, qosho) + triple op- = FIVE directional operations in one paragraph. The refinement is aggressive from the first line.

`cphy` — CPH- CLUSTER DETECTED. The cfh-/cph- signature appears on the refinement companion. It was ABSENT from f93r (the raw herb recipe). This confirms the pattern: cfh-/cph- appears only in PROCESSED material, not raw inputs.

First daiin (shodaiin) appears in the OPENING paragraph. Compare f93r where the first daiin didn't appear until P.8. The refinement companion verifies IMMEDIATELY — because the material has already been extracted and partially stabilized by f93r. It's not raw anymore; it merits checking from the start.

**P.10 (4 tokens): TERMINAL LABEL — Product Specification**
`ychol.chs.ckhy.scheeol=`

- `ychol` = y(moist/receptive) + ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Moist volatile fluid. The product state: still moist, still containing volatile, in fluid form.
- `chs` = ch(spirit) + s(salt). Spirit-salt. The volatile has been SALTED — the spirit principle bound by salt principle.
- `ckhy` = ckh(valve) + y(active). Valve active. The preparation is valve-controlled — actively gated.
- `scheeol=` = s(salt) + ch(volatile) + ee(double-e) + ol(fluid) + = (TERMINAL). Salt-volatile at double-e sensitivity in fluid. SEALED.

TERMINAL SEAL: `scheeol=` — salt-volatile-double_e-fluid. The finished product is a salt-volatilized fluid at elevated sensitivity. Compare f93r's terminal `schos=` (salt-volatile-salt sandwich). The recto named a SOLID structure (salt encapsulating volatile); the verso names a LIQUID preparation (salt-volatile in double-e fluid).

These are TWO DIFFERENT PRODUCTS from the same herb:
- f93r: salt-volatile-salt SOLID (preserved extract)
- f93v: salt-volatile-ee-fluid LIQUID (active preparation)

The herb yields both a stored form and a working form.

**P.2 (9 tokens): TRIPLE TRANSMUTATION**
`yteeody.qotody.qotchol.qocthody.ytey.oky.daiin.dar.cthom-`

- `yteeody` = y(moist) + tee(temporal-double-e) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Moist temporal double-e actively heat-fixed. Input description: the material from f93r's extraction, still moist and at elevated sensitivity.
- `qotody` = qo(transmute) + to(temporal-heat) + dy(fixed). Transmute temporal heat to fixation.
- `qotchol` = qo(transmute) + t(temporal) + ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Transmute temporal volatile to fluid.
- `qocthody` = qo(transmute/circulate) + cth(conduit-energy) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Circulate through conduit with active heat-fixation.
- `ytey` = y(moist) + t(temporal/energy) + e(essence) + y(active). Moist temporal essence active.
- `oky` = ok(phase-shift) + y(active). Active phase shift.
- `daiin` = FIX/STABILIZE → verification complete. Second daiin.
- `dar` = d(fix) + ar(root). Fix to root.
- `cthom` = cth(conduit-energy) + om(heat-vessel). Conduit energy to vessel.

THREE consecutive qo- tokens: qotody → qotchol → qocthody. TRIPLE TRANSMUTATION. Three different transmutation routes:
1. `qotody`: transmute temporal heat → fixed
2. `qotchol`: transmute temporal volatile → fluid
3. `qocthody`: circulate through conduit → active fixation

Three pathways into the same material simultaneously. The refinement doesn't just transmute once and check — it hits the material from three angles at once, then verifies (daiin), fixes to root (dar), and sends to vessel (cthom).

**P.3 (10 tokens): DOUBLE VERIFICATION + DEEP ROOT**
`dchos.chody.qockhol.oky.cheodaiin.oty.daiin.otal.dair.akal-`

- `dchos` = d(fix) + ch(volatile) + os(heat-salt). Fix volatile with heat-salt. The volatile fraction is being pinned by combined heat and salt.
- `chody` = cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat fixed.
- `qockhol` = qo(circulate) + ckh(valve) + ol(fluid). Circulate through valve into fluid. Valve-gated circulation.
- `oky` = ok(phase-shift) + y(active). Phase shift active.
- `cheodaiin` = che(volatile-essence) + od(heat-fix) + aiin(verification). Volatile essence heat-fixed, VERIFIED. Third daiin.
- `oty` = ot(temporal-heat) + y(active). Temporal heat active.
- `daiin` = FIX/STABILIZE → verification. Fourth daiin.
- `otal` = ot(temporal-heat) + al(structure). Temporal heat structures.
- `dair` = d(fix) + ai(completion) + r(root). Fix to complete root. DEEP ROOT FIXATION — the dair token combines fixation, completion, and root. Everything goes as deep as possible.
- `akal` = ak(crystal) + al(structure). CRYSTAL STRUCTURE. The material has CRYSTALLIZED.

DOUBLE VERIFICATION: cheodaiin + daiin in the same paragraph. The refinement companion checks TWICE. Compare f93r which barely verified at all (0.19/para). The refinement DOUBLES DOWN on checking because it's performing precise operations on already-extracted material.

`dair` + `akal` at paragraph end = fix-complete-root + crystal-structure. The material is fixed to its deepest root AND crystallized into structure. This is the clamped endpoint the title promised: the volatile extract has been driven to crystal form.

**P.4 (10 tokens): SALT-INITIATED DOUBLE EXTRACTION**
`sol.shol.shdchy.qokchol.qokchody.chol.chol.cthy.ykchy.dar-`

- `sol` = s(salt) + ol(fluid). Salt fluid.
- `shol` = sh(transition) + ol(fluid). Transitional fluid.
- `shdchy` = sh(vigorous-transition) + d(fix) + ch(volatile) + y(active). Vigorous transition fixes volatile actively.
- `qokchol` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Extract body volatile into fluid.
- `qokchody` = qo(extract) + k(body) + cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Extract body volatile heat to fixation.
- `chol` = ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Volatile fluid. #1.
- `chol` = ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Volatile fluid. #2.
- `cthy` = cth(conduit-energy) + y(active). Conduit active.
- `ykchy` = y(moist) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + y(active). Moist body volatile active.
- `dar` = d(fix) + ar(root). Fix to root.

DOUBLE EXTRACTION: qokchol + qokchody. Extract body volatile to fluid, extract body volatile heat to fixation. Two extraction routes from the same body.

DOUBLED chol.chol — volatile fluid named twice. Emphatic repetition. The fluid medium is volatile fluid, volatile fluid. The VML uses word repetition as emphasis — documented by mainstream research as a manuscript-wide phenomenon.

**P.5 (9 tokens): VERIFIED FIXATION WITH SALT**
`tshoky.cthody.qotchol.ckhol.dchom.s.olo.oteos.chodaiindy-`

- `tshoky` = t(energy) + sh(salt/transition) + ok(phase-shift) + y(active). Energy-salt phase-shift active.
- `cthody` = cth(conduit) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Conduit heat-fixed active.
- `qotchol` = qo(transmute) + t(temporal) + ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Transmute temporal volatile to fluid.
- `ckhol` = ckh(valve) + ol(fluid). Valve-fluid.
- `dchom` = d(fix) + ch(volatile) + om(heat-vessel). Fix volatile into heated vessel.
- `s` = BARE SALT.
- `olo` = ol(fluid) + o(heat). Heated fluid.
- `oteos` = ot(temporal-heat) + e(essence) + os(heat-salt). Temporal-heat essence with heat-salt.
- `chodaiindy` = cho(volatile-heat) + daiin(verified) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat VERIFIED AND FIXED. Fifth daiin — but fused with dy (fixed). The verification and fixation are SIMULTANEOUS. This compound token doesn't verify then fix — it does both at once.

`chodaiindy` — FUSED VERIFICATION-FIXATION. The daiin verification is welded to dy fixation in a single token. This is the "clean clamped endpoint" — verification and fixation are no longer sequential operations but a single clamped state.

**P.6 (9 tokens): VALVE-CONTROLLED CIRCULATION TO VESSEL**
`ytchol.ckhol.qochocthy.ctha.chkeey.cthodys.dar.she.qokam-`

- `ytchol` = y(moist) + t(energy) + ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Moist energy-volatile fluid.
- `ckhol` = ckh(valve) + ol(fluid). Valve fluid.
- `qochocthy` = qo(circulate) + cho(volatile-heat) + cth(conduit) + y(active). Circulate volatile heat through active conduit.
- `ctha` = cth(conduit) + a(beginning/opening). Conduit opens.
- `chkeey` = ch(spirit) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Spirit-body at double-e active. The material's spirit and body fractions are BOTH at elevated sensitivity. Whole-material sensitivity.
- `cthodys` = cth(conduit) + od(heat-fix) + y(active) + s(salt). Conduit heat-fixes actively with salt.
- `dar` = d(fix) + ar(root). Fix to root.
- `she` = BARE TRANSITION-ESSENCE. Two characters. Imperative: TRANSITION.
- `qokam` = qo(extract) + k(body) + am(vessel). Extract body into vessel.

`chkeey` — spirit-body at double-e. BOTH components of the material (spirit AND body) are at elevated sensitivity. The refinement has brought the ENTIRE preparation to double-e, not just one fraction. This is comprehensive sensitivity — the whole product responds.

Terminal sequence: `dar.she.qokam` = fix to root → transition → extract to vessel. The paragraph ends by FIXING, then immediately TRANSITIONING and EXTRACTING into the storage vessel. Fix-shift-store in three tokens.

**P.7 (8 tokens): VERIFICATION CLUSTER**
`oees.ckheody.ockheey.koldy.tchodaiin.ctheos.shodaiin.qokeeam-`

- `oees` = o(heat) + ee(double-e) + s(salt). Heat at double-e with salt. Three principles in three characters.
- `ckheody` = ckh(valve) + e(essence) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Valve essence heat-fixed active.
- `ockheey` = o(heat) + ckh(valve) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Heat through valve at double-e active.
- `koldy` = k(body) + ol(fluid) + dy(fixed). Body fluid fixed.
- `tchodaiin` = tch(energy-volatile) + od(heat-fix) + aiin(verified). Energy-volatile heat-fixed VERIFIED. Sixth daiin.
- `ctheos` = cth(conduit) + e(essence) + os(heat-salt). Conduit essence heat-salted.
- `shodaiin` = sh(transition) + od(heat-fix) + aiin(verified). Transition heat-fixed VERIFIED. Seventh daiin.
- `qokeeam` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + am(vessel). Extract body at double-e into vessel.

DOUBLE VERIFICATION: tchodaiin + shodaiin. Both the energy-volatile AND the transition are verified in the same paragraph. P.7 is a VERIFICATION CLUSTER — two daiin checks followed by extraction into vessel at double-e. The refinement companion checks EXHAUSTIVELY before committing to vessel.

`qokeeam` — extract body at double-e to vessel. The FINAL EXTRACTION at elevated sensitivity into the storage vessel. The double-e tells us this extraction is precise, sensitive, measured.

**P.8 (11 tokens): GALLOWS PROJECTION WITH VERIFICATION**
`dcho.chody.teol.sheol.cheeol.dair.okchey.cthey.dsheom.okeey.dama-`

- `dcho` = d(fix) + ch(volatile) + o(heat). Fix volatile with heat.
- `chody` = cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat fixed.
- `teol` = t(energy/temporal) + e(essence) + ol(fluid). Temporal essence fluid.
- `sheol` = sh(transition) + e(essence) + ol(fluid). Transition essence fluid.
- `cheeol` = ch(volatile) + ee(double-e) + ol(fluid). Volatile at double-e in fluid. Triple -eol sequence: teol → sheol → cheeol. Three different fluids in sequence — temporal, transitional, volatile-double-e.
- `dair` = d(fix) + ai(complete) + r(root). Fix complete root. Third dair on the page.
- `okchey` = ok(phase-shift) + ch(volatile) + e(essence) + y(active). Phase-shift volatile essence active.
- `cthey` = cth(conduit) + e(essence) + y(active). Conduit essence active.
- `dsheom` = d(fix) + sh(transition) + e(essence) + om(vessel). Fix transition-essence into vessel. The transition is captured and fixed into vessel.
- `okeey` = ok(phase-shift) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Phase-shift at double-e active.
- `dama` = d(fix) + am(vessel) + a(opening). Fix into vessel-opening. Or: dam(fix-vessel) + a. The vessel is sealed.

ELEVEN tokens — the DENSEST paragraph on the page. Three `-eol` fluid tokens in sequence (teol, sheol, cheeol) create a FLUID CASCADE: the material passes through temporal fluid, transition fluid, then volatile-double-e fluid. Three fluid stages in three tokens.

THREE d-prefix tokens (dcho, dair, dsheom, dama = four actually). Heavy fixation paragraph. But each fixation targets a DIFFERENT thing: volatile (dcho), root (dair), transition-essence (dsheom), vessel (dama). Distributed fixation — fix everything at once, from different angles.

**P.9 (10 tokens): THE TRIPLE-E TOKEN + DOUBLE ROOT SEAL**
`odeeeodl.cheodar.oksho.chody.okchey.cthol.oly.ytchol.sar.dar-`

- `odeeeodl` = o(heat) + d(fix) + eee(TRIPLE-E) + od(heat-fix) + l(layer/structure). Heat-fix at TRIPLE-E sensitivity, heat-fix into layered structure. THE TRIPLE-E TOKEN. Maximum sensitivity between double fixation layers. This is the highest sensitivity token on f93v — the refinement companion deploys triple-e at its final processing paragraph.
- `cheodar` = che(volatile-essence) + od(heat-fix) + ar(root). Volatile essence heat-fixed to root.
- `oksho` = ok(phase-shift) + sh(transition) + o(heat). Phase-shift transition through heat.
- `chody` = cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat fixed.
- `okchey` = ok(phase-shift) + ch(volatile) + e(essence) + y(active). Phase-shift volatile essence active.
- `cthol` = cth(conduit) + ol(fluid). Conduit fluid.
- `oly` = ol(fluid) + y(active). Active fluid.
- `ytchol` = y(moist) + tch(energy-volatile) + ol(fluid). Moist energy-volatile fluid.
- `sar` = s(salt) + ar(root). SALT TO ROOT. Salt principle driven to maximum depth.
- `dar` = d(fix) + ar(root). FIX TO ROOT.

DOUBLE ROOT SEAL: `sar.dar` — salt-root, fix-root. The final two tokens of the last processing paragraph BOTH target root: salt it deep, fix it deep. Two roots. The preparation is anchored at its deepest level by both salt and fixation simultaneously.

`odeeeodl` — TRIPLE-E between double fixation-heat. Structure: o-d-eee-od-l. Heat-fix | TRIPLE-E | heat-fix-layer. The maximum sensitivity is SANDWICHED between fixation operations, just as f93r's terminal `schos` sandwiched volatile between salt. The sandwich pattern recurs: bracket the active principle between stabilizing operations.
