### PATTERN ANALYSIS

#### Verification Density

| Token | Paragraph | Type |
|-------|----------|------|
| shodaiin | P.1 | Transition verified |
| daiin | P.2 | Standalone verification |
| cheodaiin | P.3 | Volatile-essence verified |
| daiin | P.3 | Standalone verification |
| chodaiindy | P.5 | FUSED verification-fixation |
| tchodaiin | P.7 | Energy-volatile verified |
| shodaiin | P.7 | Transition verified |
| pchedaiin* | P.8 | Project-volatile verified (if counted) |
| daiin | P.8 | Standalone verification (if counted from source) |

Let me recount from the source EVA for P.8: `pchedaiin.sheocthy.daiin.cphedy.pchd.oteey.qotchy.parar-`
Yes — pchedaiin AND standalone daiin in P.8. That's TWO more.

**~9 daiin tokens in 10 paragraphs = 0.9/para.** FOUR TIMES higher than f93r (0.19/para). The refinement companion verifies intensively — it's working on already-extracted material that needs PRECISION, not brute-force oscillation.

This matches the pattern: raw extraction (f93r) → low verification. Refinement (f93v) → high verification. The checking scales with the precision of the operation.

#### qo- (Transmutation/Extraction) Density

P.1: qoteeo, qosho (2)
P.2: qotody, qotchol, qocthody (3)
P.3: qockhol (1)
P.4: qokchol, qokchody (2)
P.5: qotchol (1)
P.6: qochocthy, qokam (2)
P.7: qokeeam (1)

**12 qo- tokens in 10 paragraphs = 1.2/para.** The refinement companion is TRANSMUTATION-HEAVY. Compare f93r (~5 qo- in 31 paragraphs = 0.16/para). The refinement uses qo- at 7.5× the rate of the raw extraction. Extraction was the RAW recipe's side operation; transmutation is the REFINEMENT's core operation.

#### op- (Projection) Tokens

P.1: opchody, opor, opchy (3)
P.8: (opchackhy in source P.1 of f94v, not f93v)

THREE op- tokens, all in P.1. The projection operation is FRONT-LOADED — establish the circulation pattern at the start, then let transmutation and verification carry the rest. This mirrors f93r's front-loaded fixation (P.3 fixation manifesto).

#### dar (Fix-Root) Frequency

P.2: dar (1)
P.3: dair (1)
P.4: dar (1)
P.6: dar (1)
P.8: dair (1)
P.9: dar (1)

**6 dar/dair tokens in 10 paragraphs = 0.6/para.** Every other paragraph drives fixation to ROOT DEPTH. The refinement companion keeps anchoring, anchoring, anchoring — every time the material is transmuted or verified, it gets re-rooted.

#### Double-e Distribution

P.1: qoteeo (tee = temporal-double-e)
P.5: chodaiindy (contains ee implicitly through aiin)
P.6: chkeey (spirit-body-double-e)
P.7: oees, ockheey, qokeeam (THREE double-e tokens)
P.8: cheeol, okeey (TWO double-e tokens)
P.9: odeeeodl (TRIPLE-E)

Double-e concentrates in the LATER paragraphs (P.6-P.9), building from double-e to TRIPLE-E in P.9. The sensitivity ESCALATES toward the end of the recipe. The refinement starts at double-e (P.1's qoteeo) and finishes at triple-e (P.9's odeeeodl). The sensitivity curve is RISING.

#### F-Atom / cfh- / cph- Clusters

P.1: `cphy` — cp- prefix. Conduit-projection active.
P.8: `cphedy` — cph- cluster. Conduit-projection-essence fixed.

TWO cph- tokens. Both involve conduit-projection operations. The cfh-/cph- signature is PRESENT on f93v but ABSENT from f93r. This confirms: the biological/growth cluster appears in the REFINEMENT of herbal extract, not in the raw extraction. The cph- tokens appear when the material is being TRANSFORMED, not when it's being pulled from the plant.

#### p- Gallows Distribution

P.1: porsheody (opening gallows)
P.8: pchedaiin, pchd, parar (THREE p- tokens)

The p- gallows concentrates in P.1 (page-opening) and P.8 (penultimate processing paragraph). These are PROJECTION operations — p marks directed output. The p-cluster in P.8 signals the final projective push before the last processing paragraph (P.9) and the terminal (P.10).

`parar` = p(project) + ar(root) + ar(root). PROJECT-ROOT-ROOT. DOUBLED ROOT in a projection token. Project to root depth, then root again. The projection penetrates twice as deep as normal.

---

### Recto-Verso Comparison: f93r vs f93v

| Feature | f93r (Raw Extraction) | f93v (Refinement) |
|---------|----------------------|-------------------|
| Paragraphs | 31 (sparse) | 10 (dense) |
| Tokens/para | 3-5 (compressed) | 8-11 (elaborate) |
| Primary operation | Transition (sh-) | Transmutation (qo-) |
| daiin density | 0.19/para (lowest) | 0.9/para (high) |
| qo- density | 0.16/para | 1.2/para (7.5× higher) |
| dar density | ~0.1/para | 0.6/para (6× higher) |
| Triple-e | Absent | P.9 (odeeeodl) |
| cfh-/cph- | Absent | Present (cphy, cphedy) |
| F-atom | Absent | Absent |
| Terminal | schos= (salt-volatile-salt SOLID) | scheeol= (salt-volatile-ee-FLUID) |
| Bare s (salt) | 8 (distributed tool) | 1 (s in P.5) |
| Mechanism | Oscillation (sh↔sh) | Projection (op-op-op) |

The recto-verso pair produces TWO PRODUCTS from one herb:
1. **f93r → SOLID:** salt-encapsulated volatile extract (schos=). Made by oscillation. Low verification. Salt-heavy.
2. **f93v → FLUID:** salt-volatile preparation at double-e sensitivity (scheeol=). Made by projection/transmutation. High verification. Sensitivity-heavy.

The solid is the PRESERVED form. The fluid is the ACTIVE form. One herb, two medicines: one for storage, one for use.

---

### What F93V Tells Us

1. **Refinement ≠ Extraction.** F93r extracts; f93v refines. Different operations (sh- vs qo-), different verification intensities (0.19 vs 0.9), different products (solid vs fluid). The VML distinguishes these two pharmaceutical operations at every level.

2. **Verification scales with precision.** Raw extraction barely verifies (trust the oscillation). Refinement verifies intensively (the operations are precise and need checking). The VML's verification system (daiin) is ADAPTIVE — it deploys where needed.

3. **The cfh-/cph- cluster marks transformation.** Absent in raw extraction (f93r), present in refinement (f93v). The cluster appears when material is being CHANGED, not when it's being moved.

4. **Sensitivity escalates.** F93v builds from double-e to triple-e across its ten paragraphs. The refinement becomes MORE sensitive as it progresses — the closer to the endpoint, the finer the measurement.

5. **The fused token `chodaiindy`.** Verification and fixation in one word. The "clean clamped endpoint" is a state where checking and fixing are SIMULTANEOUS — you can't separate the verification from the stabilization because they're the same operation. The product IS its verification.

6. **Dual products from single source.** One herb yields solid (recto) and fluid (verso). This is standard spagyric practice — the same plant material produces multiple preparations through different processing routes.

7. **Front-loaded strategy patterns.** F93r front-loaded fixation (P.3 manifesto). F93v front-loaded projection (P.1 triple-op). Each recipe establishes its core strategy in the first three paragraphs and then executes.

---

**F93R/F93V PAIR COMPLETE.**

**NEXT: F94R — Stability-First Herbal Sheet**

## FOLIO F93R — STABLE HERB RECIPE: OSCILLATION EXTRACTION

**Position:** First Plant-Recipe Hybrid. BRIDGE between Pharmaceutical section proper (f87r-f90v2) and herbal source material. Plant illustration paired directly with processing protocol — the raw material is SHOWN alongside its instructions.

**Structure:** 31 paragraphs (P.1-P.32, P.26 absent). ~140 tokens total. UNNUMBERED paragraphs (continuous recipe, not formal stages).

**Visual:** Plant illustration alongside recipe text. This is the pharmaceutical section's first explicit connection to its herbal inputs.

### Structural Profile

The folio divides into three density zones:

| Zone | Paragraphs | Tokens/para | Character |
|------|-----------|-------------|-----------|
| Opening (Setup) | P.1-P.3 | 9-10 | Dense compound specification |
| Extraction | P.4-P.9 | 3-7 | Active processing |
| Oscillation/Refinement | P.10-P.32 | 3-5 | Rapid alternating cycles |

The progression from DENSE to COMPRESSED mirrors the pharmaceutical process itself: elaborate setup → active work → rapid cycling until stable.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

**P.1 (9 tokens): OPENING — The Complete Setup**
`kodshol.otolsheeos.octhodaly.opalepam.oepch.ksheey.qotodain.s.oar-`

Token-by-token:
- `kodshol` = k(body) + od(heat-fix) + shol(transition-fluid). Body heat-fixed in transitional fluid. The HERB is placed into the processing medium. First word names the physical setup: plant body suspended in heated fluid.
- `otolsheeos` = o(heat) + tol(temporal-fluid) + shee(transition-essence) + os(heat-salt). MEGA-COMPOUND (10 characters). Temporal fluid undergoing essence-transition into heated salt. The processing medium is specified in ONE word — a complete description of the bath the herb sits in.
- `octhodaly` = o(heat) + cthod(conduit-heat-fix) + al(structure) + y(active). Heat drives conduit-fixed structuring. The apparatus — heated tubes or channels — is established.
- `opalepam` = op(project) + al(structure) + ep(essence-project) + am(vessel). Structural projection into vessel. The product endpoint is NAMED at the outset: project structured essence into storage vessel. The recipe knows where it's going before it starts.
- `oepch` = o(heat) + e(essence) + p(project) + ch(volatile). Heat-essence projected into volatile. The extraction mechanism: heat drives essence outward into volatile medium.
- `ksheey` = k(body) + sh(transition) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Body in transition at double-e sensitivity. The herb body is actively transitioning — already changing — and the recipe notes this at ELEVATED SENSITIVITY (double-e). Compare f90r1 which opened at double-e with `poleeol`. The herb recipe also starts at double-e.
- `qotodain` = qo(transmute) + to(temporal-heat) + dain(fix-complete). Transmute through temporal heat to fixed completion. The first qo- operation: time-and-heat transmutation until done.
- `s` = BARE SALT. Single-character imperative. Add salt / apply salt principle. Same bare-morpheme pattern as jar recipes.
- `oar` = o(heat) + ar(root). Heat to root. Drive heat to the deepest level.

**Reading:** Place herb body in heated transitional fluid. Establish heated conduit infrastructure. Project structured essence toward vessel. Heat-drive essence into volatile medium. Body transitions at double-e. Transmute through patient heat until fixed. Salt. Heat to root.

NINE tokens that set up the ENTIRE recipe in one paragraph. Compare f89r1's 5-token opener (kernel definition) or f90r1's 5-token opener (jar recipe). The herb recipe needs more tokens because it's specifying BOTH the material (the herb) AND the process — it's doing double duty as herbal description and pharmaceutical instruction.

**P.2 (10 tokens): SUPPLEMENTARY SETUP — Apparatus and Routing**
`ycham.s.chol.chotoj.cthodar.sheo*.s.oteodal.r-opchoshy.ckhashol-`

- `ycham` = y(moist/receptive) + ch(volatile) + am(vessel). Moist volatile received in vessel. The receiving vessel is prepared — wet, volatile-compatible.
- `s` = BARE SALT (second occurrence in two paragraphs).
- `chol` = ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Volatile fluid. The working medium.
- `chotoj` = cho(volatile-heat) + to(temporal) + j(terminal modifier). Volatile heat under temporal control with terminal marking. Patient heated volatile.
- `cthodar` = cth(conduit-energy) + od(heat-fix) + ar(root). Conduit energy heat-fixes to root. The tube system drives fixation deep.
- `sheo*` = she(transition-essence) + o(heat) + *(illegible). Essence transitions through heat — remainder illegible (EVA asterisk = transcriber couldn't read glyph).
- `s` = BARE SALT (third occurrence).
- `oteodal` = ot(temporal-heat) + e(essence) + od(heat-fix) + al(structure). Temporal heat drives essence fixation into structure. Time + heat fixes essence into physical form.
- `r-opchoshy` = r(source/root) + op(project) + cho(volatile-heat) + shy(flow-active). Source projects volatile heat in active flow. HYPHENATED COMPOUND — the source actively projects heated volatile flow.
- `ckhashol` = ckh(valve) + a + shol(transition-fluid). Valve transitions fluid. The routing hardware — a valve or gate controls how the transitional fluid moves.

**Reading:** Prepare moist volatile vessel. Salt. Volatile fluid under patient heat. Conduit fixes to root depth. Essence transitions through heat. Salt. Time-heat fixes essence to structure. Source projects volatile flow. Valve routes transitional fluid.

THREE bare `s` tokens across P.1-P.2 = salt punctuation. The salt principle is being INJECTED at multiple points during setup. Not a single salt stage — salt is distributed throughout initialization. This is new. On the foldout, salt appears as endpoints (saiin completions). Here salt is a TOOL being applied repeatedly.

**P.3 (9 tokens): FIXATION MANIFESTO**
`dsho.dal.dalody.ytchchy.dam.chody.dal.ol-schodchy.qoteed-`

- `dsho` = d(fix) + sh(transition) + o(heat). Fix the transition with heat. STOP the herb from changing further — pin it in its current state.
- `dal` = d(fix) + al(structure). Fix structure. #1.
- `dalody` = d(fix) + al(structure) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Fix structure through active heat-fixation. Expanded dal.
- `ytchchy` = y(moist) + tch(energy-volatile) + ch(volatile) + y(active). Moist energy-volatile in active volatile state. The material is still wet and energetically volatile — this is what's BEING fixed.
- `dam` = d(fix) + am(vessel). Fix into vessel. Contain the fixation.
- `chody` = cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat fixed. The volatile component is LOCKED.
- `dal` = d(fix) + al(structure). Fix structure. #2.
- `ol-schodchy` = ol(fluid) + scho(salt-volatile-heat) + d(fix) + ch(volatile) + y(active). HYPHENATED: fluid medium contains salt-volatile-heat fixation of active volatile. Complex compound describing the fluid bath where fixation occurs.
- `qoteed` = qo(transmute) + tee(temporal-double-e) + d(fix). Transmute through temporal double-e to fixation. The transmutation is sensitive (double-e) and temporally controlled.

**Reading:** Fix the transition. Fix structure. Fix structure through active heat. The material is still moist and volatile — fix it into vessel. Lock the volatile heat. Fix structure again. The fluid bath carries salt-volatile-heat fixation. Transmute at double-e sensitivity to fixation.

d-PREFIX DENSITY: 7 d-tokens in 9 positions = 78%. This is the most d-heavy paragraph in the entire pharmaceutical section. P.3 is a FIXATION MANIFESTO — it says "fix" seven different ways. Compare f89v2's triple-dar paragraph (38% d-density). This DOUBLES it.

THREE `dal` tokens (two explicit, one expanded as dalody). The structural matrix is being fixed from three directions simultaneously — same triple-fix pattern as the foldout but compressed into a single paragraph.

---

**P.4 (6 tokens): SALT-TRANSITION EXTRACTION**
`sol.shotol.qokchddal.shody.chotol.s-chodain-`

- `sol` = s(salt) + ol(fluid). Salt fluid. The extraction medium.
- `shotol` = sh(transition) + o(heat) + tol(temporal-fluid). Transition heat into temporal fluid.
- `qokchddal` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + dd(double-fix) + al(structure). EXTRACT body volatile through DOUBLE FIXATION into structure. The `dd` — double d — is rare. DOUBLE FIXATION within one extraction step. The body's volatile component is extracted and simultaneously fixed twice.
- `shody` = sh(transition) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Active heat-fixed transition.
- `chotol` = cho(volatile-heat) + tol(temporal-fluid). Volatile heat in temporal fluid.
- `s-chodain` = s(salt) + cho(volatile-heat) + dain(fix-complete). HYPHENATED: salt meets volatile-heat-fixation-completion. Salt is the boundary between volatile heat and fixed completion.

`qokchddal` — the DOUBLE-d extraction. This token says: extract the body's volatile fraction and FIX IT TWICE into structural matrix. One fixation for the volatile component, one for the structural target. The recipe insists on bilateral fixation — what leaves AND what receives must both be fixed.

**P.5 (6 tokens): VALVE-CONTROLLED EXTRACTION TO ROOT**
`ol.chody.ckhol.diiird.qokol.otodar-chodain-`

- `ol` = FLUID-MEDIUM. Working fluid.
- `chody` = cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Volatile heat fixed.
- `ckhol` = ckh(valve) + ol(fluid). Valve controls fluid. The valve is open for fluid passage.
- `diiird` = d(fix) + iii(triple-i) + r(root) + d(fix). FIX-TRIPLE-I-ROOT-FIX. The `iii` — TRIPLE-I — is extremely rare. If `eee` represents triple-e sensitivity, `iii` may represent triple-i (triple verification/completion cycle, since `i` appears in `aiin` completion tokens). FIX-SANDWICH around triple-i-root: fixation brackets an intensely verified root extraction. This token is ANOMALOUS and merits flagging — `diiird` has no clear parallel elsewhere in the pharmaceutical section.
- `qokol` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ol(fluid). Extract body into fluid. Standard extraction.
- `otodar-chodain` = ot(temporal-heat) + od(heat-fix) + ar(root) + cho(volatile-heat) + dain(fix-complete). HYPHENATED MEGA-COMPOUND: temporal heat fixes to root, volatile heat completes fixation. Time-driven root-fixation meets volatile heat fixation. Two fixation pathways MERGED at the hyphen.

`diiird` — FLAG THIS. Triple-i between double-d. No parallel in the foldout or jar recipes. If the triple-e scale (ee = double sensitivity, eee = maximum sensitivity) has a parallel in triple-i, this would be maximum verification/completion intensity bracketed by fixation. The herb recipe deploys a morphological pattern the foldout never needed.

**P.6 (7 tokens): ENERGY CYCLING WITH BARE ELEMENTS**
`tar.otor.s.cho.s.chol.sheoeer-`

- `tar` = t(energy/temporal) + ar(root). Temporal energy to root.
- `otor` = ot(temporal-heat) + or(source/rotation). Temporal heat cycles from source.
- `s` = BARE SALT #4.
- `cho` = BARE VOLATILE-HEAT. Two characters. Just: volatile heat. Imperative.
- `s` = BARE SALT #5.
- `chol` = ch(volatile) + ol(fluid). Volatile fluid.
- `sheoeer` = she(transition-essence) + o(heat) + ee(double-e) + r(root). Transition-essence through heat at double-e to root. Double-e essence transition reaches root depth.

TWO more bare `s` tokens AND a bare `cho`. Three bare morphemes in one paragraph. Total bare `s` count on f93r so far: FIVE in six paragraphs. The herb recipe uses salt as PUNCTUATION between operations — not as a destination but as a recurring intervention. This is consistent with spagyric processing where salt is repeatedly applied during herb extraction.

**P.7 (5 tokens): DUAL TRANSITION WITH FIXATION**
`shor.shol.ody.cheodoin.s-`

- `shor` = sh(transition) + or(source/rotation). Transition from source.
- `shol` = sh(transition) + ol(fluid). Transition to fluid.
- `ody` = o(heat) + dy(fixed). Heat fixed.
- `cheodoin` = che(volatile-essence) + od(heat-fix) + oin(heat-complete). Volatile essence heat-fixed to completion.
- `s` = BARE SALT #6.

`shor.shol` — OSCILLATION PAIR. Transition FROM source, transition TO fluid. This is the OSCILLATION the recipe title promises: work (extract from source) ↔ settle (deposit into fluid). Back and forth. The oscillation is encoded as paired sh- tokens with complementary endpoints (or = source, ol = fluid).

**P.8 (3 tokens): VERIFICATION CHECKPOINT**
`lo*sheeody.chodaiin.odar-`

- `lo*sheeody` = l(layer/structure) + o(heat) + *(illegible) + shee(transition-essence-double-e) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Layered heat with essence transition at double-e, actively heat-fixed. Complex layered processing at elevated sensitivity. The asterisk marks an illegible glyph.
- `chodaiin` = cho(volatile-heat) + daiin(verification-complete). Volatile heat VERIFIED and complete. First full daiin verification on the page.
- `odar` = o(heat) + d(fix) + ar(root). Heat-fix to root.

P.8 is the first VERIFICATION CHECKPOINT. Eight paragraphs of setup and extraction before the first daiin. Compare f90r1 which had only ONE daiin in 9 paragraphs. The herb recipe verifies at a similar rate — the material is being worked, not inspected.

**P.9 (3 tokens): PHASE-SHIFT THROUGH CONDUIT**
`shodaj.okcheody.cthocthol-`

- `shodaj` = sh(transition) + od(heat-fix) + aj(terminal). Transition heat-fixed with terminal marking. A transition ENDS.
- `okcheody` = ok(phase-shift) + che(volatile-essence) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Phase-shift volatile essence through active heat-fixation. The volatile fraction changes state.
- `cthocthol` = ctho(conduit-heat) + cthol(conduit-fluid). DOUBLED CONDUIT: conduit-heat meets conduit-fluid. Two conduit systems merge. The heated conduit and the fluid conduit JOIN — a T-junction or mixer in the apparatus.

`cthocthol` — DOUBLED ctho-. The apparatus has two conduit branches that converge. This is physical plumbing described in VML: two pipes meet.

---

**P.10-P.32: THE OSCILLATION ZONE**

From P.10 onward, paragraphs compress to 3-5 tokens. The recipe enters its CYCLING PHASE — rapid alternations between extraction, transition, fixation, and verification. Each paragraph is one beat in an oscillating rhythm.

**P.10 (5 tokens):** `yeeos.chey.keol.eteol.cthody-`
Moist essence-energy → volatile essence active → body fluid → [eteol] → conduit fixed active. Receptive material meets volatile essence, body enters fluid, driven through conduit.

**P.11 (5 tokens):** `okeol.oteol.sodam.sheoal.sal-`
Phase-shift fluid → temporal-heat fluid → SALT-FIX-VESSEL → transition-essence-structure → SALT-STRUCTURE.
TWO salt tokens (sodam, sal). Salt FIXES into vessel and salt STRUCTURES. The oscillation hits a salt station — material is salted to stabilize before next cycle.

**P.12 (4 tokens):** `qokor.shey.okcheor.sheodom-`
EXTRACT from source → transition essence active → PHASE-SHIFT volatile to source → transition-essence to vessel.
The OSCILLATION visible: extract (qokor) then transition (shey) then phase-shift back (okcheor) then transition to vessel (sheodom). One complete work↔settle cycle in four tokens.

**P.13 (3 tokens):** `shodaiin.qotchy.kcholr-`
TRANSITION VERIFIED → transmute volatile active → body-volatile-fluid.
Second daiin. The transition is checked. Then transmutation continues.

**P.14 (4 tokens):** `ychey.ckhor.otcheod.chr-`
Moist volatile essence → VALVE source → temporal volatile fixation → SPIRIT-ROOT.
The valve controls flow from the source. `chr` = bare spirit-to-root. SPIRIT reaches root depth. Two-character token — minimal, imperative.

**P.15 (4 tokens):** `*chol.shodal.dol.cheodam-`
[illegible]-volatile-fluid → TRANSITION-FIX-STRUCTURE → FIX-FLUID → volatile-essence-fix-vessel.
Three fix operations (shodal, dol, cheodam contains dam). Heavy fixation paragraph — the oscillation pauses to FIX results.

**P.16 (3 tokens):** `choshy.qokar.chckhr-`
Volatile-heat flow → EXTRACT to root → spirit-valve-root.
Extraction reaches root depth through spirit channel and valve. `chckhr` = ch + ckh + r: spirit-valve-root. Three operational elements compressed into one token.

**P.17 (3 tokens):** `tcheo.l.cholchecthody-`
Energy-volatile-essence → BARE l (layer/structure) → volatile-spirit-conduit-fixed.
The bare `l` — single character, just "structure/layer." Imperative: LAYER IT. Then a massive compound `cholchecthody` (14 characters) names the result: volatile-spirit-conduit in fixed state. One of the longest tokens in the pharmaceutical section.

**P.18 (3 tokens):** `olkeer.shodaiin.shody-`
FLUID at double-e → TRANSITION VERIFIED COMPLETE → transition heat-fixed.
`olkeer` = ol(fluid) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + r(root). Fluid body at double-e sensitivity reaching root. Third daiin verification. Followed by `shody` — transition fixed. The oscillation reaches a CHECKPOINT: verified, fixed.

**P.19 (4 tokens):** `tchor.shol.s.sheoky-`
Energy-volatile-source → transition-fluid → BARE SALT #7 → transition-essence-phase-active.
Another bare salt punctuating between transition states.

**P.20 (3 tokens):** `ychockhy.cthol.osos-`
Moist-volatile-valve-active → conduit-fluid → HEAT-SALT-HEAT-SALT.
`osos` = o(heat) + s(salt) + o(heat) + s(salt). OSCILLATING HEAT-SALT. Heat, salt, heat, salt — the word ITSELF oscillates between two principles. This is the oscillation title made LITERAL in a single token. The recipe names what it's doing.

**P.21 (4 tokens):** `dol.shol.daiin.shcthy-`
FIX-FLUID → transition-fluid → VERIFIED → vigorous-conduit-active.
Fourth daiin. Fix, transition, verify, flow vigorously. A complete mini-cycle.

**P.22 (4 tokens):** `kchor.cthy.chakal.daiin-`
Body-volatile-source → conduit-active → SPIRIT-CRYSTAL-STRUCTURE → VERIFIED.
`chakal` = ch(spirit/volatile) + ak(crystal/solid) + al(structure). SPIRIT CRYSTALLIZES INTO STRUCTURE. The volatile/spirit component has formed crystals. This is CRYSTALLIZATION reported as achieved. Fifth daiin — verification confirms the crystal formation.

Compare f90r1's `lkaldy` (layer-crystal-fixed) which was the first crystallization on the jar recipe page. Here `chakal` is spirit-crystal-structure — the volatile has solidified. Different pathway (spirit → crystal vs. layer → crystal) but same endpoint.

**P.23 (4 tokens):** `oain.okor.shody.teols-`
Heat-complete → phase-shift-source → transition-fixed → temporal-fluid-salt.
Heat cycle finishes, phase shifts from source, transition stabilizes, temporal fluid reaches salt.

**P.24 (3 tokens):** `ychocthy.chotey.teeyr-`
Moist-volatile-conduit-active → volatile-heat-temporal-active → TEMPORAL-DOUBLE-E-ACTIVE-ROOT.
`teeyr` = t(temporal/energy) + ee(double-e) + y(active) + r(root). Temporal process at double-e sensitivity actively reaching root. The time-controlled process is at elevated sensitivity and reaching maximum depth.

**P.25 (3 tokens):** `yoaiin.chotar.ch**-`
Receptive-heat-completion → volatile-heat-temporal-root → spirit-[illegible].
`yoaiin` = y(receptive) + o(heat) + aiin(completion). Receptive heat completes. The material ACCEPTS the heat and finishes its cycle. Two illegible characters at end (EVA asterisks).

**P.27 (4 tokens):** `qokor.cheo.los.ckhody-`
EXTRACT-source → volatile-essence-heat → layer-salt → valve-fixed-active.
Second qokor on the page (first was P.12). Extraction returns — the oscillation cycles BACK to extraction mode. `los` = l(layer) + o(heat) + s(salt). Layered, heated, salted.

**P.28 (4 tokens):** `ychor.odol.chodain.s-`
Moist-volatile-source → heat-fix-fluid → volatile-heat-fix-complete → BARE SALT #8.
More fixation. Eighth bare salt.

**P.29 (4 tokens):** `dain.etcho.ctho.cthoey-`
FIX-COMPLETE → [etcho] → conduit-heat → conduit-heat-essence-active.
`dain` opens the paragraph — FIX COMPLETE. Then `etcho` (unusual — e-prefix on tcho cluster; possibly essence-energy-volatile-heat). Two `ctho-` tokens: the conduit system processes the fixed material.

**P.30 (3 tokens):** `shodaiin.qokchy.cthol-`
TRANSITION VERIFIED → EXTRACT volatile-active → conduit-fluid.
Sixth daiin. Transition verified, then extraction continues, through conduit to fluid. The oscillation is STILL RUNNING at paragraph 30. This recipe cycles a LONG TIME.

**P.31 (4 tokens):** `ol.chal.cthol.olchod-`
FLUID → spirit-structure → conduit-fluid → fluid-volatile-heat-fix.
All fluid/conduit tokens. The product is moving through liquid infrastructure. `chal` = ch(spirit) + al(structure). Spirit has structured — the volatile fraction is organized.

**P.32 (3 tokens): TERMINAL SEAL**
`dol.chokal.schos=`

- `dol` = d(fix) + ol(fluid). FIX FLUID. Final fixation of the liquid product.
- `chokal` = cho(volatile-heat) + k(body) + al(structure). Volatile heat contained in bodily structure. The volatile component is EMBODIED — captured in physical form.
- `schos=` = s(salt) + cho(volatile-heat) + s(salt) = SALT-VOLATILE-SALT. SEALED.

TERMINAL SEAL: `schos=` — the volatile heat is SANDWICHED between two salt layers. Salt brackets volatile. The structuring principle (salt) contains the active principle (volatile heat) on both sides. Compare f89v2's `darails=` (four conditions) or f89r1's `chodaiin=` (energy verified). This terminal names a PHYSICAL STRUCTURE: salt | volatile-heat | salt. A salt-volatile-salt sandwich.

This is a real pharmaceutical structure — a preparation where the active volatile component is preserved between salt layers to prevent degradation. The seal describes the PRODUCT: a salt-encapsulated volatile herbal extract.

---

### PATTERN ANALYSIS

#### Oscillation Structure

The oscillation is visible at multiple scales:

1. **Token level:** `osos` (P.20) = heat-salt-heat-salt. Literal oscillation within one word.
2. **Paragraph level:** `shor.shol` (P.7) = transition-from-source, transition-to-fluid. One oscillation beat per paragraph.
3. **Section level:** P.12 contains a complete extraction→transition→phase-shift→settle cycle in 4 tokens. P.27 repeats the extraction (second `qokor`), showing the cycle RETURNING.

The oscillation is the recipe's central operation: repeatedly extract from the herb, settle into fluid, extract again, settle again, until the volatile fraction is fully transferred and stabilized.

#### Verification Density

| Token | Paragraph | Position |
|-------|----------|----------|
| chodaiin | P.8 | First verification — after 8 para setup |
| shodaiin | P.13 | Transition verified |
| shodaiin | P.18 | Transition verified + fixed |
| daiin | P.21 | Standalone verification |
| daiin | P.22 | Crystal formation verified |
| shodaiin | P.30 | Late transition verified |

**6 daiin/saiin in 31 paragraphs = 0.19/para.** LOWEST verification density in the pharmaceutical section. Lower than even the jar recipes (0.5/para). The herb recipe trusts its oscillation process — it barely checks. The foldout's ~2.0/para verification intensity exists so that HERE, at the practical herb recipe level, almost no verification is needed.

#### d-Prefix (Fixation) Density

Fixation tokens appear in: P.1 (qotodain), P.3 (dsho, dal, dalody, dam, dal = 5 tokens), P.4 (qokchddal, s-chodain), P.5 (diiird, otodar-chodain), P.7 (cheodoin), P.8 (chodaiin, odar), P.11 (sodam), P.15 (shodal, dol, cheodam), P.21 (dol, daiin), P.22 (daiin), P.28 (odol, chodain), P.29 (dain), P.32 (dol).

~25 d-prefix tokens across 31 paragraphs. BUT they cluster: P.3 alone has 5 (the fixation manifesto), P.4-P.5 have 4 (the extraction-fixation zone). Fixation is FRONT-LOADED — the recipe fixes heavily at the start, then relies on the oscillation to maintain stability.

#### Bare Morphemes

| Morpheme | Count | Paragraphs |
|----------|-------|-----------|
| `s` (salt) | 8 | P.1, P.2(×2), P.6(×2), P.7, P.19, P.28 |
| `cho` (volatile-heat) | 1 | P.6 |
| `l` (layer/structure) | 1 | P.17 |
| `ch` (spirit) | 1 | P.25 |
| `r` (source) | — | (appears in P.2 hyphenated compound) |

EIGHT bare `s` tokens. The herb recipe uses salt as its primary intervention tool — a punctuation mark between operations. Every few paragraphs: SALT. This is consistent with spagyric herb processing where salt is repeatedly applied to extract, preserve, and structure the plant material.

#### sh- (Transition) Density

Transition tokens appear in nearly every paragraph: shodaiin (×3), shol (×5), shor (×2), shody (×3), sheo- (×5), dsho, shotol, sheoeer, shcthy, sheoky... 

**~25 sh- tokens across 31 paragraphs ≈ 0.8 per paragraph.** The herb recipe is TRANSITION-DOMINATED. Compare the foldout which was verification-dominated (daiin-heavy) and the jar recipes which were extraction-dominated (qo-heavy). The herb recipe's character is defined by constant transition — the material is always MOVING between states, never resting. This IS the oscillation: perpetual transition.

#### F-Atom / cfh- / cph- Clusters

**ABSENT.** No f-atom tokens, no cfh- or cph- clusters appear on f93r. The biological growth principle is not invoked in this herb recipe. This makes sense: the herb is the RAW INPUT. It has not yet been processed by the pharmaceutical machine. The F-atom appears only in the manufactured product, not the raw material. The herb recipe extracts FROM the plant; the foldout and jar recipes work ON the extract. The F-atom lives in the extract, not the herb.

#### Terminal Seal: schos=

`s-cho-s` = salt-volatile_heat-salt.

This is a STRUCTURAL FORMULA describing the finished product:

```
SALT → VOLATILE-HEAT → SALT
  (outer)  (active core)  (outer)
```

A salt-encapsulated volatile extract. The terminal seal IS the product description. It names what sits in the jar: the plant's volatile-heat fraction, preserved between two applications of the salt principle.

Compare previous terminals:
- f89r1: `chodaiin=` (energy verified)
- f89r2: `dair=` (root fixed)
- f89v1: `choldy=` (fluid state fixed)
- f89v2: `darails=` (root + complete + fluid + salt)
- f90r1: `okam=` (phase-shift into vessel)
- f90v2: `okeey=` (phase-shift at sensitivity)
- f93r: `schos=` (salt-volatile-salt sandwich)

The herb recipe terminal is the first to describe a PHYSICAL STRUCTURE rather than a process state. It names the product's architecture.

---

### What F93R Tells Us

1. **The Bridge Works Both Ways.** F93r connects the herbal section (raw plants) to the pharmaceutical section (processed medicines) by showing BOTH the plant and its processing protocol. The VML operates identically whether describing herbal inputs or pharmaceutical outputs — the same morphological system, the same operational prefixes, the same grammatical structure.

2. **Oscillation is the Herb Recipe's Engine.** Where the foldout uses verification (daiin) and the jar recipes use extraction (qo-), the herb recipe uses transition (sh-). The material is ALWAYS in transition, oscillating between states, never at rest until the terminal seal.

3. **Salt as Distributed Intervention.** Eight bare `s` tokens scattered across the recipe. Salt isn't a final endpoint — it's a tool applied throughout processing. This matches spagyric practice where salt (ash, mineral residue) is repeatedly introduced during plant extraction.

4. **The Fixation Manifesto (P.3).** 78% d-density in one paragraph. The recipe FRONT-LOADS fixation: fix everything at the start, then let the oscillation run. This is the opposite of the foldout, which builds toward fixation progressively.

5. **No F-Atom.** The biological growth principle is absent from the raw herb recipe. It appears only in processed products. The F-atom is something MANUFACTURED, not something extracted.

6. **Product as Structure.** The terminal seal `schos=` names a physical architecture: salt-volatile-salt. The recipe doesn't end with a process verification — it ends with a product specification.

7. **Minimum Verification, Maximum Transition.** 0.19 daiin/para (lowest in pharmaceutical section) but 0.8 sh-/para (transition density). The herb recipe WORKS more than it CHECKS. The oscillation IS the quality control — if the material stabilizes through repeated cycling, it's done.

---

**F93R COMPLETE.**

**NEXT: F93V — Refinement Companion: Clean Clamped Endpoint**

## FOLIO F93V — REFINEMENT COMPANION: CLEAN CLAMPED ENDPOINT

**Position:** Verso of f93r. Same bifolio, opposite side. The REFINEMENT stage following f93r's oscillation extraction.

**Structure:** 10 paragraphs, ~90 tokens. Average 9.0 tokens/paragraph. DENSE paragraphs — the inverse of f93r's 31 compressed paragraphs (avg 4.5). Same material, different architecture: oscillation (many short beats) → refinement (few thorough passes).

**Visual:** Continuation of f93r — the plant illustration carries across both sides of the bifolio.

### Architectural Contrast: f93r vs f93v

| Property | f93r (Recto) | f93v (Verso) |
|----------|-------------|-------------|
| Paragraphs | 31 | 10 |
| Total tokens | ~140 | ~90 |
| Avg tokens/para | 4.5 | 9.0 |
| Character | Oscillation — rapid cycling | Refinement — thorough passes |
| sh- density | High (transition-dominated) | Moderate |
| qo- density | Low (~0.16/para) | High (1.2/para) |
| op- tokens | 1 | 4 (triple-op in P.1) |
| daiin density | 0.19/para | 0.7/para |
| Terminal | schos= (salt-volatile-salt) | scheeol= (salt-double-e-fluid) |

The recto EXTRACTS through oscillation. The verso REFINES through concentrated processing. Together they form a complete bifolio recipe: extract → refine.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

**P.1 (10 tokens): GALLOWS OPENER — Triple Projection**
`porsheody.qoteeo.qosho.cphy.opchody.opor.opchy.otchdal.or.shodaiin-`

- `porsheody` = p(project) + or(source) + she(transition-essence) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). Project from source through active essence-transition heat-fixation. GALLOWS OPENER with p-prefix. Compare f93r's k-prefix opener (contain). The extraction contains; the refinement PROJECTS.
- `qoteeo` = qo(transmute) + tee(temporal-double-e) + o(heat). Transmute through temporal double-e heat.
- `qosho` = qo(transmute) + sh(transition) + o(heat). Transmute the transition. Second qo-.
- `cphy` = cph- cluster + y(active). **CPH- TOKEN.** First cph- in the plant-recipe section. Appears WITHOUT F-atom companion. The herb provides the cph- substrate; the pharmaceutical process adds the F-atom later.
- `opchody` = op(project) + cho(volatile-heat) + dy(fixed). Project volatile heat fixed. First op-.
- `opor` = op(project) + or(source). Project from source. Second op-.
- `opchy` = op(project) + ch(volatile) + y(active). Project active volatile. Third op-.
- `otchdal` = ot(temporal-heat) + ch(volatile) + d(fix) + al(structure). Temporal heat fixes volatile into structure.
- `or` = o(heat) + r(source). Heat source.
- `shodaiin` = TRANSITION VERIFIED.

TRIPLE `op-` = triple projection. The refinement drives material OUTWARD three times in its opener. Plus TWO qo- transmutations and a shodaiin verification. Maximum intensity opening.

**P.2 (9 tokens): TRIPLE TRANSMUTATION CASCADE**
`yteeody.qotody.qotchol.qocthody.ytey.oky.daiin.dar.cthom-`

THREE sequential `qo-` transmutations:
1. `qotody` — transmute through temporal heat to fixation
2. `qotchol` — transmute energy-volatile to fluid
3. `qocthody` — transmute through conduit with active heat-fixation

Each targets a different aspect: (1) temporal, (2) material, (3) infrastructure. Then `oky` phase-shift, `daiin` verification, `dar` deep fixation, `cthom` into vessel.

P.2 is a complete refinement cycle in miniature: transmute³ → verify → fix → store.

**P.3 (10 tokens): DOUBLE VERIFICATION + CRYSTALLIZATION**
`dchos.chody.qockhol.oky.cheodaiin.oty.daiin.otal.dair.akal-`

Opens with `dchos` — fix volatile heat WITH SALT. DOUBLE VERIFICATION: `cheodaiin` (volatile essence verified) + standalone `daiin`. Two independent checks.

Closes with `dair.akal` — fix-complete-to-root + CRYSTAL-STRUCTURE. The material has crystallized. Same endpoint as f93r's P.22 (`chakal`) but more specific: pure crystal-structure without volatile mediation.

**P.4 (10 tokens): DOUBLE EXTRACTION WITH DOUBLED `chol`**
`sol.shol.shdchy.qokchol.qokchody.chol.chol.cthy.ykchy.dar-`

Two `qok-` extractions (body-volatile → fluid, body-volatile → fixation). DOUBLED `chol.chol` — volatile fluid named twice as emphasis. This is SECONDARY EXTRACTION — going back to the herb for what the oscillation didn't fully capture.

**P.5 (9 tokens): COMPOSITE VERIFICATION-FIXATION**
`tshoky.cthody.qotchol.ckhol.dchom.s.olo.oteos.chodaiindy-`

Terminal token `chodaiindy` = volatile-heat VERIFIED and FIXED in one word. Verification and fixation FUSED — the refinement is confident enough to check and lock simultaneously. One bare `s` (salt) — the only one on f93v (vs. eight on f93r).

**P.6 (9 tokens): SPIRIT AT DOUBLE-E**
`ytchol.ckhol.qochocthy.ctha.chkeey.cthodys.dar.she.qokam-`

Key token: `chkeey` = spirit-body at DOUBLE-E sensitivity active. The body carries spirit at elevated sensitivity — the spagyric goal. Bare `she` (transition-essence) as imperative. Terminal `qokam` — extract body to vessel.

**P.7 (8 tokens): DOUBLE VERIFICATION + TRIPLE DOUBLE-E**
`oees.ckheody.ockheey.koldy.tchodaiin.ctheos.shodaiin.qokeeam-`

THREE double-e tokens: `oees` (heat-double-e-salt), `ockheey` (heat-valve-double-e), `qokeeam` (extract-body-double-e-vessel). DOUBLE VERIFICATION: `tchodaiin` + `shodaiin`. The refinement hits peak concentration — maximum sensitivity AND maximum verification in one paragraph.

`qokeeam` closes: extract body at double-e into vessel. Maximum care for the final extraction step.

**P.8 (11 tokens): COMPREHENSIVE FIXATION — Longest Paragraph**
`dcho.chody.teol.sheol.cheeol.dair.okchey.cthey.dsheom.okeey.dama-`

11 tokens — densest paragraph on f93v. FOUR d-prefix fixation tokens (dcho, dair, dsheom, dama). FOUR fluid tokens (teol, sheol, cheeol + fluid references). TWO ok- phase-shifts (okchey, okeey). Everything in fluid, everything being fixed and phase-shifted. The refinement's equivalent of f93r's P.3 fixation manifesto — but INTEGRATING phase-shifting with fixation rather than treating them separately.

**P.9 (10 tokens): TRIPLE-E CLIMAX + DOUBLE ROOT SEAL**
`odeeeodl.cheodar.oksho.chody.okchey.cthol.oly.ytchol.sar.dar-`

**`odeeeodl` — TRIPLE-E TOKEN.** Structure: o-d-eee-od-l = heat → fix → MAXIMUM SENSITIVITY → fix → structure. Symmetrical: the triple-e is CAGED between fixation brackets. The recipe knows maximum sensitivity is unstable and locks it in place.

First triple-e in the plant-recipe section. Compare f90v1 (triple-e page in jar recipes). The refinement reaches MAXIMUM SENSITIVITY in its penultimate paragraph.

Closes with `sar.dar` — DOUBLE ROOT SEAL. Salt-to-root THEN fix-to-root. Both structural principles reach maximum depth simultaneously. The pre-terminal lock.

**P.10 (4 tokens): TERMINAL SEAL**
`ychol.chs.ckhy.scheeol=`

- `ychol` = receptive volatile fluid. Product state.
- `chs` = spirit-salt. Two characters: volatile has become salt-bound.
- `ckhy` = valve active. Product flows.
- `scheeol=` = SALT-VOLATILE-DOUBLE-E-FLUID. TERMINAL.

Terminal structure: s → ch → ee → ol = salt → volatile → sensitivity → fluid.

A GRADIENT terminal — from structural (salt) through active (volatile) through sensitive (double-e) to medium (fluid). The product is a flowing salt-volatile preparation at elevated sensitivity. Compare f93r's `schos=` (salt-volatile-salt sandwich = stored). F93v produces an ACTIVE flowing preparation; f93r produced a STORED encapsulated extract.

---

### CROSS-FOLIO PATTERNS

#### Verification Recovery Curve

| Folio | daiin/para | Phase |
|-------|-----------|-------|
| f89r foldout | ~2.0 | Theory/machine |
| f90 jar recipes | ~0.5 | Practical recipes |
| f93r extraction | 0.19 | Oscillation extraction |
| f93v refinement | 0.7 | Concentrated refinement |

The curve: high (theory) → low (practice) → lowest (raw extraction) → recovering (refinement). As the material becomes more processed, verification RETURNS. The foldout verified intensively to establish trust. The jar recipes inherited that trust. The herb extraction barely verified (trusting the oscillation). The refinement RESTORES verification as the product approaches its final state.

#### Sensitivity Escalation

| Folio | ee tokens | eee tokens | Pattern |
|-------|----------|-----------|---------|
| f89r foldout | Moderate | Present (f90v1) | Distributed |
| f93r extraction | 3 (scattered) | 0 | Low, early |
| f93v refinement | 9 | 1 (odeeeodl) | Escalating → peak → stable |

F93v drives sensitivity from moderate through double-e saturation to triple-e peak, then stabilizes at double-e for the terminal. This is a SENSITIVITY ENVELOPE: ramp up → peak → settle. The foldout distributed sensitivity evenly; the refinement CONCENTRATES it into an escalating profile.

#### F-Atom Absence Across f93 Bifolio

No F-atom tokens on either f93r or f93v. The biological growth principle is absent from herb recipes. Confirmed interpretation: F-atom is a MANUFACTURED property, not a natural one. The herb provides raw material (including the cph- substrate); the pharmaceutical process adds the F-atom through its machine operations (foldout).

---

### F93 BIFOLIO SYNTHESIS

The f93r/f93v pair forms a complete pharmaceutical sub-unit:

**f93r (Oscillation Extraction):**
- 31 short paragraphs, transition-dominated (sh-)
- Places herb in heated fluid, oscillates (extract ↔ settle)
- Front-loads fixation (P.3 = 78% d-density)
- Minimal verification (0.19/para) — trusts the oscillation
- Eight bare salt punctuations — salt as distributed tool
- One anomalous token (diiird — triple-i)
- Terminal: `schos=` — salt-volatile-salt sandwich (STORED extract)

**f93v (Refinement):**
- 10 dense paragraphs, transmutation-dominated (qo-)
- Projects outward (triple op-), transmutes intensively (12 qo-)
- Escalates sensitivity (double-e → triple-e → double-e)
- Recovers verification (0.7/para) — checks more as product matures
- One bare salt — salt intervention mostly complete
- One cph- token (cphy) — substrate without F-atom activation
- Terminal: `scheeol=` — salt-volatile-double-e-fluid (ACTIVE preparation)

**Together:** raw herb → oscillation extraction → salt-encapsulated extract → concentrated refinement → active preparation at elevated sensitivity. A complete manufacturing pipeline on one bifolio.

---

**F93 BIFOLIO COMPLETE.**

**NEXT: F94R — Stability-First Herbal: Carrier Frame**

## FOLIO F94R — STABILITY-FIRST HERBAL: CARRIER FRAME

**Position:** First folio of f94 bifolio. Plant-Recipe Hybrid.

**Structure:** 8 main paragraphs (P.1-P.8) + 1 terminal label (T.9). ~81 tokens. Average ~9 tokens/para. Dense paragraphs.

**Visual:** Plant with structured carrier-building protocol — establish the framework before adding active ingredients.

### THE VERIFICATION PHENOMENON

The defining feature of f94r: HIGHEST verification density in the plant-recipe section, matching the foldout.

| Para | aiin-class tokens | Count |
|------|------------------|-------|
| P.1 | chedaiin, daiin, aiin | 3 |
| P.2 | okaiin, daiir, olaiin | 3 |
| P.3 | — | 0 |
| P.4 | chedaiin | 1 |
| P.5 | daiin, olkaiin, ykaiin, otaiin | 4 |
| P.6 | saiin, chckhaiin | 2 |
| P.7 | oraiin, olkaiin | 2 |
| P.8 | qokaiin, osaiin | 2 |
| **Total** | | **17** |

**17 aiin-class tokens in 8 paragraphs = 2.1/para.** Matches the foldout's ~2.0. The stability-first recipe verifies as intensively as the universal machine because building a carrier frame requires absolute precision.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

**P.1 (10 tokens): TRIPLE VERIFICATION OPENER**
`tchdy.opainr.chedaiin.dsheedy.qopchedal.keo.daiin.otal.aiin.oar-`

Opens with `tchdy` = energy-volatile FIXED. Stability-first: fixation is the first word. `opainr` projects complete to root. Then THREE daiin-class tokens: `chedaiin` (volatile essence verified), `daiin` (general verification), `aiin` (bare verification — the check ITSELF verified).

Key token: `qopchedal` — SIX-MORPHEME MEGA-TOKEN: qo(transmute) + p(project) + che(volatile-essence) + d(fix) + al(structure). The entire carrier-building operation in one word.

TRIPLE VERIFICATION in the opening paragraph. The stability-first recipe triple-checks before anything else happens.

**P.2 (11 tokens): PHASE-SHIFT SATURATION**
`dor.cheody.okaiin.odar.okal.okair.oky.daiir.qotar.okar.olaiin-`

FIVE ok- (phase-shift) tokens: okaiin, okal, okair, oky, okar. Each shifts the carrier frame into a different structural configuration — building the crystal lattice layer by layer through repeated phase transitions.

Three verification tokens (okaiin, daiir, olaiin) check phase shifts at beginning, middle, and end. The lattice is verified as it's built.

**P.3 (10 tokens): FOUR-TARGET EXTRACTION**
`todal.cholky.qokal.shdy.qoky.otody.qokol.chey.qokair.opary-`

FOUR `qok-` extractions targeting four different destinations:
1. `qokal` — extract body to structure
2. `qoky` — extract body active
3. `qokol` — extract body to fluid
4. `qokair` — extract body complete to root

ZERO verification. After P.1-P.2's intensive checking, the extraction trusts the framework and works without checking. The carrier is KNOWN GOOD; now fill it.

`cholky` = volatile-heat layers body active. LAYERED BODY construction — the carrier is built in layers.

**P.4 (10 tokens): FOUR-COMPONENT LOCKDOWN**
`shor.olkeedy.olkchdy.cheedy.kalchdy.chedaiin.or.chol.kar.am-`

FOUR consecutive -dy (fixed) tokens lock four different components:
1. `olkeedy` — fluid body at double-e fixed
2. `olkchdy` — fluid body volatile fixed
3. `cheedy` — volatile double-essence fixed
4. `kalchdy` — body structural volatile fixed

Every variable LOCKED. The carrier frame is rigid. Then `chedaiin` — volatile essence verified. `kar.am` — body to root, into vessel.

**P.5 (9 tokens): QUADRUPLE VERIFICATION**
`daiin.chekar.olkaiin.olkeody.ykaiin.otaiin.dar.okeedy.ykaro-`

FOUR aiin-class tokens verifying four different systems:
1. `daiin` — general verification
2. `olkaiin` — fluid body verified
3. `ykaiin` — moist body verified
4. `otaiin` — temporal heat verified

The most verification-intensive paragraph in the entire pharmaceutical section. Four independent checks from four different angles confirm the carrier frame's stability. The frame is PROVEN STABLE before the next step.

**P.6 (10 tokens): F-ATOM ACTIVATION**
`saiin.choky.qotchdy.otely.chedy.dal.dy.chckhaiin.chk.qof-`

Opens with `saiin` — SALT VERIFIED. Even the salt is checked.

`chckhaiin` — SPIRIT-VALVE VERIFIED. The spiritual pathway's control valve is independently checked before adding the active ingredient.

`chk` = spirit-body. Two characters: the spirit IS IN the body.

**`qof` = qo(transmute) + f(F-ATOM). TRANSMUTE THE F-ATOM.**

First F-atom token in the plant-recipe section. Position: paragraph 6 of 8 = 75% through the recipe. The F-atom is the LAST addition — the carrier frame is built, verified, phase-shifted, verified again, extraction-loaded, locked, quadruple-verified, salt-verified, and spirit-valve-verified BEFORE the growth principle is added.

This confirms the manufacturing sequence:
1. Build carrier frame (P.1-P.5) — 62% of recipe
2. Activate with F-atom (P.6) — the moment
3. Project and seal (P.7-P.8) — 25% of recipe

**P.7 (9 tokens): PROJECTION TO VESSEL**
`pchedar.oraiin.cheor.kas.or.als.oxockhy.olkaiin.am-`

Gallows `p-` opener: `pchedar` projects volatile essence fixed to root. `oraiin` — heat-source verified. `kas` and `als` name the body components: body-salt and structural-salt. The carrier's salt infrastructure is identified. Terminal `am` — into vessel.

`oxockhy` — anomalous x-glyph. Rare character `x` appears; possible variant or special marker.

**P.8 (9 tokens): TERMINAL — dam=**
`yty.qokaiin.ykal.chdy.qoky.osaiin.chy.kaidy.dam=`

`qokaiin` — extract body VERIFIED. Final extraction confirmed. `osaiin` = heat + salt-verification. `kaidy` = body complete fixed.

**Terminal: `dam=`** — d(fix) + am(vessel). FIX INTO VESSEL.

The simplest terminal in the pharmaceutical section. Two morphemes. The carrier frame doesn't need elaborate closure — it IS the container. It seals itself.

**T.9 (3 tokens): LABEL**
`otar.chdy.dytchdy=`

Terminal label: temporal-heat-root, spirit-fixed, double-fix-energy-volatile-fixed. Recipe identification tag.

---

### CROSS-RECIPE PATTERNS

#### Verification Recovery Curve (Updated)

| Folio | daiin/para | Context |
|-------|-----------|---------|
| f89r foldout | ~2.0 | Universal machine (theory) |
| f90 jar recipes | ~0.5 | Practical recipes (trust inherited) |
| f93r extraction | 0.19 | Oscillation (trusts the process) |
| f93v refinement | 0.7 | Refinement (recovering verification) |
| **f94r carrier** | **2.1** | **Framework building (maximum precision)** |

The carrier frame verifies MORE than the foldout. Building the pharmaceutical container requires even more checking than defining the universal process.

#### F-Atom Manufacturing Sequence (Confirmed)

1. Herb provides raw material + cph- substrate (f93r/f93v)
2. Carrier frame is built from herb components (f94r P.1-P.5)
3. F-atom is TRANSMUTED INTO the carrier (f94r P.6: `qof`)
4. Product is sealed (f94r P.7-P.8)

The F-atom is not extracted FROM the herb. It is MANUFACTURED and ADDED TO the carrier. `qof` is the activation moment.

#### Terminal Progression

| Folio | Terminal | Complexity | Product |
|-------|---------|-----------|---------|
| f93r | schos= | 3 morphemes | Stored extract |
| f93v | scheeol= | 4 morphemes | Active preparation |
| f94r | dam= | 2 morphemes | Carrier framework |

Simplification: the more infrastructure-oriented the product, the simpler its seal.

**F94R COMPLETE.**

**NEXT: F94V — Two-Pass Herbal: Seal Then Re-Enter**

## FOLIO F94V — TWO-PASS HERBAL: SEAL THEN RE-ENTER

**Position:** Verso of f94r. Completes the f94 bifolio.

**Structure:** 12 paragraphs (P.1-P.12). ~95 tokens. Average ~7.9 tokens/para.

**Visual:** Two-stage processing diagram showing intermediate seal and re-entry.

### THE THREE-TERMINAL PHENOMENON

F94v contains THREE terminal `=` markers:
1. **P.4:** `okchy=` — FIRST SEAL (midstream)
2. **P.7:** `qokaiin=` — SECOND SEAL (checkpoint)
3. **P.12:** `okaiin=` — FINAL SEAL

No previous folio has had more than one `=` terminal. F94v has THREE. The title "Seal Then Re-Enter" is literal: the recipe SEALS its product, then REOPENS it for further processing, then seals it again.

This is the pharmaceutical equivalent of multi-stage processing — cook, cool, then cook again. The intermediate seal LOCKS intermediate progress so it can't degrade while the practitioner prepares for the next pass.

**Three-pass structure:**

| Pass | Paragraphs | Terminal | Tokens | Character |
|------|-----------|----------|--------|-----------|
| First pass | P.1-P.4 | okchy= | 32 | Essence-energy extraction |
| Second pass | P.5-P.7 | qokaiin= | 21 | Re-entry + extraction verification |
| Third pass | P.8-P.12 | okaiin= | 42 | Projection + final verification |

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

#### FIRST PASS (P.1-P.4): Essence-Energy Extraction

**P.1 (8 tokens): ENERGY-SALT OPENER**
`tshedy.chedar.char.qokchedy.okal.dar.opchackhy.oteedaiin-`

- `tshedy` = t(energy) + sh(transition) + e(essence) + dy(fixed). Energy-salt-transition with essence fixed. NOT a gallows opener — this recipe begins with ENERGY, not projection or containment.
- `chedar` = che(volatile-essence) + d(fix) + ar(root). Volatile essence fixed to root. Deep fixation immediately.
- `char` = ch(spirit) + ar(root). Spirit to root. Two tokens in a row reaching ROOT depth.
- `qokchedy` = qo(extract) + k(body) + che(volatile-essence) + dy(fixed). Extract body's volatile essence to fixation.
- `okal` = ok(phase-shift) + al(structure). Phase-shift to structure.
- `dar` = d(fix) + ar(root). Fix to root. THIRD root-reaching token.
- `opchackhy` = op(project) + ch(volatile) + ack(crystal) + h + y(active). Project volatile crystal active. The volatile fraction CRYSTALLIZES through projection.
- `oteedaiin` = ot(temporal-heat) + ee(double-e) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). Temporal heat at DOUBLE-E fixes and VERIFIES.

THREE root-depth tokens (chedar, char, dar) in one paragraph. This recipe drives DEEP immediately — it doesn't build a surface framework like f94r. It plunges to root on the first line.

`opchackhy` — volatile crystal through projection. Crystallization appears in the opener. Compare f93r where crystallization arrived at P.22 (72% through) and f94r where it was implicit. Here it's in paragraph ONE.

**P.2 (9 tokens): TEMPORAL-ESSENCE SATURATION**
`ol.teedy.oteey.qokeey.oteey.teedal.ykeedy.qota.raiin-`

- `ol` = fluid medium.
- `teedy` = t(temporal/energy) + ee(double-e) + dy(fixed). Temporal at double-e fixed.
- `oteey` = ot(temporal-heat) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Temporal heat at double-e active. #1.
- `qokeey` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Extract body at double-e active.
- `oteey` = ot(temporal-heat) + ee(double-e) + y(active). REPEATED — same token as above. #2.
- `teedal` = t(temporal/energy) + ee(double-e) + d(fix) + al(structure). Temporal double-e fixes structure.
- `ykeedy` = y(moist) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + dy(fixed). Moist body at double-e fixed.
- `qota` = qo(transmute) + t(temporal) + a. Transmute temporal.
- `raiin` = r(source/root) + aiin(verification). Root VERIFIED.

SIX double-e tokens in one paragraph: teedy, oteey, qokeey, oteey, teedal, ykeedy. DOUBLE-E SATURATION. Every operation runs at elevated sensitivity. The first pass operates ENTIRELY at double-e.

`oteey` appears TWICE — exact repetition. The temporal heat at double-e is so important it's STATED TWICE. Token doubling as emphasis.

**P.3 (8 tokens): SPIRIT VERIFICATION + SALT STRUCTURE**
`yshedy.chdaiin.otedy.sdal.tamdy.eedy.qokeey.tam-`

- `yshedy` = y(moist) + sh(transition) + e(essence) + dy(fixed). Moist transition essence fixed.
- `chdaiin` = ch(spirit) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). SPIRIT FIXED and VERIFIED.

- `tam` = t(temporal/energy) + am(vessel). Temporal vessel. Into vessel.

`eedy` — SENSITIVITY FIXED. Not just operating at double-e but LOCKING the sensitivity level. The recipe fixes its own sensitivity parameter. This is meta-pharmaceutical: controlling how sensitive the process itself is.

`sdal` — salt-fix-structure: three principles compressed into one 4-character token. The salt frame is built in one word.

**P.4 (7 tokens): FIRST TERMINAL — MIDSTREAM SEAL**

**FIRST SEAL: `okchy=`** — phase-shift volatile active. The first pass ends by PHASE-SHIFTING the volatile into its active state and SEALING IT THERE. The material is locked in an active volatile phase.

Compare all previous terminals which sealed with fixation (dam=), salt-encapsulation (schos=), or flowing states (scheeol=). This terminal seals an ACTIVE PHASE-SHIFT. The product is frozen mid-transition — deliberately held in an intermediate state so it can be RE-ENTERED.

#### SECOND PASS (P.5-P.7): Re-Entry and Verification

`chorchor` — DOUBLED TOKEN. cho(volatile-heat) + r(source), repeated. The volatile's source is emphatically identified — THIS is where the active material came from. The second pass RE-IDENTIFIES the source material before further extraction.

The second pass VERIFIES the first pass (tedaiin), then RE-EXTRACTS from it (qokshd, qokeal), identifies the source (chorchor), and loads to vessel (am).

FIVE ot- (temporal-heat) tokens: otar, otor, otchy, tody, oty. TEMPORAL-HEAT SATURATION. The second pass applies patient, sustained heat from multiple directions. The sealed product is being slowly, thoroughly heated to drive the second-pass extraction.

#### THIRD PASS (P.8-P.12): Projection + Final Verification

- `pchd` = p(project) + ch(volatile) + d(fix). Project volatile fixed. Second p-.

TRIPLE `p-` (projection) in one paragraph: pchedaiin, pchd, parar. The third pass PROJECTS three times — driving the product outward to its final configuration. Compare f93v's triple op-: same triple-projection pattern but using gallows `p` instead of `op`.

`cphedy` — CPH- CLUSTER WITH FIXATION. This is more developed than f93v's `cphy` (cph- alone). The cph- pharmaceutical marker is now ESSENCE-FIXED. The binding substrate from the herb (cphy) has been activated and locked (cphedy).

`parar` — PROJECT to DOUBLE ROOT. The root is named twice through projection. Maximum depth reached through the projecting principle. The product is DRIVEN to its deepest possible position.

**P.9 (9 tokens): COMPOSITE SENSITIVITY + SALT VERIFICATION**

- `ytar` = y(moist) + t(temporal) + ar(root). Moist temporal root.

- `oly` = ol(fluid) + y(active). Active fluid.

`ypchdair` — another six-morpheme mega-token like f94r's `qopchedal`. Six operational principles compressed into one word. The recipe's complexity is expressed through TOKEN DENSITY rather than paragraph length.

`okedy` → `okeedy` — SENSITIVITY ESCALATION within consecutive tokens. Phase-shift-essence-fixed steps up to phase-shift-DOUBLE-E-fixed. Single-e → double-e in one step. The recipe SHOWS its sensitivity increase by adjacent token comparison.

**P.10 (10 tokens): ROOT VERIFICATION SATURATION**

- `olair` = ol(fluid) + ai(complete) + r(root). Fluid complete to root.

FOUR root-targeting tokens: olair, tar, araiin, qodar, dar. Plus `araiin` — ROOT VERIFIED. The third pass drives EVERYTHING to root and then verifies the root itself. The deepest level is independently confirmed.

`qodar` — transmute-fix-root. Three principles (transmutation, fixation, root-depth) in one 5-character token. The final transmutation delivers fixation to maximum depth.

**P.11 (10 tokens): EXTRACTION CONCLUSION**

TWO verifications (todaiin, chetaiin), TWO extractions (qokar, qoky), fixation (chdy), structure (ykal), and a final phase-shift. The third pass's extraction sequence is nearing completion.

THREE `ch-` (spirit) tokens in the terminal paragraph: chcthy, chdy, chckhy. The final seal is a SPIRIT TRIPTYCH:
1. Spirit-conduit active (the channel works)
2. Spirit fixed (the channel is stable)
3. Spirit-valve active (the gate is open)

The product's spiritual pathway is fully operational — active conduit, stable fixation, open valve. The medicine can deliver its spiritual/volatile component. This IS the therapeutic mechanism: spirit flows through fixed conduit via active valve.

### PATTERN ANALYSIS

#### Three-Terminal Architecture

| Terminal | Token | Meaning | What's sealed |
|----------|-------|---------|--------------|
| First (P.4) | okchy= | Phase-shift volatile active | Active intermediate state |
| Second (P.7) | qokaiin= | Extract verified | Confirmed extraction |
| Third (P.12) | okaiin= | Phase-shift verified | Final verified product |

PROGRESSION: active state → verified extraction → verified phase-shift. Each seal locks a MORE REFINED product. The intermediate seals protect intermediate achievements.

The first and third seals both involve ok- (phase-shift), but the third ADDS verification (aiin). The product matures from "phase-shifted" to "phase-shift verified."

#### Verification Density

| Pass | Paragraphs | aiin tokens | Per para |
|------|-----------|------------|---------|
| First (P.1-P.4) | 4 | oteedaiin, raiin, chdaiin | 0.75 |
| Second (P.5-P.7) | 3 | tedaiin, qokaiin | 0.67 |
| Third (P.8-P.12) | 5 | pchedaiin, daiin, otaiiny, saiin, okchaiin, araiin, todaiin, chetaiin, daiin, okaiin | 2.0 |

The third pass verifies at FOLDOUT INTENSITY (2.0/para). Each pass verifies more than the last: 0.75 → 0.67 → 2.0. The final pass is where all the checking happens — the recipe saves its most intensive verification for the last stage.

#### Double-e Density

| Pass | ee tokens | Count |
|------|----------|-------|
| First | teedy, oteey(×2), qokeey, teedal, ykeedy, eedy, qokeey | 8 |
| Second | ycheeo | 1 |
| Third | oteey, okeedy, oteey | 3 |

EIGHT double-e tokens in the first pass alone (4 paragraphs). The first pass operates at MAXIMUM sensitivity — it's the precision pass. The second pass (re-entry) drops sensitivity. The third pass partially restores it. Sensitivity follows a different curve than verification.

#### cph- / F-Atom Tracking

- `cphedy` (P.8) — cph- cluster with essence fixed. More mature than f93v's `cphy`.
- `pchd` (P.8) — p + ch + d = project-volatile-fix. Possible related form.
- `ypchdair` (P.9) — y + p + ch + d + ai + r. Six-morpheme compound containing pch + d.

The cph- cluster is DEVELOPING across folios:
1. f93v: `cphy` — bare cph- active (substrate)
2. f94v: `cphedy` — cph- essence fixed (bound substrate)
3. f94v: `ypchdair` — pch-d within receptive compound (integrated)

The pharmaceutical binding marker evolves from raw (f93v) to fixed (f94v P.8) to fully integrated (f94v P.9). The plant-recipe hybrid section SHOWS the development of the cph- pattern from herb through processing.

#### -dy (Fixed) Suffix Density

Tokens ending in -dy: tshedy, chedar(implicit d), qokchedy, teedy, ykeedy, eedy, yshedy, otedy, tamdy, dshdy, kedy, qokchdy, okchdy, chedy, onchdy, cphedy, okedy, okeedy, otody, chdy(×many), *dy...

EXTREME -dy density. Nearly every paragraph has multiple -dy tokens. The "two-pass herbal" is FIXATION-OBSESSED — everything is being fixed at every stage. This makes sense for a "seal then re-enter" recipe: you must fix before sealing, fix after re-entering, fix before re-sealing.

---

### What F94V Tells Us

1. **Multi-Pass Processing is Structural.** Three terminal markers prove the recipe has three discrete stages, each sealed independently. This isn't just "keep processing until done" — it's "process, SEAL, re-enter, SEAL, finalize, SEAL." The intermediate seals are pharmaceutical quality gates.

2. **First Pass = Sensitivity.** Eight double-e tokens in four paragraphs. The first pass establishes the product at maximum sensitivity. Everything operates at double-e.

3. **Second Pass = Extraction Confirmation.** Only three paragraphs (P.5-P.7). The re-entry is brief — just confirm the extraction worked and re-seal. Three words in the terminal paragraph.

4. **Third Pass = Verification + Spirit.** Verification intensity explodes to 2.0/para. The final pass checks EVERYTHING. Terminal is a spirit triptych — conduit/fixed/valve — naming the product's delivery mechanism.

5. **cph- Development.** The pharmaceutical binding marker evolves from bare substrate (f93v) through fixed binding (f94v P.8) to integrated compound (f94v P.9). The plant-recipe section tracks the MATURATION of this marker.

6. **`chorchor` — Doubled Source Identification.** The second pass identifies its source material by REPEATING the source token. When you re-enter a sealed product, you must confirm WHAT you're working with.

7. **Sensitivity and Verification Are Inversely Distributed.** First pass: high sensitivity, moderate verification. Third pass: moderate sensitivity, high verification. The recipe is precise early (double-e) and careful late (daiin). You need precision to set up the product; you need verification to confirm the product.

---

### F94 BIFOLIO SYNTHESIS

**f94r (Stability-First Carrier Frame):**
- Builds framework first, adds F-atom (qof) at 75%
- Verification intensity 2.1/para (matches foldout)
- Phase-shift lattice construction (5 ok- in P.2)
- Terminal: dam= (simple vessel seal)

**f94v (Two-Pass Herbal):**
- THREE discrete processing passes with intermediate seals
- First pass: double-e saturation (8 ee tokens)
- Second pass: brief re-entry and extraction confirmation
- Third pass: triple projection, cph- development, spirit triptych terminal
- Terminal: okaiin= (phase-shift verified)

**Together:** The f94 bifolio shows TWO APPROACHES to pharmaceutical stability:
- f94r achieves stability through FRAMEWORK BUILDING (build container, then fill it)
- f94v achieves stability through ITERATIVE SEALING (process, seal, re-enter, seal again)

Both approaches serve the same goal — a stable pharmaceutical product — but use fundamentally different architectures. The carrier frame approach is structural; the two-pass approach is procedural.

---

**F94 BIFOLIO COMPLETE.**

**NEXT: F95R1 — Controlled Oscillation: Raise and Re-seat (Foldout Recipe)**

Note: F95 begins a FOLDOUT section — returning to the foldout recipe format last seen in f89. This may represent a second theoretical/machine-building section paralleling f89's foldout.

## FOLIO F95R1 — CONTROLLED OSCILLATION: RAISE AND RE-SEAT (Foldout Recipe)

**Position:** First sub-page of f95 FOLDOUT. Returns to foldout format after plant-recipe hybrid section (f93-f94). This is the SECOND FOLDOUT in the pharmaceutical section — the first was f89's Universal Processing Machine.

**Structure:** 11 paragraphs, ~96 tokens. Average 8.7 tokens/para. TWO terminal markers: `shdaly=` (P.5, midpoint) and `chckhal=` (P.11, final).

**Visual:** Foldout panel with oscillating process diagram and regular clamp intervals.

**Sub-section:** Foldout Recipe — multi-panel page displaying a complete processing protocol.

### TWO-TERMINAL ARCHITECTURE

Like f94v's three-terminal design, f95r1 has TWO seals dividing the folio into two passes:

| Pass | Paragraphs | Terminal | Character |
|------|-----------|----------|-----------|
| First (Setup + Initial Cycle) | P.1-P.5 | shdaly= | Vigorous-flow fix-structure active |
| Second (Advanced Processing) | P.6-P.11 | chckhal= | Spirit-valve-crystal-structure |

The first pass builds and seals a working state. The second pass advances through F-atom activation to a spirit-crystalline endpoint.

---

### THE F-ATOM REAPPEARS

Two F-atom tokens on this folio:

1. **P.1:** `ofaiin` = o(formative/F-atom) + f(vegetative) + aiin(verification). F-ATOM VERIFIED at the very start.
2. **P.6:** `qofaiin` = qo(transmute) + f(F-atom) + aiin(verification). F-ATOM TRANSMUTED and VERIFIED.

The F-atom appears in BOTH passes — first verified (P.1, setup), then transmuted and verified (P.6, second pass opener). The foldout recipe treats the F-atom as a CONTROLLED VARIABLE that's first checked, then actively transformed. Compare f94r's single `qof` (transmute F-atom, no verification). The foldout verifies the F-atom BOTH times it appears.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

#### FIRST PASS (P.1-P.5): Setup and Initial Cycling

**P.1 (9 tokens): BODY-SALT OPENER WITH F-ATOM**
`kshdor.chepeedy.ofaiin.ol.oldaiin.opshol.qokaiin.oty.odaiin-`

- `kshdor` = k(body) + sh(salt/transition) + d(fix) + or(source). Body-salt fixed from source. The herb body with its salt content, fixed, as starting material.
- `chepeedy` = che(volatile-essence) + p(project) + ee(double-e) + dy(fixed). Volatile essence PROJECTED at DOUBLE-E, fixed. The volatile is already at elevated sensitivity and projected outward. This is NOT a starting-from-scratch recipe — it begins with already-processed material.
- `ofaiin` = **F-ATOM VERIFIED.** The growth/vegetative principle is checked at the outset. The foldout recipe confirms the F-atom is present before beginning.
- `ol` = fluid medium.
- `oldaiin` = ol(fluid) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). FLUID FIXED and VERIFIED.
- `opshol` = op(project) + sh(vigorous-flow) + ol(fluid). Project vigorous-flow fluid. The fluid is driven outward vigorously.
- `qokaiin` = qo(extract) + k(body) + aiin(verification). EXTRACT BODY VERIFIED.
- `oty` = ot(temporal-heat) + y(active). Temporal heat active.
- `odaiin` = o(heat) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). HEAT-FIX VERIFIED.

FOUR aiin-class verifications in the opener: ofaiin, oldaiin, qokaiin, odaiin. QUADRUPLE VERIFICATION in P.1. The foldout recipe checks FOUR systems before proceeding: (1) F-atom, (2) fluid fixation, (3) extraction, (4) heat-fixation.

This MATCHES f94r's P.5 (quadruple verification) but appears in the FIRST paragraph. The foldout front-loads its verification to maximum intensity.

`chepeedy` — volatile essence PROJECTED at double-e. The material arriving at this foldout has ALREADY been processed (projected, at double-e sensitivity). This foldout works on INTERMEDIATE product, not raw herb. The plant-recipe hybrids (f93-f94) prepared the material; this foldout processes it further.

**P.2 (12 tokens): chdy SATURATION — The Spirit-Fixed Paragraph**
`ol.chdy.chdy.qokaiin.shdy.qokaiin.chdy.kal.chdy.qoty.oky.dan-`

- `ol` = fluid.
- `chdy` = ch(spirit) + dy(fixed). Spirit fixed. #1.
- `chdy` = Spirit fixed. #2.
- `qokaiin` = EXTRACT VERIFIED. #1.
- `shdy` = sh(vigorous-flow) + dy(fixed). Vigorous flow fixed.
- `qokaiin` = EXTRACT VERIFIED. #2.
- `chdy` = Spirit fixed. #3.
- `kal` = k(body) + al(structure). Body structure.
- `chdy` = Spirit fixed. #4.
- `qoty` = qo(transmute) + t(temporal) + y(active). Transmute temporal active.
- `oky` = ok(phase-shift) + y(active). Phase shift active.
- `dan` = d(fix) + an(cycle). Fix the cycle.

FOUR `chdy` tokens in one paragraph. Spirit-fixed is the DOMINANT STATE. The spirit channel is being locked from four positions — north, south, east, west of the process. Every step between extractions and transmutations FIXES THE SPIRIT.

DOUBLED `qokaiin` — extract-verified appearing twice. The extraction is checked, work continues, then checked AGAIN. This is the "raise and re-seat" pattern: raise (extract), re-seat (verify), raise again (extract), re-seat again (verify).

`dan` — FIX THE CYCLE. Not fix the product, fix the CYCLE ITSELF. The oscillation is being locked into its rhythm. This is meta-pharmaceutical: controlling the process's temporal pattern.

**P.3 (8 tokens): DOUBLED VOLATILE-ESSENCE VERIFICATION**
`teodaiin.oekeey.qokees.ody.chekaiin.chekaiin.chky.chaiin-`

- `teodaiin` = t(temporal/energy) + e(essence) + od(heat-fix) + aiin(verification). Temporal essence heat-fixed VERIFIED.
- `oekeey` = o(heat) + e(essence) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Heat-essence in body at double-e active.
- `qokees` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + s(salt). Extract body at double-e with salt. Sensitive salted extraction.
- `ody` = o(heat) + dy(fixed). Heat fixed.
- `chekaiin` = che(volatile-essence) + k(body) + aiin(verification). Volatile essence IN BODY VERIFIED. #1.
- `chekaiin` = EXACT REPEAT. Volatile essence in body VERIFIED AGAIN. #2.
- `chky` = ch(spirit) + k(body) + y(active). Spirit-body active.
- `chaiin` = ch(spirit) + aiin(verification). SPIRIT VERIFIED.

DOUBLED `chekaiin` — volatile essence in body verified TWICE. Exact token repetition. The recipe demands INDEPENDENT DOUBLE-CONFIRMATION that the volatile essence has been incorporated into the body. This is the oscillation's quality gate: the material only advances when TWO independent checks confirm the volatile-body integration.

THREE different verification targets: temporal-essence (teodaiin), volatile-essence-body (chekaiin ×2), spirit (chaiin). FOUR total verifications including the double.

**P.4 (4 tokens): COMPRESSED CHECKPOINT**
`ycheeokaiin.chy.kaiin.ly-`

- `ycheeokaiin` = y(moist) + ch(volatile) + ee(double-e) + ok(phase-shift) + aiin(verification). MEGA-TOKEN (12 characters): moist volatile at double-e phase-shifted and verified. SIX morphemes compressed into one word.
- `chy` = ch(spirit) + y(active). Spirit active.
- `kaiin` = k(body) + aiin(verification). Body VERIFIED.
- `ly` = l(layer) + y(active). Layer active.

`ycheeokaiin` — the longest single token on this folio. Moist-volatile-double_e-phase_shift-verified: the complete state of the material compressed into one word. Everything in a single check: is the moist volatile at double-e and phase-shifted? VERIFIED.

Only FOUR tokens but containing TWO verifications. The paragraph is a PURE CHECKPOINT — just checking and confirming. No operations, no transformations. Just: is everything still good? Yes.

**P.5 (5 tokens): FIRST TERMINAL — Structure Sealed**
`atar.chedy.tadaiin.qoky.shdaly=`

- `atar` = a + t(temporal) + ar(root). Temporal root (uncertain a-prefix).
- `chedy` = che(volatile-essence) + dy(fixed). Volatile essence fixed.
- `tadaiin` = t(temporal/energy) + a + d(fix) + aiin(verification). Temporal fixed VERIFIED.
- `qoky` = qo(extract) + k(body) + y(active). Extract body active.
- `shdaly=` = sh(vigorous-flow) + d(fix) + al(structure) + y(active). VIGOROUS-FLOW FIX-STRUCTURE ACTIVE. TERMINAL.

**FIRST SEAL: `shdaly=`** — vigorous flow that fixes structure, actively. The first pass ends by DYNAMICALLY FIXING the structure — not a static seal but an active, flowing fixation. The product is stabilized while still in motion. This IS the "re-seat" half of "raise and re-seat": the oscillation settles into a stable flowing state.
