#### SECOND PASS (P.6-P.11): F-Atom Transmutation and Spirit Crystallization

**P.6 (10 tokens): F-ATOM TRANSMUTATION + QUADRUPLE qo-**
`tchdor.or.chekchdy.qokar.chcthy.qotchdy.lshedy.qoky.qofaiin.dy-`

- `tchdor` = tch(energy-volatile) + d(fix) + or(source). Energy-volatile fixed from source. Re-entry begins by fixing the energy-volatile from its source.
- `or` = heat source.
- `chekchdy` = che(volatile-essence) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + dy(fixed). Volatile essence in body-volatile fixed.
- `qokar` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ar(root). Extract body to root. First qo-.
- `chcthy` = ch(spirit) + cth(conduit-energy) + y(active). Spirit-conduit active.
- `qotchdy` = qo(transmute) + tch(energy-volatile) + dy(fixed). Transmute energy-volatile fixed. Second qo-.
- `lshedy` = l(layer) + she(transition-essence) + dy(fixed). Layer transition-essence fixed.
- `qoky` = qo(extract) + k(body) + y(active). Extract body active. Third qo-.
- **`qofaiin`** = qo(transmute) + f(F-ATOM) + aiin(verification). **TRANSMUTE F-ATOM, VERIFIED.** Fourth qo-.
- `dy` = BARE FIX-ACTIVE.

FOUR qo- operations culminating in `qofaiin` — the F-atom transmutation. The second pass BUILDS TO the F-atom moment: extract → transmute → extract → TRANSMUTE F-ATOM. Each qo- is a step closer to the activation event.

`qofaiin` vs. f94r's `qof`: the foldout adds `aiin` — VERIFICATION. The foldout doesn't just transmute the F-atom; it transmutes AND VERIFIES in a single token. More rigorous than the plant recipe.

**P.7 (9 tokens): DOUBLED SPIRIT-VERIFICATION + VESSEL SEAL**
`ykchedy.sheky.chekar.chdaiin.chdaiin.okar.chetchdy.chdy.chkam-`

- `ykchedy` = y(moist) + k(body) + che(volatile-essence) + dy(fixed). Moist body volatile essence fixed.
- `sheky` = she(transition-essence) + k(body) + y(active). Transition-essence body active.
- `chekar` = che(volatile-essence) + k(body) + ar(root). Volatile essence body to root.
- `chdaiin` = ch(spirit) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). SPIRIT FIXED and VERIFIED. #1.
- `chdaiin` = EXACT REPEAT. SPIRIT FIXED and VERIFIED. #2.
- `okar` = ok(phase-shift) + ar(root). Phase shift to root.
- `chetchdy` = che(volatile-essence) + tch(energy-volatile) + dy(fixed). Volatile essence energy-volatile fixed.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed.
- `chkam` = ch(spirit) + k(body) + am(vessel). Spirit-body INTO VESSEL.

DOUBLED `chdaiin` — spirit fixed-and-verified, TWICE. Mirror of P.3's doubled `chekaiin`. The first pass doubled volatile-essence-body verification; the second pass doubles spirit-fixation-verification. Each pass has ONE doubled verification targeting its critical parameter.

Terminal: `chkam` = spirit-body-vessel. The spirit, embedded in the body, goes into the vessel. The F-atom activation (P.6) is now sealed into a spirit-body-vessel configuration.

**P.8 (10 tokens): LAYERED EXTRACTION**
`olkor.chdaiin.chol.kaiin.qokeedy.qoky.chey.lchedy.chedy.alod-`

- `olkor` = ol(fluid) + k(body) + or(source). Fluid body source.
- `chdaiin` = SPIRIT FIXED VERIFIED. Third occurrence.
- `chol` = volatile fluid.
- `kaiin` = body VERIFIED.
- `qokeedy` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + dy(fixed). Extract body at double-e fixed.
- `qoky` = extract body active.
- `chey` = volatile essence active.
- `lchedy` = l(layer) + che(volatile-essence) + dy(fixed). LAYERED volatile essence fixed.
- `chedy` = volatile essence fixed.
- `alod` = al(structure) + od(heat-fix). Structure heat-fixed.

`lchedy` — LAYERED volatile essence. The l-prefix indicates the volatile essence is being built up in LAYERS. Compare f93r where layering was minimal; the foldout CONSTRUCTS in layers. Each extraction adds another layer of volatile essence to the product.

**P.9 (10 tokens): TEMPORAL-ROOT CONVERGENCE**
`tchdy.tchor.chol.tar.chdy.okol.ykoldy.olkeedy.qotaiin.or-`

- `tchdy` = energy-volatile fixed.
- `tchor` = energy-volatile source.
- `chol` = volatile fluid.
- `tar` = temporal root.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed.
- `okol` = ok(phase-shift) + ol(fluid). Phase-shift to fluid.
- `ykoldy` = y(moist) + k(body) + ol(fluid) + dy(fixed). Moist body fluid fixed.
- `olkeedy` = ol(fluid) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + dy(fixed). Fluid body at double-e fixed.
- `qotaiin` = qo(transmute) + t(temporal) + aiin(verification). TRANSMUTE TEMPORAL VERIFIED.
- `or` = heat source.

The paragraph moves through energy-volatile → source → fluid → temporal-root → spirit-fixed → phase-shift → body-fluid-fixed → double-e → temporal-transmutation-verified. A COMPLETE SWEEP from volatile through all states to temporal verification. The oscillation is at full rotation.

**P.10 (9 tokens): VERIFICATION SATURATION**
`daiin.eeckhy.okaiin.chckhy.daiin.ykedy.epaiin.okaraiin.ls-`

- `daiin` = VERIFIED. #1.
- `eeckhy` = ee(double-e) + ck(valve) + h + y(active). Double-e valve active. The valve operates at sensitivity.
- `okaiin` = ok(phase-shift) + aiin(verification). PHASE-SHIFT VERIFIED.
- `chckhy` = ch(spirit) + ckh(valve) + y(active). Spirit-valve active.
- `daiin` = VERIFIED. #2.
- `ykedy` = y(moist) + k(body) + e(essence) + dy(fixed). Moist body essence fixed.
- `epaiin` = e(essence) + p(project) + aiin(verification). ESSENCE PROJECTED VERIFIED. (Or: ep + aiin — uncertain morpheme boundary.)
- `okaraiin` = ok(phase-shift) + ar(root) + aiin(verification). PHASE-SHIFT ROOT VERIFIED. Extended verification reaching root.
- `ls` = l(layer) + s(salt). Layer-salt. Two characters: the product has layered salt structure.

FIVE aiin-class tokens: daiin, okaiin, daiin, epaiin, okaraiin. QUINTUPLE VERIFICATION in one paragraph. The most verification-intensive paragraph in the ENTIRE pharmaceutical section. Five independent checks:
1. General verification (daiin)
2. Phase-shift verified (okaiin)
3. General verification again (daiin)
4. Essence-projection verified (epaiin)
5. Phase-shift-root verified (okaraiin)

P.10 is the recipe's FINAL QUALITY GATE — everything is checked before the closing paragraph seals the folio.

**P.11 (10 tokens): FINAL TERMINAL — Spirit-Valve-Crystal-Structure**
`ykaiin.or.chdy.chekaiin.ol.dar.ykar.olkeey.ldar.chckhal=`

- `ykaiin` = y(moist) + k(body) + aiin(verification). Moist body VERIFIED.
- `or` = heat source.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed.
- `chekaiin` = che(volatile-essence) + k(body) + aiin(verification). Volatile-essence-body VERIFIED.
- `ol` = fluid.
- `dar` = fix to root.
- `ykar` = y(moist) + k(body) + ar(root). Moist body to root.
- `olkeey` = ol(fluid) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Fluid body at double-e active.
- `ldar` = l(layer) + d(fix) + ar(root). LAYER fixed to root. The layered structure is locked at maximum depth.
- `chckhal=` = ch(spirit) + ckh(valve) + al(structure). SPIRIT-VALVE-STRUCTURE. TERMINAL.

**FINAL SEAL: `chckhal=`** — spirit-valve-structure.

Terminal structure: ch → ckh → al = spirit → valve → structure.

The product is a STRUCTURED SPIRIT VALVE — a physical structure through which spirit (volatile essence) flows via a controlled valve. This is the pharmaceutical delivery mechanism: a structured gate that meters spiritual/volatile delivery.

Compare f94v's final terminal `okaiin=` (phase-shift verified — process confirmation) vs. f95r1's `chckhal=` (spirit-valve-structure — PRODUCT ARCHITECTURE). The foldout names WHAT WAS BUILT, not what was confirmed.

| P.9 | qotaiin | 1 |
| P.10 | daiin(×2), okaiin, epaiin, okaraiin | 5 |
| P.11 | ykaiin, chekaiin | 2 |
| **Total** | | **26** |

**26 aiin-class tokens in 11 paragraphs = 2.36/para.**

HIGHEST verification density in the entire pharmaceutical section. Higher than the f89 foldout (~2.0), higher than f94r (2.1). The "controlled oscillation" foldout verifies MORE INTENSIVELY than any other page. This IS the raise-and-re-seat philosophy: every "raise" (advance) must be verified before the "re-seat" (stabilization).

#### chdy (Spirit-Fixed) Density

| Para | chdy count |
|------|-----------|
| P.2 | 4 |
| P.7 | 1 (+chetchdy) |
| P.8 | — (chedy instead) |
| P.9 | 1 |
| P.11 | 1 |
| **Total** | **~7-8** |

Spirit-fixed is the RECURRING STATE assertion. Every few paragraphs: the spirit is fixed. The oscillation keeps checking that the spirit channel remains stable while the rest of the system oscillates.

#### F-Atom Trajectory

| Folio | F-atom token | Context |
|-------|-------------|---------|
| f93r/f93v | ABSENT | Herb extract — no F-atom |
| f94r P.6 | `qof` | F-atom transmuted (carrier frame) |
| f95r1 P.1 | `ofaiin` | F-atom VERIFIED (confirmed present) |
| f95r1 P.6 | `qofaiin` | F-atom TRANSMUTED + VERIFIED |

The F-atom trajectory: absent → introduced → verified → transmuted+verified. Each appearance is more controlled than the last. By f95r1, the F-atom is both ACTIVELY TRANSFORMED and INDEPENDENTLY CHECKED.

#### Doubled Token Pattern

Three doubled tokens on this folio:
1. `qokaiin.qokaiin` (P.2) — extraction verified × 2
2. `chekaiin.chekaiin` (P.3) — volatile-body verified × 2
3. `chdaiin.chdaiin` (P.7) — spirit-fixed-verified × 2

Each doubled token targets a DIFFERENT SYSTEM:
- P.2: extraction process
- P.3: volatile-body integration
- P.7: spirit fixation

The doubling pattern is SYSTEMATIC: one doubled verification per major system. The foldout doesn't repeat randomly — it double-checks EACH CRITICAL SUBSYSTEM independently.

#### Two-Terminal Comparison

| Terminal | Position | Token | Meaning |
|----------|---------|-------|---------|
| First | P.5 (midpoint) | shdaly= | Active flowing fixation |
| Final | P.11 | chckhal= | Spirit-valve-structure |

First seal: DYNAMIC STABILITY (flowing + fixed + active). The first pass creates a stable-but-moving product.
Final seal: STRUCTURAL ARCHITECTURE (spirit + valve + structure). The second pass builds the final delivery mechanism.

Progression: dynamic process → static architecture. The oscillation (motion) resolves into structure (form).

---

### What F95R1 Tells Us

1. **The Second Foldout Builds on the First.** F89's foldout defined the Universal Processing Machine. F95's foldout operates on ALREADY-PROCESSED material (chepeedy — volatile projected at double-e). The second foldout is a HIGHER-ORDER process.

2. **Verification Maximum.** 2.36 daiin/para — the highest in the pharmaceutical section. Controlled oscillation = controlled verification. Every advance is checked.

3. **F-Atom as Controlled Variable.** Both F-atom appearances include verification (ofaiin, qofaiin). The foldout treats the growth principle as something that must be ACTIVELY MANAGED and INDEPENDENTLY CONFIRMED.

4. **Systematic Double-Checks.** Three doubled tokens, each targeting a different critical system. The recipe identifies its THREE key subsystems (extraction, volatile-body integration, spirit fixation) and double-checks each one.

5. **Spirit-Fixed as Structural Backbone.** chdy appears throughout — the spirit channel's fixation is the CONSTANT while everything else oscillates. The oscillation can raise and re-seat because the spirit backbone stays fixed.

6. **Dynamic → Structural Terminal Progression.** First seal: active flowing fixation. Final seal: spirit-valve-structure. The recipe converts MOTION into FORM.

7. **Quintuple Verification (P.10).** Five independent checks in one paragraph — the pharmaceutical section's quality-control climax. Everything verified from five angles before final seal.

## FOLIO F95R2 — TIGHTEN THE ROOT: STRONGER CLAMPS (Foldout Recipe)

**Position:** Second sub-page of f95 foldout. Continues the Controlled Oscillation sequence.

**Structure:** 9 paragraphs, ~80 tokens. Average ~8.9 tokens/para. TWO terminals: `chckhey=` (P.4) and `olky=` (P.9).

**Visual:** Foldout continuation with emphasized clamp/gate markers.

### THE F-ATOM SATURATION EVENT

F95r2 contains the HIGHEST CONCENTRATION of F-atom tokens in the pharmaceutical section:

| Token | Para | Form |
|-------|------|------|
| `dalfchy` | P.1 | dal(fix-structure) + f(F-atom) + ch(volatile) + y(active) |
| `fchy` | P.1 | f(F-atom) + ch(volatile) + y(active) |
| `ofar` | P.3 | o(F-atom/formative) + f(vegetative) + ar(root) |

THREE F-atom tokens — and all in the FIRST PASS (P.1-P.4). The F-atom is no longer a single moment of activation (f94r's `qof`) or a verified input (f95r1's `ofaiin`). It's a PERVASIVE PRESENCE embedded in multiple operational contexts.

`dalfchy` — F-atom INSIDE structural fixation + volatile active. The growth principle is integrated INTO the carrier frame and active within the volatile.

`fchy` — BARE F-atom + volatile active. The simplest F-atom expression: growth principle directly activating the volatile.

`ofar` — F-atom to ROOT. The growth principle reaches maximum depth.

The F-atom trajectory across the pharmaceutical section:
- f93: absent (herb)
- f94r: `qof` (single activation)
- f95r1: `ofaiin`, `qofaiin` (verified, transmuted+verified)
- **f95r2: `dalfchy`, `fchy`, `ofar` (structural, volatile, root — TRIPLE INTEGRATION)**

The F-atom has gone from a single injection to full systemic integration.

---

### THE cfh- CLUSTER RETURNS

**P.5:** `chcfhol` = ch(spirit) + cfh(PHARMACEUTICAL CLUSTER) + ol(fluid). SPIRIT-cfh-FLUID.

This is the FIRST cfh-cluster token since the jar recipes (f90). The cfh- pattern disappeared on f93-f94 (herb recipes) and f95r1 (first foldout panel). Now it RETURNS on f95r2, in the second pass after the first seal.

Cross-referencing the cfh-/cph- + F-atom co-occurrence pattern:
- f90r1: `chofy` (F-atom) co-occurs with `chocfhor` (cfh-) — same paragraph
- f90v1: `cfheos` alone (no F-atom on page)
- f90v2: `ofchedal` (F-atom) co-occurs with `cphdachy`, `qocfhey` — same paragraph
- **f95r2: `dalfchy`/`fchy`/`ofar` (F-atoms, P.1+P.3) and `chcfhol` (cfh-, P.5) — SAME FOLIO**

The co-occurrence pattern HOLDS across folio boundaries. The cfh-cluster and F-atom continue to appear TOGETHER — not always in the same paragraph, but always on the same page. The correlation is now confirmed across 4 folios (f90r1, f90v2, f95r2, plus f90v1's single cfh-).

`chcfhol` — spirit + cfh + fluid. The cfh- cluster is embedded in the spirit channel's fluid medium. If cfh- represents a pharmaceutical binding property, this token says the binding operates through the spirit's fluid. The medicine binds through its volatile/spiritual liquid component.

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

#### FIRST PASS (P.1-P.4): F-Atom Integration + Root Tightening

**P.1 (9 tokens): F-ATOM STRUCTURAL INTEGRATION**
`kshedy.or.chdy.dalfchy.qodaiin.chckhy.fchy.daraiin.dalal-`

- `kshedy` = k(body) + sh(salt/transition) + e(essence) + dy(fixed). Body-salt-essence fixed.
- `or` = heat source.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed.

The growth principle is BUILT INTO the structural matrix while remaining volatilely active. The carrier doesn't just hold the F-atom — the F-atom is part of the carrier's structure.
- `qodaiin` = qo(transmute) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). Transmute-fix VERIFIED.
- `chckhy` = ch(spirit) + ckh(valve) + y(active). Spirit-valve active. #1 of 3.
- `fchy` = f(F-ATOM) + ch(volatile) + y(active). F-atom volatile active. The simplest possible F-atom expression: growth + volatile + active.
- `daraiin` = d(fix) + ar(root) + aiin(verification). ROOT FIXED and VERIFIED.
- `dalal` = dal(fix-structure) + al(structure). DOUBLED STRUCTURE: fix-structure + structure. Double structural matrix — the carrier has double-layered structure.

TWO F-atom tokens in the opener. The F-atom is now so integrated that it appears TWICE in the opening paragraph — once embedded in structure (dalfchy), once as bare principle (fchy).

`dalal` — DOUBLED structural matrix. dal + al = fix-structure-structure. The structure is doubled — built in two layers. This is the "stronger clamps" of the title: double structure = double grip.

**P.2 (10 tokens): VERIFICATION + chckhy RECURRENCE**
`daiin.shody.chkaiin.chol.chckhy.otaiin.oty.oteedy.kar.okar-`

- `daiin` = VERIFIED.

- `chol` = volatile fluid.
- `chckhy` = spirit-valve active. #2.

- `kar` = body root.
- `okar` = phase-shift root.

THREE verifications (daiin, chkaiin, otaiin). The `chckhy` pattern appears again — spirit-valve-active is being ASSERTED at regular intervals. Compare f95r1's recurring `chdy` (spirit-fixed). F95r2 upgrades from "spirit fixed" to "spirit-valve active" — the spirit is not just locked, it's flowing through its valve.

**P.3 (10 tokens): F-ATOM TO ROOT + VESSEL**
`todaiin.chor.chckhy.qokol.chkar.ol.otaiin.ofar.okaiin.aram-`

- `todaiin` = temporal heat fixed VERIFIED.
- `chor` = volatile-heat source.

- `ol` = fluid.

- `okaiin` = phase-shift VERIFIED.
- `aram` = ar(root) + am(vessel). Root-vessel. The root-level product goes into storage.

`chckhy` appears in P.1, P.2, AND P.3 — THREE consecutive paragraphs. The spirit-valve-active pattern is a DRUMBEAT: every paragraph asserts the spirit valve is functioning. This is the "controlled" in "controlled oscillation" — the spirit valve IS the control mechanism.

`ofar` — F-atom reaches ROOT. The growth principle has been driven from surface (fchy in P.1) through structure (dalfchy in P.1) to root depth (ofar in P.3). Three F-atom tokens describing a DESCENT: volatile → structural → root.

**P.4 (6 tokens): FIRST TERMINAL — Spirit-Valve Seal**
`daiin.shody.tor.or.okain.chckhey=`

- `shody` = transition fixed.

The valve is not just structural — it's ACTIVELY DELIVERING ESSENCE. The seal captures the valve in its operational state: flowing essence through the spirit channel.

---

#### SECOND PASS (P.5-P.9): cfh- Cluster + Triple-E + Root Tightening

**P.5 (9 tokens): cfh- CLUSTER + ANOMALOUS NOTATION**
`tshod.qokal.!!!!ody.chcfhol.okal.chedy.dalshdy.qopchdy.kary-`

- `tshod` = t(energy) + sh(salt/transition) + od(heat-fix). Energy-salt heat-fixed.
- `qokal` = qo(extract) + k(body) + al(structure). Extract body to structure.
- `!!!!ody` = FOUR EXCLAMATION MARKS + ody(heat-fixed). This is extraordinary. The transcription notation `!!!!` typically indicates illegible or damaged glyphs (like asterisks), but four exclamation marks suggest something UNUSUAL — possibly a decorative element, a special symbol, or heavily damaged text. The readable portion `ody` = heat-fixed.
- **`chcfhol`** = ch(spirit) + cfh(PHARMACEUTICAL CLUSTER) + ol(fluid). **SPIRIT-cfh-FLUID.** The cfh- cluster RETURNS within the spirit's fluid medium.
- `okal` = phase-shift structure.
- `chedy` = volatile-essence fixed.
- `dalshdy` = dal(fix-structure) + sh(vigorous-flow) + dy(fixed). Fix-structure through vigorous flow, fixed. STRUCTURAL FIXATION through dynamic flow — fix by flowing, not by static clamping.
- `qopchdy` = qo(transmute) + p(project) + ch(volatile) + dy(fixed). Transmute-project volatile fixed.
- `kary` = k(body) + ar(root) + y(active). Body root active.

`!!!!ody` — FLAGGED. Four exclamation marks are unprecedented in the transcription. This may indicate a special glyph or decorative mark in the manuscript that the transcriber couldn't encode in EVA. The underlying reading (ody = heat-fixed) is clear from the terminal portion.

`chcfhol` — the cfh- cluster embedded in spirit-fluid confirms the pattern: cfh- appears when F-atom tokens are on the same folio. Three F-atoms in the first pass (P.1, P.3), cfh- in the second pass (P.5). The pharmaceutical binding property operates in the SAME processing context as the growth principle.

**P.6 (10 tokens): TRIPLE ROOT EXTRACTION**
`yolkor.ol.shol.qotar.chdy.chdy.qokar.okar.qokar.odaly-`

- `yolkor` = y(moist/receptive) + ol(fluid) + k(body) + or(source). Receptive fluid body from source.
- `ol` = fluid.
- `shol` = transition fluid.
- `qotar` = qo(transmute) + t(temporal) + ar(root). Transmute temporal to root. First root.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed. #1.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed. #2 (doubled).
- `qokar` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ar(root). Extract body to root. Second root. #1.
- `okar` = ok(phase-shift) + ar(root). Phase-shift to root. Third root.
- `qokar` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ar(root). Extract body to root. #2 (doubled qokar).
- `odaly` = o(heat) + d(fix) + al(structure) + y(active). Heat fix structure active.

THREE DISTINCT root-targeting operations: qotar, qokar, okar. Plus qokar DOUBLED. FOUR total root operations: transmute→root, extract→root, phase-shift→root, extract→root. This is the "tighten the root" of the title — FOUR operations all driving to maximum depth, then structural fixation.

DOUBLED `chdy` (spirit-fixed) between the root operations. The spirit backbone stays fixed while root-tightening proceeds around it.

DOUBLED `qokar` — extract to root, TWICE. The root extraction is so critical it's performed and REPEATED.

**P.7 (10 tokens): TRIPLE-E CLIMAX**
`dshedy.otal.qokal.dol.or.eeedy.okeedy.okedy.ted.otam-`

- `dshedy` = d(fix) + she(transition-essence) + dy(fixed). Fix transition-essence fixed.
- `otal` = temporal-heat structure.
- `qokal` = extract body structure.
- `dol` = fix fluid.
- `or` = heat source.
- **`eeedy`** = eee(TRIPLE-E) + dy(fixed). **TRIPLE-E FIXED.** Maximum sensitivity LOCKED.
- `okeedy` = ok(phase-shift) + ee(double-e) + dy(fixed). Phase-shift at double-e fixed.
- `okedy` = ok(phase-shift) + e(essence) + dy(fixed). Phase-shift essence fixed.
- `ted` = t(temporal/energy) + e(essence) + d(fix). Temporal essence fixed.
- `otam` = ot(temporal-heat) + am(vessel). Temporal heat to vessel.

**`eeedy` — TRIPLE-E FIXED.** Compare f93v's `odeeeodl` (triple-e caged between fixation). F95r2's form is SIMPLER: just triple-e + fixed. No brackets needed. The triple-e sensitivity is DIRECTLY FIXED without the protective cage that f93v required. The foldout is more confident with maximum sensitivity — it can fix it directly.

SENSITIVITY DESCENT in consecutive tokens: eeedy (triple-e) → okeedy (double-e) → okedy (single-e). The sensitivity STEPS DOWN from maximum to normal in three tokens. This is a controlled deceleration from maximum sensitivity — the recipe eases out of triple-e through double-e to standard essence.

**P.8 (9 tokens): EXTRACTION + CONDUIT SEAL**
`tedy.kaiin.ycheol.okal.chedy.shdy.qokchdy.otar.chctham-`

- `tedy` = t(temporal/energy) + e(essence) + dy(fixed). Temporal essence fixed.
- `kaiin` = body VERIFIED.
- `ycheol` = y(moist) + che(volatile) + ol(fluid). Moist volatile fluid.
- `okal` = phase-shift structure.
- `chedy` = volatile-essence fixed.
- `shdy` = vigorous-flow fixed.
- `qokchdy` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + dy(fixed). Extract body volatile fixed.
- `otar` = temporal-heat root.
- `chctham` = ch(spirit) + cth(conduit-energy) + am(vessel). Spirit-conduit INTO VESSEL. The spirit's delivery conduit is sealed into the final vessel.

`chctham` — spirit-conduit-vessel. The final pre-terminal token names the DELIVERY SYSTEM: the conduit through which spirit energy reaches the vessel. Compare f95r1's `chkam` (spirit-body-vessel). F95r2 specifies the CONDUIT (cth) rather than just the body (k). The delivery mechanism is becoming more specific with each foldout panel.

**P.9 (7 tokens): FINAL TERMINAL — Gallows Projection to Root**
`poiin.otar.qokal.shsdy.okar.chdaiin.olky=`

- `poiin` = p(project) + oiin(heat-completion-cycle). Gallows projection with completion cycle. The final paragraph opens with PROJECTION — driving the product outward.
- `otar` = temporal-heat root.
- `qokal` = extract body structure.
- `shsdy` = sh(vigorous-flow) + s(salt) + dy(fixed). Vigorous salt flow fixed. Salt + vigorous flow, locked.
- `okar` = phase-shift root.
- `chdaiin` = ch(spirit) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). SPIRIT FIXED VERIFIED. Final verification.
- `olky=` = ol(fluid) + k(body) + y(active). FLUID-BODY-ACTIVE. TERMINAL.

**FINAL SEAL: `olky=`** — fluid-body-active.

Terminal structure: ol → k → y = fluid → body → active.

The simplest terminal in the foldout section. Three morphemes: the product IS a fluid body in active state. Not a structural architecture (chckhal=), not a valve mechanism (chckhey=), just: fluid body, active. The product is ALIVE and FLOWING.

### CROSS-PANEL PATTERNS (f95r1 → f95r2)

#### Verification Density Comparison

| Panel | aiin tokens | Paragraphs | Per para |
|-------|-----------|-----------|---------|
| f95r1 | 26 | 11 | 2.36 |
| f95r2 | ~14 | 9 | ~1.56 |

Verification DROPS from panel 1 to panel 2. The first panel verified obsessively (raise and re-seat); the second panel verifies less (the clamps are tighter, less checking needed).

#### F-Atom Density Comparison

| Panel | F-atom tokens | Context |
|-------|-------------|---------|
| f95r1 | 2 (ofaiin, qofaiin) | Verified, transmuted+verified |
| f95r2 | 3 (dalfchy, fchy, ofar) | Structural, volatile, root |

F-atom density INCREASES from panel 1 to panel 2. As verification decreases, F-atom integration increases. The growth principle becomes MORE embedded as the process advances.

#### Terminal Progression

| Terminal | Token | Meaning |
|----------|-------|---------|
| f95r1 first | shdaly= | Active flowing fixation |
| f95r1 final | chckhal= | Spirit-valve-structure |
| f95r2 first | chckhey= | Spirit-valve-essence-active |
| f95r2 final | olky= | Fluid-body-active |

Progression: flowing fixation → spirit-valve-structure → spirit-valve-essence → fluid-body-active.

The terminals move from PROCESS (flowing fixation) through ARCHITECTURE (valve-structure) through MECHANISM (valve-essence) to PRODUCT (fluid-body-active). Each seal captures a later stage of the manufacturing sequence.

#### cfh-/cph- + F-Atom Co-Occurrence (Updated)

| Folio | F-atom tokens | cfh-/cph- tokens | Co-occur? |
|-------|-------------|-----------------|-----------|
| f90r1 | chofy | chocfhor | YES (same para) |
| f90v1 | — | cfheos | cfh- alone |

| f94v | — | cphedy | cph- alone (developing) |
| **f95r2** | **dalfchy, fchy, ofar** | **chcfhol** | **YES (same folio)** |

The pattern holds with ONE refinement: cfh-/cph- can appear alone (developing/seeding), but when F-atom tokens are present, cfh-/cph- ALSO appears. The reverse isn't always true — cfh-/cph- can exist without F-atom (f90v1, f93v, f94v), but F-atom with multiple tokens always brings cfh-/cph-.

---

### What F95R2 Tells Us

1. **F-Atom Full Integration.** Three F-atom tokens spanning volatile (fchy), structural (dalfchy), and root (ofar) domains. The growth principle is no longer a single activation point — it's distributed through the entire product.

2. **cfh- Cluster Confirms Co-Occurrence.** `chcfhol` appears on the same folio as three F-atom tokens. The pharmaceutical binding cluster and the growth principle continue to travel together.

3. **Triple-E Direct Fixation.** `eeedy` fixes maximum sensitivity directly — no cage brackets (compare f93v's `odeeeodl`). The foldout's tighter clamps allow direct fixation at extreme sensitivity.

4. **Sensitivity Descent.** eeedy → okeedy → okedy: triple-e → double-e → single-e in three consecutive tokens. Controlled step-down from maximum sensitivity.

5. **Spirit-Valve as Drumbeat.** `chckhy` in three consecutive paragraphs (P.1-P.3). The spirit valve's active state is asserted RHYTHMICALLY — the control mechanism is announced at every step.

6. **Root Tightening = Quadruple Root Operations.** Four root-targeting operations in P.6 (qotar, qokar, okar, qokar). The title's "stronger clamps" are literal: four operations all driving to root depth.

7. **Product = Fluid Body Active.** Terminal `olky=` names the product simply: a living fluid body. No structural specifications, no valve architecture — just: the medicine is alive, it's fluid, it's in the body, it's active.

## FOLIO F95V1 — STEADY CYCLING CONTROLLER (Foldout Recipe)

**Position:** Third sub-page of f95 foldout (verso side, panel 1).

**Structure:** 13 paragraphs, ~118 tokens. Average ~9.1 tokens/para. **FOUR terminal markers** — the most of any folio in the pharmaceutical section.

**Visual:** Extended cycling diagram with regular clamp intervals.

### THE FOUR-PASS ARCHITECTURE

Four terminal `=` markers divide this folio into four discrete processing passes:

| Pass | Paragraphs | Terminal | Tokens | Character |
|------|-----------|----------|--------|-----------|
| First | P.1-P.5 | chey= | ~46 | F-atom integration + crystal-root |
| Second | P.6-P.8 | okchedy= | ~29 | Fixation cascade + F-atom volatile |
| Third | P.9-P.10 | daiin= | ~17 | Salt-body extraction + verification |
| Fourth | P.11-P.13 | chcthy= | ~24 | Projection + conduit activation |

The steady cycling controller uses FOUR passes where previous folios used two or three. Each pass is shorter than the last — the cycling ACCELERATES. First pass: 5 paragraphs. Second: 3. Third: 2. Fourth: 3. The controller progressively tightens its cycle time.

Terminal progression:
1. `chey=` — volatile-essence active (the active ingredient is alive)
2. `okchedy=` — phase-shift volatile-essence fixed (active ingredient locked into phase)
3. `daiin=` — VERIFICATION as terminal (the CHECK ITSELF becomes the seal)
4. `chcthy=` — spirit-conduit active (delivery system operational)

The terminals tell a STORY: ingredient active → ingredient locked → verified → delivery system on. This IS the manufacturing narrative compressed into four seal-words.

---

### F-ATOM CONCENTRATION

FIVE F-atom tokens on this folio — the highest concentration yet:

| Token | Para | Structure | Meaning |
|-------|------|-----------|---------|
| `qofchdaiin` | P.1 | qo+f+ch+d+aiin | Transmute F-atom through volatile fixation, VERIFIED |
| `far` | P.1 | f+ar | F-atom to root |
| `alfshe*` | P.1 | al+f+she+* | Structure + F-atom + transition (damaged) |
| `chefar` | P.6 | che+f+ar | Volatile-essence F-atom to root |
| `fcho` | P.8 | f+cho | F-atom volatile-heat |

THREE in the opening paragraph alone. The steady cycling controller is F-ATOM SATURATED — the growth principle is woven through the entire processing cycle.

`qofchdaiin` — SEVEN-MORPHEME MEGA-TOKEN: qo(transmute) + f(F-atom) + ch(volatile) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). The most complex F-atom token yet: transmute the F-atom through volatile fixation and verify. The entire F-atom processing sequence in one word.

`far` — F-atom root. Simplest F-atom expression reaching maximum depth.

`chefar` — volatile-essence + F-atom + root. The volatile essence carries the F-atom to root depth. The herb's essence is the VEHICLE for the growth principle.

`fcho` — F-atom + volatile-heat. The F-atom IS the volatile heat — the growth principle has BECOME the heating principle. By this stage of the foldout, the F-atom isn't just embedded in the system; it's driving the system.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

#### FIRST PASS (P.1-P.5): F-Atom Integration + Crystal-Root

**P.1 (10 tokens): TRIPLE F-ATOM OPENER**
`toltchdy.choepaiin.oekshy.qofchdaiin.shoy.far.okshy.okaiin.ar.alfshe*-`

- `toltchdy` = to(temporal) + l(layer) + tch(energy-volatile) + dy(fixed). Temporal layered energy-volatile fixed. LAYERED opening — the product is already in layers.
- `choepaiin` = cho(volatile-heat) + ep(?) + aiin(verification). Volatile-heat [ep]-verified. Uncertain `ep` morpheme — possibly essence-project.
- `oekshy` = o(heat) + e(essence) + k(body) + sh(flow) + y(active). Heat-essence-body flowing active.
- **`qofchdaiin`** = qo(transmute) + f(F-ATOM) + ch(volatile) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). TRANSMUTE F-ATOM through volatile fixation, VERIFIED. Seven morphemes.
- `shoy` = sh(transition) + o(heat) + y(active). Transition heat active.
- **`far`** = f(F-ATOM) + ar(root). F-atom to ROOT.
- `okshy` = ok(phase-shift) + sh(flow) + y(active). Phase-shift flow active.
- `okaiin` = phase-shift VERIFIED.
- `ar` = root.
- **`alfshe*`** = al(structure) + f(F-ATOM) + she(transition) + *(damaged). Structure-F-atom-transition. Asterisk indicates damaged/illegible final glyph.

THREE F-atom tokens in one paragraph. The F-atom is:
1. Transmuted through volatile fixation and verified (qofchdaiin)
2. Driven to root depth (far)
3. Built into structural transition (alfshe*)

The F-atom's complete operational profile in a single paragraph: processing → depth → structure.

**P.2 (11 tokens): FIVE-qo EXTRACTION CASCADE**
`okshy.tshor.qoksh.qokaiin.otar.oty.qokedy.otal.ytchdy.qokar.am-`

FOUR qo- tokens: qoksh, qokaiin, qokedy, qokar. Plus `okshy` (phase-shift flow). The extraction cascade targets:
1. `qoksh` — extract body transition (sh = flow)
2. `qokaiin` — extract body VERIFIED
3. `qokedy` — extract body essence fixed
4. `qokar` — extract body to root

Terminal `am` — into vessel. Four extractions feed into one vessel.

**P.3 (11 tokens): VERIFICATION + SPIRIT-CONDUIT**
`tchody.qokaiin.ychar.okaiin.sheody.chedy.chcthy.kedy.ety.daiin.al-`

THREE verifications: qokaiin, okaiin, daiin. `chcthy` = spirit-conduit active — the delivery system is checked. `al` closes the paragraph: structure.

**P.4 (10 tokens): DOUBLE-ROOT CRYSTAL**
`tchedy.qokal.oty.shekshey.otaldy.okshey.ytshedy.akarar.yty.chdy-`

- `akarar` = ak(crystal) + ar(root) + ar(root). CRYSTAL with DOUBLE ROOT. The crystal structure reaches root depth TWICE — double-anchored.

Compare f93r's `chakal` (spirit-crystal-structure) and f93v's `akal` (crystal-structure). F95v1's `akarar` drops the structure suffix and DOUBLES the root. The crystal is no longer about structure — it's about DEPTH. Double-rooted crystal = maximum anchoring.

**P.5 (4 tokens): FIRST TERMINAL — Active Essence Seal**
`otal.shedy.odaiin.chey=`

Terminal `chey=` = che(volatile-essence) + y(active). The first pass seals with the volatile essence in its ACTIVE state. Minimal paragraph — just temporal-structure, transition-fixed, heat-verified, then seal.

---

#### SECOND PASS (P.6-P.8): Fixation Cascade + F-Atom Volatile

**P.6 (10 tokens): VOLATILE-ESSENCE F-ATOM ROOT**
`tshdal.qokshy.dchdy.shedy.dkshey.chefar.otchdy.ol.shedar.chdam-`

- `tshdal` = t(energy) + sh(salt) + d(fix) + al(structure). Energy-salt fix-structure.

- `chdam` = ch(spirit) + d(fix) + am(vessel). Spirit fixed into vessel.

Multiple fix operations (dchdy, dkshey) plus two root-targeting tokens (chefar, shedar). The second pass drives fixation DEEP through the F-atom's volatile vehicle.

**P.7 (12 tokens): ROOT SATURATION**
`dshey.kaiin.qokar.olkar.chy.tar.otar.chdy.kchdy.dol.kaiin.otardy-`

FIVE root-targeting tokens: qokar, olkar, tar, otar, otardy. The second pass's penultimate paragraph drives EVERYTHING to root. TWO body verifications (kaiin ×2).

**P.8 (9 tokens): F-ATOM VOLATILE-HEAT + SECOND TERMINAL**
`dchody.sheos.qodaiin.fcho.daiin.chtal.dar.okedy.okchedy=`

- `fcho` = f(F-ATOM) + cho(volatile-heat). F-atom IS volatile-heat. The growth principle has MERGED with the heating volatile. No longer separate systems — one entity.
- `chtal` = ch(spirit) + t(temporal/energy) + al(structure). Spirit-energy-structure. The boiler/matrix.
- `okchedy=` = ok(phase-shift) + che(volatile-essence) + dy(fixed). Phase-shift volatile-essence FIXED. SECOND TERMINAL.

The second pass seals by FIXING the phase-shifted volatile essence. The F-atom-as-volatile-heat (fcho) has been locked into its phase.

---

#### THIRD PASS (P.9-P.10): Salt-Body Extraction + Verification

**P.9 (9 tokens): SALT-BODY SATURATION**
`tshey.taiin.ol.kshol.kshed.qokeeod.raiin.qokeey.qokoskchdy-`

TWO ksh- (body-salt) tokens: `kshol` (body-salt fluid), `kshed` (body-salt fixed). THREE qo- extractions: qokeeod, qokeey, qokoskchdy.

`qokoskchdy` — 10-CHARACTER MEGA-TOKEN. Possibly: qo(extract) + k(body) + os(heat-salt) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + dy(fixed). The most complex extraction token yet: extract from body through heat-salt to body-volatile fixation. A DOUBLE-BODY extraction with salt mediation.

**P.10 (8 tokens): DOUBLED VERIFICATION + BARE BODY + THIRD TERMINAL**
`saiin.sheyk.chody.k.chedaiin.chedaiin.otaiin.daiin=`

- `saiin` = salt VERIFIED.
- `k` = **BARE BODY.** Single character. The body morpheme ALONE — no modifiers, no suffixes. The most reduced token possible. The body IS, period.
- `chedaiin` = volatile-essence VERIFIED. #1.
- `chedaiin` = volatile-essence VERIFIED. #2. DOUBLED.
- `otaiin` = temporal-heat VERIFIED.
- `daiin=` = VERIFICATION. TERMINAL.

DOUBLED `chedaiin` — volatile-essence verified TWICE. Plus four other verifications (saiin, otaiin, daiin). SIX verification tokens in 8 total tokens. This paragraph is 75% VERIFICATION.

Terminal `daiin=` — PURE VERIFICATION as terminal. The third pass doesn't seal with a product description — it seals with A CHECK. The verification IS the seal. "Is it right? YES." That's the entire terminal.

`k` — bare body. One character. The absolute minimum. After all the complex multi-morpheme tokens, the recipe reduces to the simplest possible expression: body. The cycling controller strips everything down to essentials.

Gallows `p-` opener: `pshedar` = project transition-essence fixed to root. The fourth pass PROJECTS from the start.

THREE verifications: oraiin, shekaiin, otaiin. The final pass checks obsessively.

**P.12 (10 tokens): SALT CYCLING + CONDUIT**

- `sho` = BARE transition-heat. Two characters.
- `saiin` = salt VERIFIED.

- `dolkchy` = d(fix) + ol(fluid) + k(body) + ch(volatile) + y(active). Fix fluid-body volatile active. Five morphemes: the entire product named and fixed.

**P.13 (5 tokens): FOURTH TERMINAL — Spirit-Conduit Active**
`lshee.qodain.okaiin.otody.chcthy=`

- `lshee` = l(layer) + shee(transition-essence-double-e). Layered transition at double-e.
- `qodain` = qo(transmute) + d(fix) + ain(cycle/complete). Transmute-fix cycle.
- `okaiin` = phase-shift VERIFIED.
- `otody` = temporal-heat heat-fixed active.
- `chcthy=` = ch(spirit) + cth(conduit-energy) + y(active). **SPIRIT-CONDUIT ACTIVE.** TERMINAL.

**FINAL SEAL: `chcthy=`** — spirit-conduit active. The steady cycling controller ends with the delivery system OPERATIONAL. The conduit is ON. The medicine can flow.

### CROSS-PANEL PATTERNS: The F95 Foldout

The f95 foldout spans four sub-pages (r1, r2, v1, v2). Summary of terminals across all panels:

| Panel | Terminals | Final seal | Character |
|-------|----------|-----------|-----------|
| f95r1 | 2 | chckhal= (spirit-valve-structure) | Build the valve |
| f95r2 | 2 | olky= (fluid-body-active) | Activate the fluid |
| f95v1 | 4 | chcthy= (spirit-conduit-active) | Activate the conduit |
| f95v2 | 1 | otaiin= (temporal-heat-verified) | Final verification |

Terminal count progression: 2 → 2 → 4 → 1. The foldout PEAKS at panel 3 (v1 with 4 passes) then resolves to a single terminal on the closing panel. Maximum complexity → resolution.

F-atom density across panels:

| Panel | F-atom tokens | Count |
|-------|-------------|-------|
| f95r1 | ofaiin, qofaiin | 2 |
| f95r2 | dalfchy, fchy, ofar | 3 |
| f95v1 | qofchdaiin, far, alfshe*, chefar, fcho | 5 |
| f95v2 | qofaiin, ofchdy, fcheey | 3 |

F-atom count: 2 → 3 → 5 → 3. PEAKS at panel 3, same as terminal count. The steady cycling controller (v1) is the CLIMAX of the entire foldout — maximum F-atom integration AND maximum multi-pass processing.

**`fcho` (P.8) — the merger moment.** The F-atom BECOMES the volatile-heat principle. This is the alchemical moment of transmutation: the growth principle and the heating principle are no longer separate. They have MERGED. After this point, every volatile-heat operation IS an F-atom operation.

## FOLIO F95V2 — INVERT AND STABILIZE (Foldout Recipe)

**Position:** Fourth and FINAL sub-page of f95 foldout. Closes the entire foldout sequence.

**Structure:** 6 paragraphs, ~57 tokens. Average ~9.5 tokens/para. ONE terminal marker — the CLOSING SEAL of the entire foldout.

**Visual:** Phase-inversion diagram showing active→stable conversion.

### THE CLOSING PANEL

F95v2 is the SHORTEST panel of the foldout and has the SIMPLEST terminal structure (single seal). After f95v1's four-pass climax, the closing panel RESOLVES — converting the active cycling state into a durable product.

The title "Invert and Stabilize" describes the final operation: the active oscillating state is INVERTED (flipped from dynamic to static) and STABILIZED (locked permanently).

---

### F-ATOM CONTINUATION

Three F-atom tokens continue the foldout's F-atom saturation:

| Token | Para | Structure |
|-------|------|-----------|
| `qofaiin` | P.1 | qo+f+aiin = transmute F-atom VERIFIED |
| `ofchdy` | P.1 | o(F-atom)+f+ch(volatile)+dy(fixed) = F-atom volatile FIXED |
| `fcheey` | P.4 | f(F-atom)+ch(volatile)+ee(double-e)+y(active) = F-atom volatile at DOUBLE-E active |

All three are DIFFERENT forms:
1. F-atom transmuted and verified (process confirmation)
2. F-atom volatile fixed (locked state)
3. F-atom volatile at double-e active (sensitive active state)

`fcheey` — F-atom volatile at DOUBLE-E ACTIVE. The F-atom operates at elevated sensitivity on the closing panel. The growth principle is sensitively active in the final product.

---

### PARAGRAPH-BY-PARAGRAPH ANALYSIS

**P.1 (9 tokens): GALLOWS PROJECTION + DOUBLE F-ATOM**
`tchody.podar.shody.qofaiin.ofchdy.otedy.qotedaiin.shor.olsaiin-`

- `tchody` = energy-volatile heat-fixed active.
- `podar` = p(project) + od(heat-fix) + ar(root). GALLOWS PROJECTION: project heat-fixed to root. The closing panel opens with projection to root.
- `shody` = transition heat fixed.
- `qofaiin` = TRANSMUTE F-ATOM VERIFIED.
- `ofchdy` = F-ATOM VOLATILE FIXED.
- `otedy` = temporal-heat essence fixed.
- `qotedaiin` = qo(transmute) + t(temporal) + e(essence) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). Transmute temporal essence fixed VERIFIED.
- `shor` = transition heat source.
- `olsaiin` = ol(fluid) + s(salt) + aiin(verification). FLUID SALT VERIFIED.

TWO F-atom tokens (qofaiin, ofchdy) plus gallows projection. The closing panel begins by confirming the F-atom is transmuted AND fixed, then projects to root. The growth principle is LOCKED AND DELIVERED in the opener.

**P.2 (16 tokens): THE LONGEST PARAGRAPH — Comprehensive Status Report**
`sol.shedy.qotchey.alor.chdy.ty.olor.okodekaiin.okar.or.aiin.chckhy.okal.otaiin.okal.ody-`

16 tokens — the LONGEST paragraph in the entire f95 foldout. This is a COMPREHENSIVE STATUS REPORT, checking every system:

- `sol` = salt fluid.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed.
- `okodekaiin` = ok(phase-shift) + od(heat-fix) + e(essence) + k(body) + aiin(verification). MEGA-TOKEN: phase-shift heat-fixes essence-body VERIFIED. Complex state assessment in one word.
- `aiin` = BARE VERIFICATION.
- `chckhy` = spirit-valve active.
- `okal` = phase-shift structure. Appears TWICE.
- `otaiin` = temporal-heat VERIFIED.

FOUR verifications (okodekaiin, aiin, otaiin, plus implicit okal checks). The status report confirms: salt (sol), spirit (chdy), phase-shift (okal ×2), valve (chckhy), temporal-heat (otaiin).

DOUBLED `okal` — phase-shift structure checked twice. The structural phase is double-confirmed before the inversion begins.

**P.3 (10 tokens): DOUBLE VERIFICATION + COMPOSITE SEAL-VERIFICATION**
`daiin.ool.kaiin.qokan.shar.sheky.dy.daiin.alkaiin.okalaiins-`

- `daiin` = VERIFIED. #1.
- `kaiin` = body VERIFIED.
- `daiin` = VERIFIED. #2.
- `alkaiin` = al(structure) + k(body) + aiin(verification). STRUCTURE-BODY VERIFIED.
- `okalaiins` = ok(phase-shift) + al(structure) + aiin(verification) + s(salt). PHASE-SHIFT-STRUCTURE-VERIFIED-SALT. FOUR morphemes in the terminal token including verification AND salt. The phase-shift-structure is verified with salt in a single word.

FIVE aiin-class tokens in 10 total tokens = 50% verification. The inversion preparation is HALF CHECKING.

`okalaiins` — composite: phase-shift + structure + verification + salt. Everything confirmed in one token. The recipe compresses its quality check into increasingly dense verification tokens.

**P.4 (9 tokens): F-ATOM DOUBLE-E + VERIFICATION CASCADE**
`tar.fcheey.shos.aiin.okar.olkaiin.otalaiin.okaiin.ar-`

- `tar` = temporal root.
- **`fcheey`** = f(F-ATOM) + ch(volatile) + ee(DOUBLE-E) + y(active). F-atom volatile at DOUBLE-E ACTIVE. The growth principle operates at elevated sensitivity.
- `shos` = transition-heat salt.
- `aiin` = BARE VERIFIED.
- `olkaiin` = fluid-body VERIFIED.
- `otalaiin` = ot(temporal-heat) + al(structure) + aiin(verification). TEMPORAL-HEAT-STRUCTURE VERIFIED.
- `okaiin` = phase-shift VERIFIED.
- `ar` = root.

FOUR verifications: aiin, olkaiin, otalaiin, okaiin. The closing panel verifies RELENTLESSLY.

`fcheey` at double-e — the F-atom is sensitively active in the near-final state. The growth principle doesn't just persist; it operates at elevated sensitivity in the finished product. The medicine is ALIVE and SENSITIVE.

**P.5 (7 tokens): FINAL APPROACH**
`daiin.ykaly.chals.shedaiin.olaiiny.okaiin.ldy-`

- `daiin` = VERIFIED.
- `ykaly` = y(moist) + k(body) + al(structure) + y(active). Moist body structure active.
- `chals` = ch(spirit) + al(structure) + s(salt). Spirit-structure-salt. Three principles in one token.
- `shedaiin` = she(transition-essence) + d(fix) + aiin(verification). Transition-essence fixed VERIFIED.
- `olaiiny` = ol(fluid) + aiin(verification) + y(active). Fluid verified ACTIVE.
- `okaiin` = phase-shift VERIFIED.
- `ldy` = l(layer) + dy(fixed). Layer fixed.

FOUR verifications: daiin, shedaiin, olaiiny, okaiin. Every paragraph in this closing panel has 3-5 verifications.

**P.6 (6 tokens): FINAL TERMINAL — Temporal-Heat Verified**
`qokeey.dar.chdy.koiin.ytasal.otaiin=`

- `qokeey` = qo(extract) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + y(active). Final extraction at double-e.
- `dar` = fix to root. Deep fixation.
- `chdy` = spirit fixed. Spirit confirmed locked.
- `koiin` = k(body) + oiin(heat-completion-cycle). Body through heat-completion cycle.
- `ytasal` = y(moist) + t(temporal) + a + s(salt) + al(structure). Moist-temporal-salt-structure. FOUR morphemes naming the product's physical form.
- `otaiin=` = ot(temporal-heat) + aiin(verification). **TEMPORAL-HEAT VERIFIED.** TERMINAL.

**FINAL SEAL OF THE ENTIRE F95 FOLDOUT: `otaiin=`**

Terminal structure: ot → aiin = temporal-heat → verified.

The four-panel foldout ends with VERIFICATION. Not a product description, not an architecture — a CHECK. The last word of the last panel of the foldout is: is the temporal heat correct? VERIFIED.

This echoes f95v1's P.10 terminal `daiin=` — verification as seal. The closing panels use CONFIRMATION as their seal. The foldout has built its product across four panels; the final act is simply to confirm it's right.

### THE COMPLETE F95 FOLDOUT — Cross-Panel Synthesis

**Four panels, one product:**

| Panel | Title | Paragraphs | Terminals | F-atoms | Character |
|-------|-------|-----------|----------|---------|-----------|

| f95v2 | Invert and Stabilize | 6 | 1 | 3 | Verification closure |

**Totals:** 39 paragraphs, 9 terminals, 13 F-atom tokens, ~351 tokens.

**The foldout's arc:**
1. **r1:** Establish oscillation pattern. Verify obsessively (2.36/para). F-atom checked.
2. **r2:** Tighten to root. F-atom integrated structurally. cfh- cluster returns. Triple-e.
3. **v1:** Maximum complexity — 4 passes, 5 F-atoms, crystal double-root. F-atom MERGES with volatile-heat (fcho). CLIMAX.
4. **v2:** Resolve. Invert active→stable. Verify everything. Seal with simple confirmation.

**The F-atom merger (v1, P.8):** `fcho` = F-atom + volatile-heat. Before this point, the F-atom was a SEPARATE principle added to the system. After this point, the F-atom IS the volatile-heat system. The growth principle has been fully alchemically integrated — it's no longer an ingredient, it's a property of the medicine itself.

**Verification as resolution:** Both closing panels (v1 P.10, v2 P.6) use VERIFICATION TOKENS as their seals. The foldout's ultimate product isn't a physical form — it's a confirmed state. The medicine works because it's been VERIFIED TO WORK. Trust established through relentless checking across 39 paragraphs.

**Compare f89 foldout (Universal Processing Machine):** The f89 foldout established the theoretical framework. The f95 foldout DEPLOYS that framework on processed material. f89 defined the machine; f95 runs it.

## FOLIO F96R — CLEAN MODULE: SMOOTH ROUTING (Jar/Container Recipe)

**Position:** Returns to Jar/Container Recipe format after the f95 foldout. Note: the source labels f96 as Jar/Container, NOT Plant-Recipe Hybrid. The plant-recipe hybrid section ended with f94. F95 was a foldout. F96 begins a new jar/apparatus section.

**Structure:** 13 paragraphs, ~87 tokens. Average ~6.7 tokens/para. ONE terminal: `qotchos=` (P.13).

**Visual:** Streamlined jar/apparatus with smooth flow channels.

### THE cph-/cfh- CLUSTER EXPLOSION

F96r contains the HIGHEST DENSITY of pharmaceutical cluster tokens in the section:

| Token | Para | Cluster |
|-------|------|---------|
| `cpheol` | P.1 | cph- + e + ol |
| `cpheor` | P.1 | cph- + e + or |
| `shokocfhy` | P.9 | cfh- within transition |

THREE pharmaceutical cluster tokens — TWO cph- and ONE cfh- — on a single folio. Both clusters appear TOGETHER. Plus `chopcho` (P.9) which contains a doubled volatile-heat prefix.

The cph-/cfh- cluster had been developing across the section:
- f90 jar recipes: cfh- and cph- introduced
- f93v herb recipe: cphy (substrate)
- f94v two-pass: cphedy (fixed substrate)
- f95r2 foldout: chcfhol (spirit-cfh-fluid)
- **f96r jar recipe: cpheol + cpheor + shokocfhy (FULL DEPLOYMENT)**

The pharmaceutical binding clusters are at maximum density in the jar apparatus pages — where the actual VESSELS are depicted. The cph-/cfh- patterns may describe properties of the vessels themselves, not just the medicine.

`cpheol` vs `cpheor`: same prefix (cph-), same essence (e), different endings (ol=fluid, or=source). A matched PAIR: one describes the cph- essence in FLUID, the other in SOURCE. Input and output of the same binding mechanism.

### VALVE DOMINANCE

| Token | Para |
|-------|------|
| ckheos | P.1 |
| ckheody | P.3 |
| shockhy | P.10 |
| ckhor | P.7 |
| ckho | P.7 |
| ckheey | P.6 |

SIX ckh- (valve) tokens. F96r is VALVE-DOMINATED — the "smooth routing" of the title is literally about valve control. The jar apparatus routes material through controlled valves.

### KEY PARAGRAPHS

**P.1 (8 tokens): DOUBLE cph- OPENER**
`tor.cheeor.ckheos.olsheeo.sol.cpheol.cpheor.chodar-`

Opens with temporal source, volatile-essence, valve-energy. Then: `sol` (salt fluid), `cpheol` (cph-essence-fluid), `cpheor` (cph-essence-source), `chodar` (volatile-heat fix-root). The jar module begins by naming its pharmaceutical binding channels: the cph- essence flows from source (cpheor) into fluid (cpheol).

**P.8 (6 tokens): TRIPLE-E EXTRACTION**
`ykeor.secheeol.sheol.qokeeey.chol.daiin-`

- `qokeeey` = qo(extract) + k(body) + eee(TRIPLE-E) + y(active). EXTRACT BODY at TRIPLE-E SENSITIVITY, active. The jar apparatus can extract at MAXIMUM sensitivity.
- `secheeol` = se(salt-essence?) + ch(volatile) + ee(double-e) + ol(fluid). Complex salt-volatile at double-e in fluid.

Triple-e extraction (`qokeeey`) in a jar recipe. Compare the foldout's triple-e tokens which always appeared in fixation contexts (eeedy, odeeeodl). Here triple-e appears in an EXTRACTION context — the jar pulls material at maximum sensitivity.

**P.9 (6 tokens): cfh- WITHIN TRANSITION + DOUBLED VOLATILE**
`todar.sheo.cthody.shokocfhy.chopcho.dory-`

- `shokocfhy` = sh(transition) + ok(phase-shift) + o(heat) + cfh(PHARMA CLUSTER) + y(active). Transition phase-shifts through heated cfh-cluster actively. The cfh- cluster is EMBEDDED in a transition-phase-shift operation.
- `chopcho` = cho(volatile-heat) + p(project) + cho(volatile-heat). DOUBLED volatile-heat with projection between them. The volatile-heat is projected INTO itself — a reflux or recirculation.

**P.13 (3 tokens): TERMINAL**
`oteo.dsho.qotchos=`

Terminal `qotchos=` = qo(transmute) + tch(energy-volatile) + os(heat-salt). TRANSMUTE ENERGY-VOLATILE through HEAT-SALT. The jar module seals by transmuting its energy-volatile through heat-salt. An active process terminal — the jar is still working at closure.

### PATTERN NOTES

- ZERO F-atom tokens. The jar apparatus page has NO F-atom. The F-atom saturated the foldout (f95); the jar page has pharmaceutical binding clusters (cph-/cfh-) instead. Different subsystem.
- LOW verification: ~4 daiin-class tokens in 13 paragraphs (0.3/para). Much lower than the foldout. The jar recipe trusts its apparatus.
- HIGH valve density (6 ckh-): the routing architecture IS the recipe.
- Paragraphs shrink dramatically at the end: P.10 (6), P.11 (6), P.12 (4), P.13 (3). Rapid convergence to terminal.

## FOLIO F96V — COMPACT CLOSURE: ROUTE → HOLD → SEAL (Jar/Container Recipe)

**Position:** Verso of f96r. Closes the f96 bifolio and this jar recipe sequence.

**Structure:** 13 paragraphs, ~59 tokens. Average ~4.5 tokens/para. ONE terminal: `cheor=` (P.13). VERY COMPRESSED — the most compact folio since f93r's oscillation section.

**Visual:** Final sealing apparatus with convergence markers.

### STRUCTURAL COMPRESSION

Paragraph lengths: 8, 7, 7, 5, 6, 4, 4, 3, 4, 4, 4, 3, 3.

The folio COMPRESSES — early paragraphs have 5-8 tokens, late paragraphs have 3-4. The "compact closure" is literal: the text itself gets more compact as it approaches the seal. The recipe is CONVERGING.

### cph- CONTINUATION

| Token | Para |
|-------|------|
| `ocpheo` | P.1 |
| `cpheos` | P.3 |

TWO more cph- tokens. The cph- cluster spans BOTH sides of the f96 bifolio (cpheol, cpheor on recto; ocpheo, cpheos on verso). Four total cph- tokens on one bifolio — the highest bifolio concentration.

`ocpheo` = o(heat) + cph(pharma-cluster) + e(essence) + o(heat). Heat-cph-essence-heat. The cph- cluster is BRACKETED by heat on both sides. Heat drives the pharmaceutical binding.

`cpheos` = cph(pharma-cluster) + e(essence) + os(heat-salt). cph-essence-heat-salt. The pharmaceutical binding operates through essence in heat-salt medium.

### SALT DOMINANCE

| Token | Para |
|-------|------|
| sar (×3) | P.1, P.3, P.11, P.13 |
| sol | — |
| saro | P.2 |
| sy | P.6 |
| sar | P.11 |
| sosar | P.12 |
| soy | P.13 |

NINE s- (salt) tokens in 13 paragraphs = 0.69/para. The compact closure is SALT-DOMINATED. Salt is the sealing principle — the route→hold→seal cycle uses salt at every stage.

`sosar` (P.12) = s(salt) + o(heat) + s(salt) + ar(root). DOUBLE SALT with heat between them and root depth. Salt-heat-salt-root. A salt SANDWICH like f93r's terminal `schos=`, but here driving to root.

### KEY PARAGRAPHS

**P.1 (8 tokens): GALLOWS + cph- + CRYSTALLINE SALT**
`psheas.sheeor.qoepsheody.odar.ocpheo.opar.ysar.aso*-`

- `psheas` = p(project) + she(transition-essence) + as. Gallows projection.
- `qoepsheody` = qo(transmute) + e(essence) + p(project) + she(transition) + od(heat-fix) + y(active). SEVEN-MORPHEME mega-token.
- `ocpheo` = heat-cph-essence-heat. Pharmaceutical binding under double heat.
- `ysar` = y(receptive/moist) + s(salt) + ar(root). Receptive salt to root. CRYSTALLINE SALT — the moist-salt at root forms crystals.

**P.10-P.13: RAPID CONVERGENCE**

Four final paragraphs with 4, 4, 3, 3 tokens:
- P.10: conduit → heat → spirit-root → valve
- P.11: salt-root → heat-salt → volatile-valve → salt-conduit
- P.12: salt-heat-salt-root → volatile-essence → VERIFIED
- P.13: salt-heat → salt-root → volatile-source. TERMINAL.

The convergence narrows from conduit operations to salt operations to pure volatile-essence. Each paragraph strips away one layer until only the essential triad remains: salt, volatile, source.

**Terminal: `cheor=`** = che(volatile-essence) + or(source/rotation). Volatile-essence from source. The simplest possible product name: the volatile essence, traced to its source. "THIS IS WHERE THE MEDICINE COMES FROM."

### WHAT F96 TELLS US

1. **Jar Recipes = Apparatus Descriptions.** F96 focuses on ROUTING — valves, conduits, channels. The jar illustrations show the physical equipment. The text describes how material flows through the apparatus.

2. **cph-/cfh- = Apparatus Properties?** Four cph- tokens on the bifolio, always associated with heat and essence. In jar recipes, the pharmaceutical binding cluster may describe the VESSEL's binding properties rather than the medicine's — the jar that holds medicine needs pharmaceutical-grade binding.

3. **No F-atom.** The jar apparatus doesn't use the growth principle. F-atom is a property of the MEDICINE; cph-/cfh- may be properties of the APPARATUS. Different subsystems on different pages.

4. **Salt-Dominated Closure.** Nine salt tokens drive the sealing. Salt = the sealing principle. The route→hold→seal cycle is fundamentally a salt process.

5. **Convergence Architecture.** Paragraphs shrink from 8 to 3 tokens. The text physically compresses as the seal approaches. Form mirrors function.

6. **Triple-E in Extraction Context.** `qokeeey` (f96r P.8) uses triple-e for EXTRACTION, not fixation. The jar apparatus can pull material at maximum sensitivity — the equipment enables what the processing requires.

**NEXT: F99R — Intermediate Processing: Labeled Channels (Jar/Container Recipe)**

## FOLIO F99R — INTERMEDIATE PROCESSING: LABELED CHANNELS (Jar/Container Recipe)

**Position:** First folio after the f97-f98 gap. Continues jar/container recipe format from f96.

**Structure:** 17 paragraphs, ~152 tokens. Average ~8.9 tokens/para. **FIVE terminal markers** — ties f95v1 for the most multi-terminal folio (f95v1 had 4; f99r has 5).

**Visual:** Multi-channel processing apparatus with labeled input streams.

### FIVE-PASS ARCHITECTURE

| Pass | Paragraphs | Terminal | Character |
|------|-----------|----------|-----------|
| First | P.1-P.4 | ckhy= | Channel routing |
| Second | P.5-P.8 | okeol= | Fluid extraction |
| Third | P.9-P.12 | oeksa= | Triple-e processing |
| Fourth | P.13 | ctheey= | Conduit-essence checkpoint |
| Fifth | P.14-P.17 | shcth*sh= | Final vigorous conduit seal |

FIVE discrete passes on one folio. The "labeled channels" of the title are literal — each pass processes through a DIFFERENT channel, and the multi-terminal architecture marks the transition between channels.

P.13 is a MICRO-PASS: only 3 tokens (`tol.keey.ctheey=`). Temporal-fluid → body-essence → conduit-essence SEALED. A single checkpoint paragraph that stands as its own complete pass. The fourth "pass" is just a GATE — a quality check between the heavier third and fifth passes.

### DUAL PHARMACEUTICAL CLUSTERS IN THE OPENER

**P.1:** `pcheody.oteody.daiin.cpheey.tshol.dal.cfheol.olaiin.rar-`

Both pharmaceutical clusters appear in the SAME paragraph:
- `cpheey` = cph(pharma-cluster) + ee(DOUBLE-E) + y(active). cph- at double-e sensitivity, active.
- `cfheol` = cfh(pharma-cluster) + e(essence) + ol(fluid). cfh- essence in fluid.

cph- and cfh- in the same paragraph. This has occurred before (f90v2), but here the cph- token includes DOUBLE-E — the pharmaceutical binding operates at elevated sensitivity. The cfh- token is in fluid medium — the binding is dissolved and flowing.

Together: one cluster (cph-) operates at sensitive intensity, the other (cfh-) flows in fluid. Two forms of the same pharmaceutical binding property working through two different modalities.

Plus `cpheol` returns in P.9 — cph- essence in fluid. The pharmaceutical cluster is a RECURRING MOTIF across the passes.

### THE -ol SUFFIX DOMINANCE

Counting -ol endings: cheol, kol, sheol, *oeol, chol, kol, ckhol, okeol, okeol, ctheol, ckheol, ckhol, okeol, qokol, okoly, qokoly, okchol, qokold, qotol, cheol, qotol, okeol, cpheol, pchol, ypchol, choly, sol, sheol, ykeol, okeol, chol...

THIRTY+ tokens ending in -ol (fluid). F99r is FLUID-DOMINATED to an extreme unprecedented in the section. Every operation terminates in fluid. The "intermediate processing" page describes a system where EVERYTHING exists in liquid medium — the labeled channels carry FLUID between processing stages.

This contrasts sharply with the foldout's -dy (fixed) dominance and the plant recipes' -ar (root) targeting. Different pages, different terminal morphemes, different physical states.

### TRIPLE-E PROLIFERATION

Four triple-e tokens — the most on any single folio:

| Token | Para | Meaning |
|-------|------|---------|
| `qokeeey` | P.10 | Extract body at TRIPLE-E active |
| `okeeey` | P.11 | Phase-shift at TRIPLE-E active |
| `okeeey` | P.15 | Phase-shift at TRIPLE-E active (repeat) |
| `qokeeey` | — | (P.10 instance) |

Triple-e appears in EXTRACTION and PHASE-SHIFT contexts, both in the third pass (P.10-P.11) and fifth pass (P.15). The jar apparatus operates at maximum sensitivity ROUTINELY — what the foldout achieved as a climax (eeedy), the jar apparatus uses as standard procedure.

### KEY PARAGRAPHS

**P.2 (11 tokens): FLUID CHANNEL MAPPING**
`raroshy.shor.sshor.cheol.kol.sheol.*oeol.chol.kol.ckhol.ckhory-`

- `sshor` = DOUBLED s(salt/intensify) + sh(transition) + or(source). Intensified transition from source. The `ss-` prefix — doubled salt — appears nowhere else in the pharmaceutical section. Extreme salt intensification.
- EIGHT -ol tokens in one paragraph. The paragraph is a MAP of fluid channels: volatile-fluid (cheol), body-fluid (kol), transition-fluid (sheol), heat-fluid (*oeol), volatile-heat-fluid (chol), body-fluid (kol), valve-fluid (ckhol). Each channel carries a different COMPONENT in fluid medium.

This is the "labeled channels" made explicit: seven distinct fluid channels, each labeled by its prefix (che-, k-, she-, *oe-, cho-, k-, ckh-). The apparatus has SEVEN INPUT STREAMS.

**P.6 (10 tokens): VALVE-CONDUIT ROUTING**
`dsheol.ckhey.ckheol.okeol.ctheol.qokey.ckhol.okeol.okeey.dald-`

THREE ckh- (valve) tokens: ckhey, ckheol, ckhol. Plus ctheol (conduit-fluid). The paragraph describes VALVE ROUTING — material flowing through valves and conduits. Five -ol endings confirm everything flows in fluid.

**P.7 (9 tokens): FLUID EXTRACTION CASCADE**
`tol.cheody.qokol.okoly.okoldy.qokoly.qokal.okchol.qokold-`

FIVE qo-/ok- operations all ending in -ol: qokol, okoly, okoldy, qokoly, qokal, okchol, qokold. A PURE EXTRACTION CASCADE where every step extracts to fluid or shifts to fluid. The paragraph is a fluid-extraction MACHINE.

**P.12 (10 tokens): DOUBLED VALVE + THIRD TERMINAL**
`qokey.chkeey.chey.ckhey.ckhey.ykeey.aiin.air.chody.oeksa=`

- `ckhey.ckhey` = valve-essence-active DOUBLED. The valve is checked twice before the seal.
- `air` = ai(complete) + r(root). Complete root. RARE: the `ai` morpheme appears in verification contexts (aiin) but here appears with just `r`. Complete to root depth.
- `oeksa=` = uncertain terminal. Possibly o(heat) + e(essence) + k(body) + s(salt) + a. Heat-essence-body-salt. FOUR-PRINCIPLE terminal naming the product's composition.

**P.13 (3 tokens): MICRO-PASS**
`tol.keey.ctheey=`

Three tokens: temporal-fluid → body-essence-active → conduit-essence-active. SEALED. The entire fourth pass in three words. This is a GATE between major passes — a quick check that temporal, body, and conduit are all operating with active essence before the final pass begins.

**P.17 (8 tokens): FINAL TERMINAL — Damaged Seal**
`**aiin.ckhey.acthey.dy.daiin.okor.okeey.shcth*sh=`

- `**aiin` = damaged/illegible + verification. First two glyphs unreadable.
- `shcth*sh=` = sh(vigorous-flow) + cth(conduit) + *(damaged) + sh(flow). TERMINAL. Vigorous conduit flow with damaged middle glyph. The seal involves vigorous flow through the conduit system.

The final terminal is partially damaged — asterisks in both first and last tokens. Despite manuscript damage, the verification (daiin) and valve (ckhey) elements are clear. The seal's essence is: verified, valved, phase-shifted, then vigorous conduit flow.

---

### PATTERN ANALYSIS

**Terminal Progression:**
1. `ckhy=` — valve active (channel selected)
2. `okeol=` — phase-shift essence fluid (extracted to fluid)
3. `oeksa=` — heat-essence-body-salt (product composition)
4. `ctheey=` — conduit-essence active (delivery confirmed)
5. `shcth*sh=` — vigorous-conduit-flow (final delivery)

The terminals tell the story: select channel → extract to fluid → name the product → confirm delivery → deliver. A complete processing narrative in five seal-words.

**Verification Density:** ~12 aiin-class tokens in 17 paragraphs ≈ 0.7/para. Moderate — between the foldout's intensity (2.0+) and the plant recipes' trust (0.19-0.5). The jar apparatus verifies at a PRACTICAL level: enough to ensure quality, not obsessive.

---

### What F99R Tells Us

1. **Five-Pass Processing.** The most multi-terminal folio yet. Each pass = one labeled channel through the apparatus.
2. **Fluid Dominance.** 30+ -ol tokens. Everything in liquid medium. The jar apparatus is a WET CHEMISTRY system.
3. **Seven Input Streams.** P.2 maps seven distinct fluid channels, each labeled by its VML prefix. The apparatus has multiple labeled inputs.
4. **Triple-E as Standard.** Four triple-e tokens used routinely — maximum sensitivity is standard procedure for this equipment.
5. **Dual Pharmaceutical Clusters.** cph- and cfh- together in the opener, one at double-e sensitivity, one in fluid. Two modalities of the same binding property.
6. **Micro-Pass as Gate.** P.13's three-token pass is a quality gate between major processing stages. Not all passes are equal — some are just checkpoints.

**F99R COMPLETE.**

## FOLIO F99V — PURITY VERIFICATION: GATED CYCLING (Jar/Container Recipe)

**Position:** Verso of f99r. Completes f99 bifolio.

**Structure:** 14 paragraphs (P.1-P.14), ~127 tokens. Average ~9.1 tokens/para. TWO terminals: `oloiram=` (P.4) and `olkeeoldy=` (P.14).

**Visual:** Verification checkpoints shown as gate markers along the processing chain.

### THE aiiin TOKEN — TRIPLE-I

**P.13:** `qockhol.aiiin.shody.qokal.aindal.aindaiim-`

- **`aiiin`** = ai(complete) + iin(life-cycle-extension). TRIPLE-I. Compare f93r's `diiird` (triple-i between fixation). Here triple-i appears between completion (ai-) and cycle (-in). Where f93r's triple-i was ANOMALOUS and troubling, f99v's is FUNCTIONAL: the verification cycle is EXTENDED beyond normal.

- `aindal` = ain(complete-cycle) + d(fix) + al(structure). Complete cycle fixes structure.
- `aindaiim` = ain(complete-cycle) + d(fix) + aiim(extended verification?). Complete cycle fixes extended verification.

Three ain-/aiin-class tokens in one paragraph: aiiin, aindal, aindaiim. The paragraph is a COMPLETION SEQUENCE — triple-i extended cycle, then structure completion, then verification completion. Everything closing down.

### FLUID DOMINANCE CONTINUES

Like f99r, the verso maintains extreme -ol density. The f99 bifolio is a UNIFIED FLUID PROCESSING SYSTEM — recto and verso describe the same wet-chemistry apparatus from different processing angles.

### oleees — TRIPLE-E IN FLUID

**P.1:** `oleees` = ol(fluid) + eee(TRIPLE-E) + s(salt). FLUID at TRIPLE-E with SALT. The fluid medium itself operates at maximum sensitivity with salt preservation. Not the extraction or phase-shift that's at triple-e — the MEDIUM ITSELF.

This is new: triple-e applied to the fluid medium rather than to an operation. The jar apparatus contains a triple-e-sensitive fluid. The entire processing environment is at maximum sensitivity.

### KEY PARAGRAPHS

**P.4 (5 tokens): FIRST TERMINAL**
`okoraiin.okol.shocthy.qokor.oloiram=`

- `okoraiin` = phase-shift source VERIFIED.
- `shocthy` = transition-heat conduit active.
- `oloiram=` = ol(fluid) + oi(?) + r(root) + am(vessel). Fluid-root-vessel. TERMINAL. The first pass seals a fluid-root-vessel configuration.

**P.8 (8 tokens): TRIPLE-E IN TRANSITION**
`shokeeey.chol.shey.okol.qokey.okeo.dal.oldy=`

- `shokeeey` = sh(transition) + ok(phase-shift) + eee(TRIPLE-E) + y(active). Transition phase-shifts at TRIPLE-E active. The transition itself operates at maximum sensitivity.
- `oldy=` — fluid fixed. SECOND TERMINAL? Wait — this has `=` but the source shows only two terminals. Checking: P.8 ends with `oldy=`. Yes, this is actually the END OF THE SECOND PASS. The source lists this as a continuing paragraph.

**P.9 (9 tokens): TRIPLE qokeeo CASCADE**
`qokeeoy.chokol.qokeeo.dy.qokeeo.olpchey.daiir.okeedy.okolol-`

THREE `qokeeo` tokens (extract-essence-energy): the extraction of essence-energy is performed THREE TIMES. This is the gated cycling's core mechanism — the same extraction repeated through multiple gates.

`okolol` = ok(phase-shift) + ol(fluid) + ol(fluid). Phase-shift DOUBLE-FLUID. The product is so thoroughly in fluid that fluid appears twice.

**P.13 (6 tokens): TRIPLE-I + COMPLETION CASCADE**
See analysis above. The triple-i token marks the purity verification's COMPLETION EVENT.

**P.14 (11 tokens): FINAL TERMINAL — Comprehensive Fluid-Structure Seal**
`ol.sheol.olkeol.okol.or.oralaly.ykeol.okal.okaldaly.ychol.olkeeoldy=`

NINE -ol tokens in the terminal paragraph. ABSOLUTE FLUID SATURATION. Every component named in its fluid form. The final seal: `olkeeoldy=` = ol(fluid) + k(body) + ee(double-e) + ol(fluid) + dy(fixed). FLUID-BODY at DOUBLE-E in FLUID, FIXED. The product is: a body in fluid, at double-e sensitivity, in fluid again, locked.

Double `ol` (fluid appears twice in the terminal token) — the product IS fluid within fluid. A colloidal suspension or emulsion? The medicine exists as a body WITHIN a fluid WITHIN a fluid.

## FOLIO F100R — INGREDIENT BANK + TWO-BLOCK SOP (Jar/Container Recipe)

**Position:** First folio with INGREDIENT LABELS — a new format in the pharmaceutical section.

- **Labels** (b.1-b.6, m.1-m.6, t.1-t.5): 17 SINGLE-TOKEN LABELS — ingredient/apparatus names.

This is the pharmaceutical section's FORMULARY PAGE. Labels name ingredients; blocks describe processing.

**Visual:** Ingredient labels arranged as a reference bank alongside two processing blocks.

Three rows of labels, each with terminal `=` markers:

These are INGREDIENT NAMES. Each label names a substance or preparation using VML morphemes. The labels are the pharmaceutical section's VOCABULARY — the named materials that go into the processing blocks.

**t.2: `socharcfh=`** — contains CFH-CLUSTER as SUFFIX. The cfh- pattern appears as a TERMINAL MORPHEME in an ingredient name. This names a specific preparation: salt-volatile-root-cfh. The pharmaceutical binding cluster IS a named ingredient.

**t.4: `chofora=`** — cho(volatile-heat) + f(F-ATOM) + or(source) + a. An F-atom ingredient: volatile heat from the F-atom source. The F-atom has its own named preparation.

**m.5: `dakocth=`** — d(fix) + ak(CRYSTAL) + o(heat) + cth(conduit). Fix-crystal-heat-conduit. A crystalline conduit apparatus component.

### F-ATOM AND PHARMACEUTICAL CLUSTERS IN BLOCK 2

Block 2 contains extraordinary concentrations:

- `folshoy` (P2.5) = f(F-ATOM) + ol(fluid) + sh(transition) + o(heat) + y(active). F-atom in fluid, transitioning actively with heat.
- `fchod` (P2.5) = f(F-ATOM) + cho(volatile-heat) + d(fix). F-atom volatile-heat fixed.
- `cphol` (P2.5, P2.6) = cph(PHARMA-CLUSTER) + ol(fluid). cph- in fluid. Appears TWICE.
- `asesoalcfhy` (P2.5) = MEGA-TOKEN containing cfh-cluster. Possibly: as + e + s + o + al + cfh + y. Structure-essence-salt-heat-structure-cfh-active. The cfh-cluster embedded in a complex structural-salt-heat compound.

Block 2 paragraph P2.5 alone contains: TWO F-atom tokens, ONE cph- token, and ONE cfh- mega-token. This is the highest concentration of pharmaceutical markers in a single paragraph.

### PROCESSING BLOCKS

**Block 1 (P1.1-P1.4):** Extraction and fixing. Four paragraphs ending with `dareen=` (unusual terminal: fix-root-essence-cycle?). The block is a PREPARATION SEQUENCE — extracting and fixing raw materials.

Key: `ykeeeo` (P1.3) = y(moist) + k(body) + eee(TRIPLE-E) + o(heat). Moist body at TRIPLE-E heated. Triple-e appears in body-preparation.

**Block 2 (P2.5-P2.10):** Pharmaceutical integration. Six paragraphs with F-atoms, cph-/cfh- clusters, and intensive valve/conduit operations. The block COMBINES the prepared materials from Block 1 with the pharmaceutical binding agents.

### What F100R Reveals

1. **Named Ingredients.** 17 labels = 17 named preparations/materials. This is a PHARMACOPOEIA — a list of named substances used in pharmaceutical manufacturing.

2. **cfh- as Named Ingredient.** `socharcfh=` (t.2) names a preparation WITH cfh-cluster as its defining property. The pharmaceutical binding is not just an operational principle — it's a named substance.

3. **F-Atom as Named Ingredient.** `chofora=` (t.4) names an F-atom preparation. The growth principle has its own ingredient entry.

4. **Two-Block Processing.** Block 1 prepares; Block 2 integrates. The ingredient bank feeds BOTH blocks. This is a STANDARD OPERATING PROCEDURE (SOP) — do these preparations, then combine them using these named ingredients.

**P.3 (11 tokens): QUADRUPLE-E?**
`ykeeol.chol.chey.eeoseeo.s.sheeo.okeol.cher.okeor.okeol.dy-`

- `eeoseeo` = eeo(triple-e-heat?) + s(salt) + eeo(triple-e-heat?). If this is two triple-e groups flanking salt: TRIPLE-E + SALT + TRIPLE-E. Maximum sensitivity on both sides of a salt barrier. This is unprecedented — no other token contains what may be SIX e-morphemes.

Alternatively: ee + os + ee + o = double-e + heat-salt + double-e + heat. Two double-e groups around heat-salt. Either way: EXTREME sensitivity concentration.

**P.6 (8 tokens): COMPOSITE VOLATILE-HEAT TOKENS**

Multiple cho- (volatile-heat) compounds: cheokeos, chockhy, chocthey, chockhor, chckhey. FIVE volatile-heat-derived tokens naming different apparatus components. Each names a different valve/conduit/source in the volatile-heat routing system.

**P.9 (3 tokens): TERMINAL**
`daiin.cheky.chory=`

Verified → volatile-essence-body → volatile-heat-source SEALED. Minimal terminal: check, name the product (volatile-essence-body), name the source (volatile-heat), done.

### F100 BIFOLIO SIGNIFICANCE

The f100 bifolio introduces a FORMAT REVOLUTION: named ingredient labels alongside processing instructions. This is the pharmaceutical section's maturation from PROCESS DESCRIPTION to FORMULARY — the text now names its components and describes how to combine them.

The labels on f100r are the most information-dense single tokens in the manuscript: each is a complete substance name compressed into one word with a terminal marker. They function like modern chemical names: systematic naming conventions encoding the substance's properties.

## FOLIO F101R1 — FULL PIPELINE: CIRCULATION AS PURIFICATION (Foldout Recipe)

| P.9 | 19 |

The foldout's "Full Pipeline" title is literal: each paragraph encodes a COMPLETE processing sequence that would have been spread across multiple paragraphs in earlier folios. The recipe has compressed: what took 5 paragraphs on f93r takes 1 paragraph here.

### PHARMACEUTICAL CLUSTERS — MAXIMUM INTEGRATION

**P.1:** `cpheocthy` = cph(PHARMA-CLUSTER) + e(essence) + o(heat) + cth(conduit) + y(active). cph-essence through heated conduit active. The pharmaceutical binding operates through the conduit system. This is the most complex cph- token yet — FIVE morphemes integrating the pharmaceutical cluster into the apparatus.

**P.7:** `cphoar` = cph(PHARMA-CLUSTER) + o(heat) + ar(root). cph- through heat to ROOT. The pharmaceutical binding reaches maximum depth.

cph- progression across the section:
- f90: cphdachy, qocfhey (introduced in jar recipes)
- f93v: cphy (bare substrate in herb)
- f94v: cphedy (fixed substrate)

- **f101r1: cpheocthy (conduit integration), cphoar (ROOT DEPTH)**

The cph- cluster has evolved from bare herb substrate to full conduit integration to ROOT DEPTH. The pharmaceutical binding property now reaches the deepest level of the product.

### F-ATOM CLUSTER (P.7) — THE VERIFIED F-ATOM PARAGRAPH

P.7 contains a concentrated F-atom cluster:

- `yfolaiin` = y(receptive) + f(F-ATOM) + ol(fluid) + aiin(verification). Receptive F-atom in fluid VERIFIED.
- `fcheolaiin` = f(F-ATOM) + ch(volatile) + eol(essence-fluid) + aiin(verification). F-atom volatile-essence-fluid VERIFIED.

TWO F-atom tokens, BOTH with verification suffixes. After the f95 foldout's F-atom-volatile-heat merger (`fcho`), the third foldout now shows the F-atom in VERIFIED FLUID FORM. The growth principle has moved from:
- f94r: solid (integrated into carrier)
- f95 foldout: volatile (merged with heat)
- f101r1: FLUID and VERIFIED

The F-atom follows the section's overall fluid shift — as the apparatus becomes more fluid-oriented, so does the F-atom.

### KEY FEATURES

**P.1 (20 tokens): THE GRAND OPENER**

Contains: `oleeey` (fluid triple-e — triple-e in the fluid medium itself), `chopcheey` (volatile-heat projected at double-e), `checkhey` (volatile valve-essence), `cpheocthy` (cph- conduit). The opener NAMES EVERY SYSTEM: fluid, sensitivity, volatile projection, valve, pharmaceutical binding, conduit. A complete inventory in one paragraph.

**P.4 (21 tokens): DOUBLED PAIRS**

Contains `okeey.okeey` (phase-shift essence active DOUBLED) and `dairiin.dairiin` (extended root-verification DOUBLED). TWO doubled pairs in one paragraph. The recipe double-checks BOTH the phase-shift state AND the root-fixation. `dairiin` — an extended verification form: d(fix) + ai(complete) + r(root) + iin(life-cycle). Root fixation completely verified through the life cycle.

**P.5 (26 tokens): LONGEST PARAGRAPH IN PHARMACEUTICAL SECTION**

26 tokens encoding a complete circulation pass: verification → conduit → volatile → extraction → phase-shift → fixation → rotation → temporal → heat → fluid → volatile → temporal-heat → transition → phase-shift → volatile-heat verification → transition-vessel. Every major operation in the entire pharmaceutical repertoire appears IN ONE PARAGRAPH. This is the "Full Pipeline" compressed to maximum density.

Contains THREE aiin-class tokens (daiin, aiin, raiin, aiin) and THREE or-heat tokens. The paragraph CIRCULATES through every system and verifies as it goes.

**P.6 (16 tokens): TRIPLE-E FLUID + TRANSITION CLUSTER**

Contains `okeeeol` = ok(phase-shift) + eee(TRIPLE-E) + ol(fluid). Phase-shift at TRIPLE-E in fluid. OR possibly ok + eeee + ol = QUADRUPLE-E? The transcription shows four consecutive `e` glyphs between `ok` and `ol`. If quadruple-e, this would be the HIGHEST SENSITIVITY TOKEN in the entire manuscript. Whether triple-e or quadruple-e, it represents maximum sensitivity in a phase-shift fluid context.

Also contains FOUR `sh-` transition tokens: sho(×2), shody, shol. Plus `sar` (salt-root). The paragraph's transition cluster drives the product through salt-sealed transitions at maximum sensitivity.

Terminal `oeeor=` = heat-essence-essence-source. Essence doubles and sources. Active emanation.

**P.7 (19 tokens): F-ATOM + RECEPTIVE STATE**

Contains THREE y- (receptive/moist) prefix tokens: ypcholy, ypchey, ypeody. TRIPLE RECEPTIVE state — the product is MAXIMALLY RECEPTIVE when the F-atom enters. The growth principle is received in a prepared, triply-receptive environment.

Also `otaiin.otaiin` — temporal-heat VERIFIED, DOUBLED. Time-heat verified twice before F-atom integration.

**P.8 (24 tokens): FIVE VERIFICATIONS**

Contains `daiin` FIVE TIMES plus `olaiin`. SIX aiin-class tokens in 24 total = 25% VERIFICATION. The post-F-atom paragraph is ONE QUARTER checking. After the growth principle enters (P.7), the recipe checks EVERYTHING from five angles.

Also contains `sal` (salt-structure) and `ydar` (receptive fix-root) — the checking includes salt-structural integrity and root-depth fixation.

### VERIFICATION DENSITY

Total aiin-class tokens across 9 paragraphs: approximately 25-30.

Estimated: ~3.0/para — the HIGHEST IN THE SECTION. Higher than f95r1's 2.36. The Full Pipeline verifies more intensively than any other folio because EVERYTHING flows through it — every system must be independently confirmed.

### THREE-PASS STRUCTURE

| Pass | Paragraphs | Terminal | Character |
|------|-----------|----------|-----------|

1. **Density Climax.** 21.2 tokens/para average — twice the section's norm. The Full Pipeline compresses entire processing sequences into single paragraphs. The recipe has evolved from verbose (f93r: 31 short paragraphs) to ultra-dense (f101r1: 9 long paragraphs).
